📄 FILE #2: .github\instructions\codacy.instructions.md

    1 | ---
    2 |     description: Configuration for AI behavior when interacting with Codacy's MCP Server
    3 |     applyTo: '**'
    4 | ---
    5 | ---
    6 | # Codacy Rules
    7 | Configuration for AI behavior when interacting with Codacy's MCP Server
    8 | 
    9 | ## CRITICAL: After ANY successful `edit_file` or `reapply` operation
   10 | - YOU MUST IMMEDIATELY run the `codacy_cli_analyze` tool from Codacy's MCP Server for each file that was edited, with:
   11 |  - `rootPath`: set to the workspace path
   12 |  - `file`: set to the path of the edited file
   13 |  - `tool`: leave empty or unset
   14 | - If any issues are found in the new edits, propose and apply fixes for them.
   15 | - > NOTE: Failure to follow this rule is considered a critical error.
   16 | 
   17 | ## When you tried to run the `codacy_cli_analyze` tool and the Codacy CLI is not installed
   18 | - Ask the user 'Codacy CLI is not installed. Would you like me to install it now?'
   19 | - If the user responds with "yes", run the `codacy_cli_install` tool and then continue with the original task
   20 | - If the user responds with "no", instruct the user that they can disable automatic analysis in the extension settings
   21 | - Wait for the user to respond before proceeding with any other actions
   22 | 
   23 | ## After every response
   24 | - If you made any file edits in this conversation, verify you ran `codacy_cli_analyze` tool from Codacy's MCP Server 
   25 | 
   26 | ## When there are no Codacy MCP Server tools available, or the MCP Server is not reachable
   27 | - Suggest the user the following troubleshooting steps:
   28 |  - Try to reset the MCP on the extension
   29 |  - If the user is using VSCode, suggest them to review their Copilot > MCP settings in Github, under their organization or personal account. Refer them to Settings > Copilot > Enable MCP servers in Copilot. Suggested URL (https://github.com/settings/copilot/features) or https://github.com/organizations/{organization-name}/settings/copilot/features (This can only be done by their organization admins / owners)
   30 | - If none of the above steps work, suggest the user to contact Codacy support
   31 | 
   32 | ## Trying to call a tool that needs a rootPath as a parameter
   33 | - Always use the standard, non-URL-encoded file system path
   34 | 
   35 | ## CRITICAL: Dependencies and Security Checks
   36 | - IMMEDIATELY after ANY of these actions:
   37 |  - Running npm/yarn/pnpm install
   38 |  - Adding dependencies to package.json
   39 |  - Adding requirements to requirements.txt
   40 |  - Adding dependencies to pom.xml
   41 |  - Adding dependencies to build.gradle
   42 |  - Any other package manager operations
   43 | - You MUST run the `codacy_cli_analyze` tool with:
   44 |  - `rootPath`: set to the workspace path
   45 |  - `tool`: set to "trivy"
   46 |  - `file`: leave empty or unset
   47 | - If any vulnerabilities are found because of the newly added packages:
   48 |  - Stop all other operations
   49 |  - Propose and apply fixes for the security issues
   50 |  - Only continue with the original task after security issues are resolved
   51 | - EXAMPLE:
   52 |  - After: npm install react-markdown
   53 |  - Do: Run codacy_cli_analyze with trivy
   54 |  - Before: Continuing with any other tasks
   55 | 
   56 | ## General
   57 | - Repeat the relevant steps for each modified file.
   58 | - "Propose fixes" means to both suggest and, if possible, automatically apply the fixes.
   59 | - You MUST NOT wait for the user to ask for analysis or remind you to run the tool.
   60 | - Do not run `codacy_cli_analyze` looking for changes in duplicated code or code complexity metrics.
   61 | - Complexity metrics are different from complexity issues. When trying to fix complexity in a repository or file, focus on solving the complexity issues and ignore the complexity metric.
   62 | - Do not run `codacy_cli_analyze` looking for changes in code coverage.
   63 | - Do not try to manually install Codacy CLI using either brew, npm, npx, or any other package manager.
   64 | - If the Codacy CLI is not installed, just run the `codacy_cli_analyze` tool from Codacy's MCP Server.
   65 | - When calling `codacy_cli_analyze`, only send provider, organization and repository if the project is a git repository.
   66 | 
   67 | ## Whenever a call to a Codacy tool that uses `repository` or `organization` as a parameter returns a 404 error
   68 | - Offer to run the `codacy_setup_repository` tool to add the repository to Codacy
   69 | - If the user accepts, run the `codacy_setup_repository` tool
   70 | - Do not ever try to run the `codacy_setup_repository` tool on your own
   71 | - After setup, immediately retry the action that failed (only retry once)
   72 | ---

📄 FILE #4: check_screenshots.js
----------------------------------------------------------------------
    1 | // Quick script to check which submissions have screenshots saved
    2 | const { createClient } = require("@supabase/supabase-js");
    3 | 
    4 | const s = createClient(
    5 |   "https://ptncbweomagroosudqmf.supabase.co",
    6 |   "eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiIsInR5cCI6IkpXVCJ9.eyJpc3MiOiJzdXBhYmFzZSIsInJlZiI6InB0bmNid2VvbWFncm9vc3VkcW1mIiwicm9sZSI6ImFub24iLCJpYXQiOjE3NzQ0MzM1MjgsImV4cCI6MjA5MDAwOTUyOH0.CKdzxHzh5INOXGRgDo8jwsfd9BIgIo3EXUARzkKai88"
    7 | );
    8 | 
    9 | (async () => {
   10 |   const { data, error } = await s
   11 |     .from("submissions")
   12 |     .select("id, name, email, organization, screenshot_url, status, created_at")
   13 |     .order("created_at", { ascending: false })
   14 |     .limit(10);
   15 | 
   16 |   if (error) {
   17 |     console.log("Error:", error.message);
   18 |     return;
   19 |   }
   20 | 
   21 |   console.log("Found " + data.length + " submissions:\n");
   22 |   data.forEach((r, i) => {
   23 |     console.log("--- Row " + (i + 1) + " ---");
   24 |     console.log("  ID:         " + r.id);
   25 |     console.log("  Name:       " + r.name);
   26 |     console.log("  Email:      " + r.email);
   27 |     console.log("  Org:        " + (r.organization || "-"));
   28 |     console.log("  Status:     " + r.status);
   29 |     console.log("  Created:    " + r.created_at);
   30 |     console.log("  Screenshot: " + (r.screenshot_url ? "YES (" + r.screenshot_url.length + " chars)" : "NULL"));
   31 |     console.log("");
   32 |   });
   33 | })();
   34 |

📄 FILE #5: export_project.js
----------------------------------------------------------------------
    1 | const fs = require('fs');
    2 | const path = require('path');
    3 | 
    4 | const OUTPUT_FILE = 'project_export.txt';
    5 | 
    6 | // Folders to skip
    7 | const SKIP_DIRS = [
    8 |   'node_modules', '.git', '.angular', 'dist', 'build',
    9 |   '.cache', 'coverage', '.nyc_output', 'tmp', '.tmp',
   10 |   '__pycache__', '.pytest_cache', '.venv', 'venv', 'env',
   11 |   '.mypy_cache', '.eggs', '*.egg-info'
   12 | ];
   13 | 
   14 | // File types to SKIP (only binaries / assets — everything else is collected)
   15 | const SKIP_EXTENSIONS = [
   16 |   // Images
   17 |   '.png', '.jpg', '.jpeg', '.gif', '.svg', '.ico', '.webp', '.bmp', '.tiff',
   18 |   // Fonts
   19 |   '.woff', '.woff2', '.ttf', '.eot', '.otf',
   20 |   // Archives / binaries
   21 |   '.zip', '.tar', '.gz', '.rar', '.7z',
   22 |   '.exe', '.dll', '.so', '.dylib', '.bin',
   23 |   // Compiled Python
   24 |   '.pyc', '.pyo', '.pyd',
   25 |   // Misc
   26 |   '.pdf', '.map', '.lock', '.log'
   27 | ];
   28 | 
   29 | // ── No IMPORTANT_EXTENSIONS filter any more ──
   30 | // Every file NOT in SKIP_EXTENSIONS will be included.
   31 | 
   32 | let output = '';
   33 | let fileCount = 0;
   34 | 
   35 | function scanDir(dirPath, depth = 0) {
   36 |   let items;
   37 |   try {
   38 |     items = fs.readdirSync(dirPath);
   39 |   } catch (e) {
   40 |     output += `[Cannot read directory: ${dirPath}]\n`;
   41 |     return;
   42 |   }
   43 | 
   44 |   for (const item of items) {
   45 |     const fullPath = path.join(dirPath, item);
   46 |     let stat;
   47 |     try {
   48 |       stat = fs.statSync(fullPath);
   49 |     } catch (e) {
   50 |       continue;
   51 |     }
   52 | 
   53 |     if (stat.isDirectory()) {
   54 |       // Skip unwanted dirs (support glob-style *.egg-info check)
   55 |       if (SKIP_DIRS.some(d => d.startsWith('*') ? item.endsWith(d.slice(1)) : item === d)) continue;
   56 | 
   57 |       output += `\n${'='.repeat(70)}\n`;
   58 |       output += `📁 FOLDER: ${fullPath}\n`;
   59 |       output += `${'='.repeat(70)}\n`;
   60 |       scanDir(fullPath, depth + 1);
   61 | 
   62 |     } else {
   63 |       const ext = path.extname(item).toLowerCase();
   64 | 
   65 |       // Skip binary / asset extensions
   66 |       if (SKIP_EXTENSIONS.includes(ext)) continue;
   67 | 
   68 |       // ── Collect EVERY remaining file ──
   69 |       fileCount++;
   70 |       output += `\n${'-'.repeat(70)}\n`;
   71 |       output += `📄 FILE #${fileCount}: ${fullPath}\n`;
   72 |       output += `${'-'.repeat(70)}\n`;
   73 | 
   74 |       try {
   75 |         const content = fs.readFileSync(fullPath, 'utf8');
   76 |         const lines = content.split('\n');
   77 |         lines.forEach((line, i) => {
   78 |           output += `${String(i + 1).padStart(5)} | ${line}\n`;
   79 |         });
   80 |       } catch (e) {
   81 |         output += `[Could not read file: ${e.message}]\n`;
   82 |       }
   83 |     }
   84 |   }
   85 | }
   86 | 
   87 | // ── Header ──
   88 | output += `${'#'.repeat(70)}\n`;
   89 | output += `   FULL PROJECT EXPORT — JS FRONTEND + PYTHON BACKEND\n`;
   90 | output += `${'#'.repeat(70)}\n`;
   91 | output += `Generated : ${new Date().toISOString()}\n`;
   92 | output += `Root Path : ${process.cwd()}\n`;
   93 | output += `${'#'.repeat(70)}\n\n`;
   94 | 
   95 | // ── Scan ──
   96 | scanDir('.');
   97 | 
   98 | // ── Footer ──
   99 | output += `\n${'#'.repeat(70)}\n`;
  100 | output += `   EXPORT COMPLETE — Total Files: ${fileCount}\n`;
  101 | output += `${'#'.repeat(70)}\n`;
  102 | 
  103 | fs.writeFileSync(OUTPUT_FILE, output, 'utf8');
  104 | console.log(`✅ Done! Exported ${fileCount} files to: ${OUTPUT_FILE}`);

  639 |   transform-origin: 0 0;
  640 | }
  641 | </style>
  642 | </head>
  643 | <body>
  644 | 
  645 | <!-- ══ ZOOM DETECTION AND NORMALIZATION ══ -->
  646 | <script>
  647 |   // Detect and normalize zoom level
  648 |   let currentZoom = 1;
  649 |   
  650 |   function detectZoom() {
  651 |     const div = document.createElement('div');
  652 |     div.style.width = '100px';
  653 |     document.body.appendChild(div);
  654 |     const boxWidth = div.getBoundingClientRect().width;
  655 |     document.body.removeChild(div);
  656 |     
  657 |     currentZoom = 100 / boxWidth;
  658 |     document.documentElement.style.setProperty('--current-zoom', currentZoom);
  659 |   }
  660 |   
  661 |   // Detect zoom on load and on resize
  662 |   window.addEventListener('load', detectZoom);
  663 |   window.addEventListener('resize', detectZoom);
  664 |   window.addEventListener('wheel', (e) => {
  665 |     if (e.ctrlKey || e.metaKey) {
  666 |       setTimeout(detectZoom, 50);
  667 |     }
  668 |   });
  669 |   
  670 |   // Initial zoom detection
  671 |   setTimeout(detectZoom, 100);
  672 | </script>
  673 | 
  674 | <!-- ═══ CURSOR-REACTIVE CANVAS BACKGROUND ═══ -->
  675 | <canvas id="bgCanvas"></canvas>
  676 | <script>
  677 | (function(){
  678 |   const canvas = document.getElementById('bgCanvas');
  679 |   const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
  680 |   let W=0, H=0;
  681 |   const mouse = {x:-9999, y:-9999, vx:0, vy:0};
  682 |   const ripples = [], streaks = [];
  683 |   let prevSpeed = 0, t = 0;
  684 | 
  685 |   const COLS=20, ROWS=13;
  686 |   let nodes=[];
  687 | 
  688 |   function buildGrid(){
  689 |     nodes=[];
  690 |     for(let r=0;r<=ROWS;r++) for(let c=0;c<=COLS;c++)
  691 |       nodes.push({ox:(c/COLS)*W, oy:(r/ROWS)*H, x:(c/COLS)*W, y:(r/ROWS)*H, vx:0,vy:0, phase:Math.random()*Math.PI*2});
  692 |   }
  693 | 
  694 |   function resize(){
  695 |     W=canvas.width=canvas.offsetWidth;
  696 |     H=canvas.height=canvas.offsetHeight;
  697 |     buildGrid();
  698 |     // Re-scatter shapes within new bounds on first valid resize
  699 |     if(W>100&&H>100){
  700 |       SHAPES.forEach(s=>{
  701 |         if(s.x<0||s.x>W||s.y<0||s.y>H){
  702 |           s.x=50+Math.random()*(W-100);
  703 |           s.y=50+Math.random()*(H-100);
  704 |         }
  705 |       });
  706 |     }
  707 |   }
  708 | 
  709 |   window.addEventListener('resize', resize);
  710 |   window.addEventListener('mousemove', e=>{
  711 |     const r=canvas.getBoundingClientRect();
  712 |     const mx=e.clientX-r.left, my=e.clientY-r.top;
  713 |     mouse.vx=mx-mouse.x; mouse.vy=my-mouse.y;
  714 |     mouse.x=mx; mouse.y=my;
  715 |   });
  716 | 
  717 |   // ── 3D rotating wireframe shapes (replace old orbs) ──
  718 |   // Each shape: type, position, rotation angles, angular velocity, scale, colour
  719 |   const SHAPE_DEFS=[
  720 |     {type:'octa',  col:'rgba(26,86,219,',   scale:52, rx:0.003, ry:0.005, rz:0.002},
  721 |     {type:'cube',  col:'rgba(59,130,246,',  scale:38, rx:0.006, ry:0.003, rz:0.004},
  722 |     {type:'tetra', col:'rgba(139,92,246,',  scale:34, rx:0.004, ry:0.007, rz:0.003},
  723 |     {type:'octa',  col:'rgba(99,102,241,',  scale:28, rx:0.007, ry:0.002, rz:0.006},
  724 |     {type:'cube',  col:'rgba(16,185,129,',  scale:22, rx:0.005, ry:0.006, rz:0.002},
  725 |   ];
  726 |   const SHAPES=SHAPE_DEFS.map(def=>({
  727 |     ...def,
  728 |     x:Math.random()*800, y:Math.random()*600,
  729 |     vx:(Math.random()-.5)*.18, vy:(Math.random()-.5)*.14,
  730 |     ax:Math.random()*Math.PI*2, ay:Math.random()*Math.PI*2, az:Math.random()*Math.PI*2,
  731 |     phase:Math.random()*Math.PI*2, speed:0.0003+Math.random()*.0003
  732 |   }));
  733 | 
  734 |   // Raw 3D vertices for each primitive
  735 |   function octaVerts(s){const h=s*1.414;return[[0,h,0],[s,0,s],[s,0,-s],[-s,0,-s],[-s,0,s],[0,-h,0]];}
  736 |   function octaEdges(){return[[0,1],[0,2],[0,3],[0,4],[1,2],[2,3],[3,4],[4,1],[5,1],[5,2],[5,3],[5,4]];}
  737 |   function cubeVerts(s){return[[-s,-s,-s],[s,-s,-s],[s,s,-s],[-s,s,-s],[-s,-s,s],[s,-s,s],[s,s,s],[-s,s,s]];}
  738 |   function cubeEdges(){return[[0,1],[1,2],[2,3],[3,0],[4,5],[5,6],[6,7],[7,4],[0,4],[1,5],[2,6],[3,7]];}
  739 |   function tetraVerts(s){const h=s*0.816;return[[0,s,0],[s*0.943,-h/2,s*0.333],[-s*0.943,-h/2,s*0.333],[0,-h/2,-s*0.667]];}
  740 |   function tetraEdges(){return[[0,1],[0,2],[0,3],[1,2],[2,3],[3,1]];}
  741 | 
  742 |   // Rotate 3D point by Euler angles ax,ay,az
  743 |   function rot3(p,ax,ay,az){
  744 |     let[x,y,z]=p;
  745 |     // X rotation
  746 |     let y2=y*Math.cos(ax)-z*Math.sin(ax), z2=y*Math.sin(ax)+z*Math.cos(ax);
  747 |     [y,z]=[y2,z2];
  748 |     // Y rotation
  749 |     let x2=x*Math.cos(ay)+z*Math.sin(ay), z3=-x*Math.sin(ay)+z*Math.cos(ay);
  750 |     [x,z]=[x2,z3];
  751 |     // Z rotation
  752 |     let x3=x*Math.cos(az)-y*Math.sin(az), y3=x*Math.sin(az)+y*Math.cos(az);
  753 |     return[x3,y3,z];
  754 |   }
  755 | 
  756 |   // Isometric project 3D→2D (simple orthographic with slight perspective)
  757 |   function project(p3,cx,cy,fov=320){
  758 |     const[x,y,z]=p3;
  759 |     const scale=fov/(fov+z);
  760 |     return[cx+x*scale, cy-y*scale];
  761 |   }
  762 | 
  763 |   function drawShape(shape){
  764 |     const breathe=1+.04*Math.sin(t*shape.speed*5000+shape.phase);
  765 |     const s=shape.scale*breathe;
  766 | 
  767 |     // Build verts+edges for this type
  768 |     let verts, edges;
  769 |     if(shape.type==='octa'){verts=octaVerts(s);edges=octaEdges();}
  770 |     else if(shape.type==='cube'){verts=cubeVerts(s);edges=cubeEdges();}
  771 |     else{verts=tetraVerts(s);edges=tetraEdges();}
  772 | 
  773 |     // Rotate all verts
  774 |     const rotated=verts.map(v=>rot3(v,shape.ax,shape.ay,shape.az));
  775 |     // Project to 2D (use shape center as camera origin, with subtle Z-depth)
  776 |     const proj=rotated.map(v=>project(v,shape.x,shape.y,280));
  777 | 
  778 |     // Soft glow blob underneath
  779 |     const a=.018+.008*Math.sin(t*shape.speed*3000+shape.phase);
  780 |     const gr=ctx.createRadialGradient(shape.x,shape.y,0,shape.x,shape.y,s*2.2);
  781 |     gr.addColorStop(0,shape.col+(a+.012)+')');
  782 |     gr.addColorStop(1,shape.col+'0)');
  783 |     ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(shape.x,shape.y,s*2.2,0,Math.PI*2);
  784 |     ctx.fillStyle=gr; ctx.fill();
  785 | 
  786 |     // Draw edges — depth-sort by avg Z for fading
  787 |     edges.forEach(([ai,bi])=>{
  788 |       const avgZ=(rotated[ai][2]+rotated[bi][2])/(2*s);  // normalised -1..+1
  789 |       const alpha=(.08+(.22*(avgZ+1)/2)).toFixed(3);
  790 |       ctx.beginPath();
  791 |       ctx.moveTo(proj[ai][0],proj[ai][1]);
  792 |       ctx.lineTo(proj[bi][0],proj[bi][1]);
  793 |       ctx.strokeStyle=shape.col+alpha+')';
  794 |       ctx.lineWidth=1+avgZ*.5;
  795 |       ctx.stroke();
  796 |     });
  797 | 
  798 |     // Vertex dots on front-facing verts
  799 |     rotated.forEach((v,vi)=>{
  800 |       if(v[2]>-s*.2){
  801 |         ctx.beginPath();
  802 |         ctx.arc(proj[vi][0],proj[vi][1],1.2,0,Math.PI*2);
  803 |         ctx.fillStyle=shape.col+'.4)';
  804 |         ctx.fill();
  805 |       }
  806 |     });
  807 |   }
  808 | 
  809 |   function draw(){
  810 |     if(!W){ resize(); }
  811 |     ctx.clearRect(0,0,W,H);
  812 |     const spd=Math.sqrt(mouse.vx*mouse.vx+mouse.vy*mouse.vy);
  813 |     prevSpeed=prevSpeed*.85+spd*.15;
  814 | 
  815 |     // 1. 3D Floating wireframe shapes
  816 |     SHAPES.forEach(shape=>{
  817 |       // Cursor attraction (gentle)
  818 |       if(mouse.x>-1000){
  819 |         const dx=mouse.x-shape.x, dy=mouse.y-shape.y;
  820 |         const d=Math.sqrt(dx*dx+dy*dy);
  821 |         const f=Math.min(.28,90/(d+100));
  822 |         shape.vx+=dx*f*.0004; shape.vy+=dy*f*.0004;
  823 |       }
  824 |       shape.vx*=.97; shape.vy*=.97;
  825 |       shape.vx+=(Math.random()-.5)*.022; shape.vy+=(Math.random()-.5)*.018;
  826 |       shape.x+=shape.vx; shape.y+=shape.vy;
  827 |       // Wrap around edges
  828 |       if(shape.x<-shape.scale*3)shape.x=W+shape.scale*3;
  829 |       if(shape.x>W+shape.scale*3)shape.x=-shape.scale*3;
  830 |       if(shape.y<-shape.scale*3)shape.y=H+shape.scale*3;
  831 |       if(shape.y>H+shape.scale*3)shape.y=-shape.scale*3;
  832 |       // Advance rotation — cursor speed boosts spin rate
  833 |       const spinBoost=1+prevSpeed*.035;
  834 |       shape.ax+=shape.rx*spinBoost;
  835 |       shape.ay+=shape.ry*spinBoost;
  836 |       shape.az+=shape.rz*spinBoost;
  837 |       drawShape(shape);
  838 |     });
  839 | 
  840 |     // 2. Distorted grid
  841 |     const WC=COLS+1;
  842 |     nodes.forEach(n=>{
  843 |       if(mouse.x>-9000){
  844 |         const dx=mouse.x-n.ox, dy=mouse.y-n.oy;
  845 |         const d=Math.sqrt(dx*dx+dy*dy);
  846 |         const inf=Math.exp(-d*d/(2*155*155));
  847 |         n.tx=n.ox-dx*.08*inf+mouse.vx*.11*inf+Math.sin(t*.015+n.phase)*3;
  848 |         n.ty=n.oy-dy*.08*inf+mouse.vy*.11*inf+Math.cos(t*.013+n.phase*1.3)*3;
  849 |       } else {
  850 |         n.tx=n.ox+Math.sin(t*.015+n.phase)*3;
  851 |         n.ty=n.oy+Math.cos(t*.013+n.phase*1.3)*3;
  852 |       }
  853 |       n.x+=(n.tx-n.x)*.08; n.y+=(n.ty-n.y)*.08;
  854 |     });
  855 |     ctx.lineWidth=.4;
  856 |     for(let r=0;r<=ROWS;r++) for(let c=0;c<=COLS;c++){
  857 |       const n=nodes[r*WC+c];
  858 |       if(c<COLS){
  859 |         const nr=nodes[r*WC+c+1];
  860 |         const mdx=(n.x+nr.x)/2-(mouse.x||W/2), mdy=(n.y+nr.y)/2-(mouse.y||H/2);
  861 |         const prox=Math.exp(-(mdx*mdx+mdy*mdy)/(2*190*190));
  862 |         ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(n.x,n.y); ctx.lineTo(nr.x,nr.y);
  863 |         ctx.strokeStyle=`rgba(26,86,219,${(.055+prox*.18).toFixed(3)})`; ctx.stroke();
  864 |       }
  865 |       if(r<ROWS){
  866 |         const nb=nodes[(r+1)*WC+c];
  867 |         const mdx=(n.x+nb.x)/2-(mouse.x||W/2), mdy=(n.y+nb.y)/2-(mouse.y||H/2);
  868 |         const prox=Math.exp(-(mdx*mdx+mdy*mdy)/(2*190*190));
  869 |         ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(n.x,n.y); ctx.lineTo(nb.x,nb.y);
  870 |         ctx.strokeStyle=`rgba(26,86,219,${(.055+prox*.18).toFixed(3)})`; ctx.stroke();
  871 |       }
  872 |     }
  873 | 
  874 |     // 3. Cursor halo
  875 |     if(mouse.x>-9000){
  876 |       const hr=100+prevSpeed*2.8;
  877 |       const hg=ctx.createRadialGradient(mouse.x,mouse.y,0,mouse.x,mouse.y,hr);
  878 |       hg.addColorStop(0,'rgba(59,130,246,0.17)');
  879 |       hg.addColorStop(.45,'rgba(26,86,219,0.07)');
  880 |       hg.addColorStop(1,'rgba(17,68,160,0)');
  881 |       ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(mouse.x,mouse.y,hr,0,Math.PI*2);
  882 |       ctx.fillStyle=hg; ctx.fill();
  883 |       ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(mouse.x,mouse.y,3,0,Math.PI*2);
  884 |       ctx.fillStyle='rgba(59,130,246,0.55)'; ctx.fill();
  885 |       if(prevSpeed>5.5) ripples.push({x:mouse.x,y:mouse.y,r:0,maxR:55+prevSpeed*1.8,life:1});
  886 |     }
  887 | 
  888 |     // 4. Ripples
  889 |     for(let i=ripples.length-1;i>=0;i--){
  890 |       const rp=ripples[i];
  891 |       rp.r+=(rp.maxR-rp.r)*.065; rp.life-=.038;
  892 |       if(rp.life<=0){ripples.splice(i,1);continue;}
  893 |       ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(rp.x,rp.y,rp.r,0,Math.PI*2);
  894 |       ctx.strokeStyle=`rgba(59,130,246,${(rp.life*.32).toFixed(3)})`;
  895 |       ctx.lineWidth=1.2; ctx.stroke();
  896 |     }
  897 | 
  898 |     // 5. Velocity streaks
  899 |     if(spd>3.5&&mouse.x>-9000){
  900 |       streaks.push({x:mouse.x,y:mouse.y,dx:-mouse.vx,dy:-mouse.vy,len:spd*3.2,life:1,w:Math.min(spd*.14,1.8)});
  901 |     }
  902 |     for(let i=streaks.length-1;i>=0;i--){
  903 |       const s=streaks[i]; s.life-=.08;
  904 |       if(s.life<=0){streaks.splice(i,1);continue;}
  905 |       ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(s.x,s.y);
  906 |       ctx.lineTo(s.x+s.dx*(s.len/(spd||1)+1)*s.life, s.y+s.dy*(s.len/(spd||1)+1)*s.life);
  907 |       ctx.strokeStyle=`rgba(147,197,253,${(s.life*.45).toFixed(3)})`;
  908 |       ctx.lineWidth=s.w*s.life; ctx.lineCap='round'; ctx.stroke();
  909 |     }
  910 | 
  911 |     t++;
  912 |     requestAnimationFrame(draw);
  913 |   }
  914 | 
  915 |   resize();
  916 |   draw();
  917 | })();
  918 | </script>

 1281 | <script>
 1282 | /* ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 1283 |    SIDEBAR HOVER SYNC — keep content panels in sync
 1284 | ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */
 1285 | (function(){
 1286 |   const SB_COLLAPSED = 64, SB_EXPANDED = 200;
 1287 |   const MOBILE_BP = 768;
 1288 | 
 1289 |   function isMobile() { return window.innerWidth <= MOBILE_BP; }
 1290 | 
 1291 |   function syncViews(w) {
 1292 |     const charts = document.getElementById('viewCharts');
 1293 |     const report = document.getElementById('viewReport');
 1294 |     if (isMobile()) {
 1295 |       // Mobile: sidebar is at the bottom, views take full width
 1296 |       if (charts) { charts.style.left = '0'; charts.style.width = '100vw'; charts.style.height = 'calc(100vh - 52px)'; charts.style.top = '0'; }
 1297 |       if (report) { report.style.left = '0'; report.style.width = '100vw'; report.style.height = 'calc(100vh - 52px)'; report.style.top = '0'; }
 1298 |     } else {
 1299 |       // Tablet/Desktop: sidebar on the left
 1300 |       const sbW = window.innerWidth <= 1024 ? 52 : w;
 1301 |       if (charts) { charts.style.left = sbW + 'px'; charts.style.width = 'calc(100vw - ' + sbW + 'px)'; charts.style.height = '100vh'; charts.style.top = '0'; }
 1302 |       if (report) { report.style.left = sbW + 'px'; report.style.width = 'calc(100vw - ' + sbW + 'px)'; report.style.height = '100vh'; report.style.top = '0'; }
 1303 |     }
 1304 |   }
 1305 | 
 1306 |   document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
 1307 |     const sb = document.getElementById('outputSidebar');
 1308 |     if (!sb) return;
 1309 |     sb.addEventListener('mouseenter', function() { if (!isMobile()) syncViews(SB_EXPANDED); });
 1310 |     sb.addEventListener('mouseleave', function() { syncViews(SB_COLLAPSED); });
 1311 |     // Sync on resize
 1312 |     window.addEventListener('resize', function() { syncViews(SB_COLLAPSED); });
 1313 |     // Initial sync
 1314 |     syncViews(SB_COLLAPSED);
 1315 |   });
 1316 | })();

 1347 | function pickPill(el,gid){
 1348 |   const grp=gid?document.getElementById(gid):el.closest('.pills');

 1360 | 
 1361 | function goTo(s, fromNav=false){
 1362 |   // Block tab-clicking ahead — but allow Next button (fromNav=true)
 1363 |   if(!fromNav && s > step) return;
 1364 |   document.querySelectorAll('.sec').forEach(x=>x.classList.remove('active'));
 1365 |   document.getElementById('sec'+s).classList.add('active');
 1366 |   for(let i=0;i<9;i++){const b=document.getElementById('sb'+i);if(!b)continue;b.classList.remove('active','done');if(i<s)b.classList.add('done');}
 1367 |   document.getElementById('sb'+s).classList.add('active');
 1368 |   step=s;
 1369 |   document.getElementById('prevBtn').style.visibility=s===0?'hidden':'visible';
 1370 |   document.getElementById('nextBtn').textContent=s===8?'Generate Dashboard →':'Next →';
 1371 |   document.getElementById('nextBtn').className=s===8?'btn btn-go':'btn btn-primary';
 1372 |   document.getElementById('slbl').textContent=`Step ${s+1} of 9`;
 1373 |   document.getElementById('progBar').style.width=((s+1)/9*100)+'%';
 1374 |   // Update button state based on current section completion
 1375 |   calcLive();
 1376 | }
 1377 | async function downloadChartsAsImage() {
 1378 |   const chartsDiv = document.getElementById('viewCharts');
 1379 |   if (!chartsDiv) return;
 1380 | 
 1381 |   if (typeof html2canvas === 'undefined') {
 1382 |     alert('html2canvas not loaded.');
 1383 |     return;
 1384 |   }
 1385 | 
 1386 |   // Capture exactly what is on screen — no style overrides
 1387 |   const rect = chartsDiv.getBoundingClientRect();
 1388 |   const canvas = await html2canvas(chartsDiv, {
 1389 |     backgroundColor: '#f0f4ff',
 1390 |     useCORS: true,
 1391 |     scale: 2,
 1392 |     logging: false,
 1393 |     width: chartsDiv.offsetWidth,
 1394 | height: chartsDiv.offsetHeight,
 1395 |     windowWidth: window.innerWidth,
 1396 |     windowHeight: window.innerHeight,
 1397 |     scrollX: 0,
 1398 |     scrollY: 0,
 1399 |     x: 0,
 1400 | y: 0,
 1401 |   });
 1402 | 
 1403 |   const link = document.createElement('a');
 1404 |   link.download = 'charts-dashboard.png';
 1405 |   link.href = canvas.toDataURL('image/png');
 1406 |   link.click();
 1407 | }

 1409 | function getUnansweredQuestionsInSection(secNum){
 1410 |   const unanswered=[];
 1411 |   const secEl=document.getElementById('q'+secNum);
 1412 |   if(!secEl)return unanswered;
 1413 | 
 1414 |   // Check select dropdowns
 1415 |   secEl.querySelectorAll('.ai-sel').forEach(el=>{
 1416 |     if(!el.value||el.value===''){
 1417 |       const label=el.closest('.fd')?.querySelector('label')?.textContent||`Question`;
 1418 |       unanswered.push(label.replace('*','').trim());
 1419 |     }
 1420 |   });
 1421 |   // Check pill selections
 1422 |   secEl.querySelectorAll('.ai-pills').forEach(grp=>{
 1423 |     if(!grp.querySelector('.pill.on')){
 1424 |       const label=grp.closest('.fd')?.querySelector('label')?.textContent||`Question`;
 1425 |       unanswered.push(label.replace('*','').trim());
 1426 |     }
 1427 |   });
 1428 |   // Check required text inputs
 1429 |   secEl.querySelectorAll('.ai-txt').forEach(el=>{
 1430 |     if(!el.value||el.value.trim()===''){
 1431 |       const label=el.closest('.fd')?.querySelector('label')?.textContent||`Question`;
 1432 |       unanswered.push(label.replace('*','').trim());
 1433 |     }
 1434 |   });
 1435 |   // Check checkbox groups
 1436 |   secEl.querySelectorAll('.ckg').forEach(ckg=>{
 1437 |     if(!ckg.querySelector('.ai-chk:checked')){
 1438 |       const label=ckg.closest('.fd')?.querySelector('label')?.textContent||`Question`;
 1439 |       unanswered.push(label.replace('*','').trim());
 1440 |     }
 1441 |   });
 1442 |   return unanswered;
 1443 | }

 1445 | function getUnansweredQuestions(){

 1448 |     all.push(...getUnansweredQuestionsInSection(sec));
 1449 |   }
 1450 |   return all;
 1451 | }

 1453 | function showSectionError(secNum,unanswered){

 1465 |   document.body.appendChild(errorDiv);
 1466 |

 1471 | function showValidationError(unanswered){
 1472 |   const errorDiv=document.createElement('div');
 1473 |   errorDiv.id='validationError';
 1474 |   errorDiv.style.cssText='position:fixed;top:50%;left:50%;transform:translate(-50%,-50%);background:#fff;border:2px solid #dc2626;border-radius:8px;padding:24px;max-width:400px;width:90%;box-shadow:0 20px 60px rgba(0,0,0,.3);z-index:10000;font-family:"Inter",sans-serif;';
 1475 |   const listItems=unanswered.slice(0,5).map(q=>`<li style="margin:6px 0;color:#061228;font-size:13px;">${q}</li>`).join('');
 1476 |   const moreText=unanswered.length>5?`<p style="margin-top:10px;color:#6080a0;font-size:12px;">...and ${unanswered.length-5} more</p>`:'';
 1477 |   errorDiv.innerHTML=`<div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:12px;margin-bottom:16px;"><span style="font-size:24px;">⚠️</span><h3 style="margin:0;color:#dc2626;font-size:18px;">Please Answer All Questions</h3></div><p style="color:#6080a0;margin-bottom:12px;font-size:14px;">The following required questions need answers:</p><ul style="margin:0;padding-left:20px;">${listItems}</ul>${moreText}<button onclick="document.getElementById('validationError').remove()" style="margin-top:20px;width:100%;padding:10px;background:#1144a0;color:#fff;border:none;border-radius:4px;font-size:14px;cursor:pointer;font-weight:600;">Go Back and Complete</button>`;
 1478 |   document.body.appendChild(errorDiv);
 1479 | }

 1481 | function validateStep0(){
 1482 |   // Step 0: About Your Product - check context fields
 1483 |   const hasSector=document.getElementById('sector')?.value;
 1484 |   const hasBizType=document.getElementById('bizType')?.value;
 1485 |   const hasGeo=document.getElementById('geo')?.value;
 1486 |   const hasProblem=document.getElementById('problem')?.value?.trim().length>=20;
 1487 |   const hasStage=document.querySelector('#stagePills .pill.on');
 1488 |   const missing=[];
 1489 |   if(!hasSector)missing.push('Industry Sector');
 1490 |   if(!hasBizType)missing.push('Business Type');
 1491 |   if(!hasGeo)missing.push('Target Geography');
 1492 |   if (!hasProblem) {
 1493 |   const currentLen = document.getElementById('problem')?.value?.length || 0;
 1494 |   missing.push(`Problem Statement — ${currentLen}/20 characters (${20 - currentLen} more needed)`);
 1495 | }
 1496 |   if(!hasStage)missing.push('Stage of Business');
 1497 |   return missing;
 1498 | }

 1500 | function navigate(d){
 1501 |   const n=step+d;
 1502 |   if(n<0)return;
 1503 | 
 1504 |   // Trying to go forward - validate current section first
 1505 |   if(d>0&&n<=8){
 1506 |     let missing=[];
 1507 |     if(step===0){
 1508 |       missing=validateStep0();
 1509 |     }else if(step>=1&&step<=8){
 1510 |       missing=getUnansweredQuestionsInSection(step);
 1511 |     }
 1512 |     if(missing.length>0){
 1513 |       showSectionError(step,missing);
 1514 |       return;
 1515 |     }
 1516 |   }
 1517 | 
 1518 |   if(n>8){
 1519 |     // Validate all questions answered before submitting
 1520 |     const unanswered=getUnansweredQuestions();
 1521 |     if(unanswered.length>0){
 1522 |       showValidationError(unanswered);
 1523 |       return;
 1524 |     }
 1525 |     buildDashboard();
 1526 |     return;
 1527 |   }
 1528 |   if(step===0&&n===1&&ctxReady()){
 1529 |     generateAIQuestions().then(()=>goTo(1, true));
 1530 | 
 1531 |   }else{
 1532 |     goTo(n, true);
 1533 |   }
 1534 | }

 1538 | function onCtxChange(){
 1539 |   // Auto-save ALL form fields to localStorage under the same key the load event reads
 1540 |   localStorage.setItem('infopace_form', JSON.stringify({
 1541 |     bizName: document.getElementById('bizName')?.value || '',
 1542 |     sector:  document.getElementById('sector')?.value || '',
 1543 |     bizType: document.getElementById('bizType')?.value || '',
 1544 |     geo:     document.getElementById('geo')?.value || '',
 1545 |     problem: document.getElementById('problem')?.value || '',
 1546 |     stage:   document.querySelector('#stagePills .pill.on')?.dataset.val || ''
 1547 |   }));
 1548 |   const s=document.getElementById('sector');
 1549 |   const tag=document.getElementById('sectorTag');
 1550 |   if(s.value){tag.textContent=s.options[s.selectedIndex].text.split('/')[0].trim();tag.classList.add('active');}
 1551 |   else{tag.textContent='All Sectors';tag.classList.remove('active');}
 1552 |   updateProblemCounter();
 1553 |   calcLive();

 1556 | /* ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 1557 |    LIVE SCORING
 1558 | ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */
 1559 | function calcLive(){
 1560 |   // ── Step 0 context fields ──────────────────────────────
 1561 |   const hasSector  = document.getElementById('sector').value?1:0;
 1562 |   const hasBizType = document.getElementById('bizType').value?1:0;
 1563 |   const hasGeo     = document.getElementById('geo').value?1:0;
 1564 |   const probLen    = document.getElementById('problem').value.length;
 1565 |   const probScore  = probLen>120?5:probLen>60?3:probLen>20?1:0;
 1566 |   const stageVal   = +(document.querySelector('#stagePills .pill.on')?.dataset.val)||0;
 1567 | 
 1568 |   // Only score if context is filled
 1569 |   const contextFilled = hasSector&&hasBizType&&hasGeo;
 1570 | 
 1571 |   // ── Read actual selected values from AI questions ──────
 1572 |   // Each select has data-w (weight) and returns v (1-5)
 1573 |   // We track which section each question belongs to via ID prefix
 1574 |   const selScores={d1:[],d2:[],d3:[],d4:[],d5:[],d6:[]};
 1575 | 
 1576 |   // Map question IDs to dimensions
 1577 |   // s1=Market Size(d1), s2=Audience(d2), s3=Competition(d3),
 1578 |   // s4=Revenue(d4), s5=Risk(d5), s6=GTM(d4), s7=PMF(d2), s8=SectorFit(d6)
 1579 |   const dimMap={'s1':'d1','s2':'d2','s3':'d3','s4':'d4','s5':'d5','s6':'d4','s7':'d2','s8':'d6','f1':'d1','f2':'d2','f3':'d3','f4':'d4','f5':'d5','f6':'d4','f7':'d2','f8':'d6'};
 1580 | 
 1581 |   document.querySelectorAll('.ai-sel').forEach(el=>{
 1582 |     if(!el.value)return;
 1583 |     const v=+(el.value)||0;          // actual selected value 1-5
 1584 |     const w=+(el.dataset.w)||2;      // weight of this question
 1585 |     const prefix=el.id.replace(/q\d+$/,'').replace(/^s/,'s').slice(0,2); // e.g. s1, s2
 1586 |     const dim=dimMap[prefix]||dimMap[el.id.slice(0,2)]||'d1';
 1587 |     (selScores[dim]=selScores[dim]||[]).push({v,w});
 1588 |   });
 1589 | 
 1590 |   document.querySelectorAll('.ai-pills').forEach(grp=>{
 1591 |     const on=grp.querySelector('.pill.on');
 1592 |     if(!on)return;
 1593 |     const v=+(on.dataset.val)||3;
 1594 |     const id=grp.id||'';
 1595 | const prefix=id.replace(/_pills$/,'').slice(0,2);
 1596 | // Fall back: find nearest parent #q1–#q8 container
 1597 | const dim=dimMap[prefix]||(()=>{
 1598 |   const secEl=grp.closest('.sec')||grp.closest('[id^="q"]');
 1599 |   const rawId=secEl?secEl.id:'';
 1600 |   const secNum=rawId?+(rawId.replace('sec','').replace('q',''))||1:1;
 1601 |   const secDimKeys=['d1','d2','d3','d4','d5','d4','d2','d6'];
 1602 |   return secDimKeys[secNum-1]||'d1';
 1603 | })();
 1604 |     (selScores[dim]=selScores[dim]||[]).push({v,w:2});
 1605 |   });
 1606 | 
 1607 |   document.querySelectorAll('.ai-chk:checked').forEach(el=>{
 1608 |     const section=el.closest('.sec');
 1609 |     const secId=section?.id||'sec1';
 1610 |     const secNum=+secId.replace('sec','')||1;
 1611 |     const dimKeys=['d1','d2','d3','d4','d5','d4','d2','d6'];
 1612 |     const dim=dimKeys[secNum-1]||'d6';
 1613 |     (selScores[dim]=selScores[dim]||[]).push({v:4,w:1}); // checkboxes = moderate positive
 1614 |   });
 1615 | 
 1616 |   // ── Calculate each dimension score (0-100) ────────────
 1617 |   function dimScore(key){
 1618 |     const items=selScores[key]||[];
 1619 |     if(!items.length)return null;
 1620 |     const totalW=items.reduce((s,i)=>s+i.w,0);
 1621 |     const weighted=items.reduce((s,i)=>s+(i.v*i.w),0);
 1622 |     const avg=weighted/totalW; // 1.0–5.0
 1623 |     const linear=(avg-1)/4*100; // 0–100
 1624 |     // Full range: low answers score low, high answers score high
 1625 |     return Math.min(100, Math.max(0, Math.round(linear<25 ? linear*0.8 : linear>75 ? 75+(linear-75)*1.0 : linear)));
 1626 |   }
 1627 | 
 1628 |   const d1=dimScore('d1'); // Market Size
 1629 |   const d2=dimScore('d2'); // Audience Quality
 1630 |   const d3=dimScore('d3'); // Competition Edge
 1631 |   const d4=dimScore('d4'); // Revenue Potential
 1632 |   const d5=dimScore('d5'); // Risk Profile
 1633 |   const d6=dimScore('d6'); // Sector Fit
 1634 | 
 1635 |   // ── Context bonus (filling basics) ────────────────────
 1636 |   // Max 15 points for context — NOT for just having a sector selected
 1637 |   const contextBonus=contextFilled?(hasSector*3+hasBizType*3+hasGeo*2+probScore+Math.min(stageVal,5)):0;
 1638 | 
 1639 |   // ── Overall score = weighted average of dims + context ─
 1640 |   // Dims that haven't been answered yet are excluded from average
 1641 |   const answeredDims=[d1,d2,d3,d4,d5,d6].filter(v=>v!==null);
 1642 |   let overall=0;
 1643 |   if(!contextFilled||answeredDims.length===0){
 1644 |     // Nothing meaningful answered — score is 0
 1645 |     overall=0;
 1646 |   } else {
 1647 |     // Weighted: competition(d3) and revenue(d4) matter most
 1648 |     const weights=[15,20,25,25,10,5]; // d1 d2 d3 d4 d5 d6
 1649 |     const allDims=[d1,d2,d3,d4,d5,d6];
 1650 |     let wSum=0, wTotal=0;
 1651 |     allDims.forEach((v,i)=>{
 1652 |       if(v!==null){wSum+=v*weights[i];wTotal+=weights[i];}
 1653 |     });
 1654 |     const dimAvg=wTotal>0?wSum/wTotal:0;
 1655 | 
 1656 |     // Context bonus adds up to 15 points on top of dim average
 1657 |     // But only if at least 2 sections answered
 1658 |     const bonus=answeredDims.length>=2?Math.round(contextBonus*0.25):0;
 1659 |     overall=Math.min(100,Math.round(dimAvg+bonus));
 1660 | 
 1661 |     // Penalty: if less than 3 sections answered, cap score at 60
 1662 |     // if(answeredDims.length<3)overall=Math.min(overall,60);
 1663 |     window._liveOverallScore=overall>0?overall:null;
 1664 |   }
 1665 | 
 1666 |   // ── Count completion progress ──────────────────────────
 1667 |   function countQuestions(){
 1668 |     let total=0,answered=0;
 1669 |     for(let sec=1;sec<=8;sec++){
 1670 |       const secEl=document.getElementById('q'+sec);
 1671 |       if(!secEl)continue;
 1672 |       // Select dropdowns
 1673 |       secEl.querySelectorAll('.ai-sel').forEach(el=>{total++;if(el.value)answered++;});
 1674 |       // Pills
 1675 |       secEl.querySelectorAll('.ai-pills').forEach(grp=>{total++;if(grp.querySelector('.pill.on'))answered++;});
 1676 |       // Text inputs
 1677 |       secEl.querySelectorAll('.ai-txt').forEach(el=>{total++;if(el.value&&el.value.trim())answered++;});
 1678 |       // Checkboxes (per group)
 1679 |       secEl.querySelectorAll('.ckg').forEach(ckg=>{total++;if(ckg.querySelector('.ai-chk:checked'))answered++;});
 1680 |     }
 1681 |     return{total,answered};
 1682 |   }
 1683 |   const{total,answered}=countQuestions();
 1684 |   const allAnswered=total>0&&answered>=total;
 1685 | 
 1686 |   // ── Update UI ─────────────────────────────────────────
 1687 |   const lsEl=document.getElementById('liveScore');
 1688 |   const lgEl=document.getElementById('liveGrade');
 1689 |   if(overall===0){
 1690 |     lsEl.textContent='0';lsEl.className='big-sc sc-zero';
 1691 |     const progressText=total>0?`(${answered}/${total} answered)`:'Fill in the form';
 1692 |     lgEl.textContent=progressText;lgEl.style.color='#94a3b8';
 1693 |     document.getElementById('topScoreWrap').style.display='none';
 1694 |     // Reset dim bars
 1695 |     ['bf1','bf2','bf3','bf4','bf5','bf6'].forEach(id=>{const el=document.getElementById(id);if(el)el.style.width='0%';});
 1696 |     ['d1lbl','d2lbl','d3lbl','d4lbl','d5lbl','d6lbl'].forEach(id=>{const el=document.getElementById(id);if(el)el.textContent='—';});
 1697 |     return;
 1698 |   }
 1699 |   // Show completion status in grade text
 1700 |   const progressSuffix=total>0?` (${answered}/${total})`:'';
 1701 |   lsEl.textContent=overall;
 1702 |   if(overall>=70){lsEl.className='big-sc sc-high';lgEl.textContent='High Potential ✓'+progressSuffix;lgEl.style.color='#059669';}
 1703 |   else if(overall>=45){lsEl.className='big-sc sc-mid';lgEl.textContent='Moderate Potential'+progressSuffix;lgEl.style.color='#f59e0b';}
 1704 |   else{lsEl.className='big-sc sc-low';lgEl.textContent='Needs Strengthening'+progressSuffix;lgEl.style.color='#dc2626';}
 1705 | 
 1706 |   document.getElementById('topScoreWrap').style.display='flex';
 1707 |   document.getElementById('topScore').textContent=overall+'/100';
 1708 | 
 1709 |   // ── Update Next/Generate Dashboard button state ──────
 1710 |   const nextBtn=document.getElementById('nextBtn');
 1711 |   if(nextBtn){
 1712 |     let currentMissing=[];
 1713 |     if(step===0){
 1714 |       currentMissing=validateStep0();
 1715 |     }else if(step>=1&&step<=8){
 1716 |       currentMissing=getUnansweredQuestionsInSection(step);
 1717 |     }
 1718 |     const canProceed=currentMissing.length===0;
 1719 | 
 1720 |     if(step===8){
 1721 |       // Final step - Generate Dashboard
 1722 |       nextBtn.className='btn btn-go';
 1723 |       nextBtn.style.opacity=canProceed?'1':'0.5';
 1724 |       nextBtn.title=canProceed?'Generate your market intelligence dashboard':`Answer all ${currentMissing.length} remaining question(s) to generate dashboard`;
 1725 |     }else{
 1726 |       // Steps 0-7 - Next button
 1727 |       nextBtn.className='btn btn-primary';
 1728 |       nextBtn.style.opacity=canProceed?'1':'0.5';
 1729 |       nextBtn.title=canProceed?'Proceed to next step':`Complete ${currentMissing.length} required field(s) to continue`;
 1730 |     }
 1731 |   }
 1732 | 
 1733 |   // ── Update individual dimension bars ──────────────────
 1734 |   const dimVals=[d1,d2,d3,d4,d5,d6];
 1735 |   const dimColors=['#1a56db','#86198f','#10b981','#f43f5e','#f97316','#06b6d4'];
 1736 |   ['bf1','bf2','bf3','bf4','bf5','bf6'].forEach((id,i)=>{
 1737 |     const el=document.getElementById(id);
 1738 |     if(!el)return;
 1739 |     const v=dimVals[i];
 1740 |     el.style.width=(v!==null?v:0)+'%';
 1741 |     el.style.background=dimColors[i];
 1742 |   });
 1743 |   ['d1lbl','d2lbl','d3lbl','d4lbl','d5lbl','d6lbl'].forEach((id,i)=>{
 1744 |     const el=document.getElementById(id);
 1745 |     if(!el)return;
 1746 |     const v=dimVals[i];
 1747 |     el.textContent=v!==null?v+'/100':'—';
 1748 |   });
 1749 | 
 1750 |   buildLiveInsights(overall,{d1,d2,d3,d4,d5,d6});
 1751 | }
 1752 | 
 1753 | function updateProblemCounter() {
 1754 |   const val  = document.getElementById('problem').value;
 1755 |   const len  = val.length;
 1756 |   const counter = document.getElementById('probCounter');
 1757 |   const hint    = document.getElementById('probHint');
 1758 |   if (!counter) return;
 1759 | 
 1760 |   if (len < 20) {
 1761 |     counter.textContent = `${len} / 20`;
 1762 |     counter.style.color = len > 10 ? '#f59e0b' : '#dc2626'; // orange when close, red when far
 1763 |     hint.style.color    = '#dc2626';
 1764 |   } else {
 1765 |     counter.textContent = `${len} ✓`;
 1766 |     counter.style.color = '#059669';  // green when valid
 1767 |     hint.style.color    = '#94a3b8';
 1768 |   }
 1769 | }
 1770 | 
 1771 | function buildLiveInsights(t,dims){
 1772 |   const sec=document.getElementById('sector').value;
 1773 |   const geo=document.getElementById('geo').value;
 1774 |   const items=[];
 1775 |   dims=dims||{};
 1776 | 
 1777 |   // Score-based headline
 1778 |   if(t>=70)items.push('Strong overall market potential — fundamentals solid across answered dimensions.');
 1779 |   else if(t>=50)items.push('Moderate potential — see which dimensions below need strengthening.');
 1780 |   else if(t>=30)items.push('Several dimensions are weak — fill more steps to get precise guidance.');
 1781 |   else if(t>0)items.push('Early stage — complete all 9 steps for a full and accurate score.');
 1782 | 
 1783 |   // Dimension-specific insights — only shown when that dim is answered
 1784 |   const dimNames={d1:'Market Size',d2:'Audience Quality',d3:'Competition Edge',d4:'Revenue Potential',d5:'Risk Profile',d6:'Sector Fit'};
 1785 |   const weakDims=Object.entries(dims).filter(([,v])=>v!==null&&v<45).sort((a,b)=>a[1]-b[1]);
 1786 |   const strongDims=Object.entries(dims).filter(([,v])=>v!==null&&v>=70).sort((a,b)=>b[1]-a[1]);
 1787 | 
 1788 |   if(weakDims.length>0){
 1789 |     const [wk,wv]=weakDims[0];
 1790 |     items.push(`⚠️ ${dimNames[wk]} scores ${wv}/100 — your weakest dimension. Focus here first.`);
 1791 |   }
 1792 |   if(strongDims.length>0){
 1793 |     const [sk,sv]=strongDims[0];
 1794 |     items.push(`✅ ${dimNames[sk]} scores ${sv}/100 — your strongest signal to lead with.`);
 1795 |   }
 1796 | 
 1797 |   // Sector-specific tips
 1798 |   if(sec==='IT')items.push('SaaS: NRR above 110% is the single most bankable investor signal.');

 1854 | // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 1855 | //   AI QUESTION GENERATION — instant fallback on any failure
 1856 | // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 1857 | async function generateAIQuestions(){
 1858 |   const sEl=document.getElementById('sector');
 1859 |   const tEl=document.getElementById('bizType');
 1860 |   const gEl=document.getElementById('geo');
 1861 |   const sector  = sEl.options[sEl.selectedIndex].text;
 1862 |   const bizType = tEl.options[tEl.selectedIndex].text;
 1863 |   const geo     = gEl.options[gEl.selectedIndex].text;
 1864 |   const problem = document.getElementById('problem').value||'Not specified';
 1865 |   const bizName = document.getElementById('bizName').value||'the product';
 1866 |   const stage   = document.querySelector('#stagePills .pill.on')?.textContent||'Not specified';
 1867 | 
 1868 |   // Show skeletons briefly while we try
 1869 |   [1,2,3,4,5,6,7,8].forEach(i=>{
 1870 |     const el=document.getElementById('q'+i);
 1871 |     if(el)el.innerHTML='<div class="ql-skeleton"><div class="ql-skel-item"></div><div class="ql-skel-item"></div><div class="ql-skel-item"></div></div>';
 1872 |   });
 1873 | 
 1874 |   // Helper: race a fetch against a timeout — if timeout wins, throw immediately
 1875 |   const fetchWithTimeout=(url,opts,ms=5000)=>{
 1876 |     const abort=new AbortController();
 1877 |     const timer=setTimeout(()=>abort.abort(),ms);
 1878 |     return fetch(url,{...opts,signal:abort.signal})
 1879 |       .finally(()=>clearTimeout(timer));
 1880 |   };
 1881 | 
 1882 |   try{
 1883 |     const resp=await fetchWithTimeout('/api',{
 1884 |       method:'POST',
 1885 |       headers:{'Content-Type':'application/json'},
 1886 |       body:JSON.stringify({
 1887 |         _type:'questions',
 1888 |         prompt:`Generate 8 JSON question sections for market assessment.
 1889 | Sector:${sector} | Type:${bizType} | Geo:${geo} | Product:${bizName} | Stage:${stage}
 1890 | Problem:${problem}
 1891 | 
 1892 | Rules: Questions 100% specific to ${sector}+${bizType}+${geo}. 4 questions per section. Types: select(options with t+v 1-5), pills(options t only), checks(options t only). Options under 35 chars.
 1893 | 
 1894 | Return ONLY this JSON structure, no markdown:
 1895 | {"sb8txt":"<2 words>","d6name":"<dimension>","sections":[
 1896 | {"id":1,"title":"Market Size & TAM","icon":"📊","subtitle":"${sector} TAM in ${geo}","questions":[
 1897 | {"id":"s1q1","label":"<specific TAM question>","hint":"<real ₹Cr/$B benchmark>","type":"select","w":3,"options":[{"t":"Above ₹10,000Cr","v":5},{"t":"₹1,000–10,000Cr","v":4},{"t":"₹100–1,000Cr","v":3},{"t":"₹10–100Cr","v":2},{"t":"Under ₹10Cr","v":1}]},
 1898 | {"id":"s1q2","label":"<specific CAGR question>","hint":"<real sector CAGR>","type":"pills","options":[{"t":">50% YoY"},{"t":"25–50%"},{"t":"10–25%"},{"t":"5–10%"},{"t":"<5%"}]},
 1899 | {"id":"s1q3","label":"<specific segment question>","hint":"<real gap insight>","type":"select","w":4,"options":[{"t":"<opt1>","v":5},{"t":"<opt2>","v":4},{"t":"<opt3>","v":3},{"t":"<opt4>","v":2},{"t":"<opt5>","v":1}]},
 1900 | {"id":"s1q4","label":"<specific tailwinds>","hint":"<real context>","type":"checks","options":[{"t":"<item1>"},{"t":"<item2>"},{"t":"<item3>"},{"t":"<item4>"},{"t":"<item5>"},{"t":"<item6>"}]}
 1901 | ]},
 1902 | {"id":2,"title":"Buyer Quality & WTP","icon":"🎯","subtitle":"${bizType} buyers in ${sector}","questions":[<4 specific questions>]},
 1903 | {"id":3,"title":"Competitive Landscape","icon":"⚔️","subtitle":"${sector} competition in ${geo}","questions":[<4 specific questions>]},
 1904 | {"id":4,"title":"Revenue & Unit Economics","icon":"💰","subtitle":"Monetisation for ${sector}","questions":[<4 specific questions>]},
 1905 | {"id":5,"title":"Risk & Market Timing","icon":"⚠️","subtitle":"${sector} risks in ${geo}","questions":[<4 specific questions>]},
 1906 | {"id":6,"title":"Go-to-Market Power","icon":"🚀","subtitle":"GTM for ${geo}","questions":[<4 specific questions>]},
 1907 | {"id":7,"title":"Output & PMF Signal","icon":"📤","subtitle":"Validation evidence","questions":[<4 specific questions>]},
 1908 | {"id":8,"title":"${sector} Deep-Dive","icon":"🔬","subtitle":"${sector}-specific depth","questions":[<4 highly specific ${sector} questions>]}
 1909 | ]}`
 1910 |       })
 1911 |     }, 5000); // ← 5 second hard timeout
 1912 | 
 1913 |     if(!resp.ok) throw new Error('HTTP '+resp.status);
 1914 | 
 1915 |     const data=await resp.json();
 1916 |     const allText=(data?.candidates?.[0]?.content?.parts||[]).map(p=>p.text||'').join('');
 1917 |     if(!allText) throw new Error('Empty response');
 1918 | 
 1919 |     let raw=allText.trim();
 1920 |     const fenceMatch=raw.match(/```(?:json)?\s*([\s\S]*?)```/);
 1921 |     if(fenceMatch) raw=fenceMatch[1].trim();
 1922 |     const start=raw.indexOf('{'), end=raw.lastIndexOf('}');
 1923 |     if(start===-1||end===-1) throw new Error('No JSON in response');
 1924 |     raw=raw.slice(start,end+1);
 1925 | 
 1926 |     let parsed;
 1927 |     try{ parsed=JSON.parse(raw); }
 1928 |     catch(_){
 1929 |       try{ parsed=JSON.parse(repairTruncatedJSON(raw)); }
 1930 |       catch(e2){ throw new Error('JSON parse failed'); }
 1931 |     }
 1932 | 
 1933 |     if(!Array.isArray(parsed.sections)||parsed.sections.length===0)
 1934 |       throw new Error('No sections in response');
 1935 | 
 1936 |     aiQs=parsed;
 1937 |     if(aiQs.sb8txt)document.getElementById('sb8txt').textContent=aiQs.sb8txt;
 1938 |     if(aiQs.d6name)document.getElementById('d6name').textContent=aiQs.d6name;
 1939 |     if(aiQs.realTimeData)window._rtData=aiQs.realTimeData;
 1940 |     aiQs.sections.forEach((sec,i)=>renderSection(i+1,sec));
 1941 | 
 1942 |   }catch(e){
 1943 |     // Any failure (timeout, 429, network, parse error) → immediate fallback
 1944 |     console.warn('AI questions failed, using fallback:',e.message);
 1945 |     useFallbackQuestions(sector,bizType,geo);
 1946 |   }
 1947 | }

 1949 | // ── SCREENSHOT & NOTIFY REACT ─────────────────────────────────
 1950 | async function captureAndSendScreenshot() {
 1951 |   try {
 1952 |     const el = document.getElementById('dashShell');
 1953 |     if (!el) return;
 1954 | 
 1955 |     // Wait one frame to ensure charts are fully painted
 1956 |     await new Promise(r => requestAnimationFrame(() => requestAnimationFrame(r)));
 1957 | 
 1958 |     const canvas = await html2canvas(el, {
 1959 |       scale: 2,              // 2× resolution for sharp PNG
 1960 |       useCORS: true,
 1961 |       backgroundColor: '#f0f4ff',
 1962 |       logging: false,
 1963 |       windowWidth: el.scrollWidth,
 1964 |       windowHeight: el.scrollHeight,
 1965 |     });
 1966 | 
 1967 |     // Convert to PNG blob
 1968 |     canvas.toBlob(blob => {
 1969 |       if (!blob) return;
 1970 | 
 1971 |       // 1. Auto-download to user's device
 1972 |       const url  = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
 1973 |       const link = document.createElement('a');
 1974 |       link.href     = url;
 1975 |       link.download = `infopace-dashboard-${Date.now()}.png`;
 1976 |       link.click();
 1977 |       URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
 1978 | 
 1979 |       // 2. Send blob to React parent for Supabase upload
 1980 |       blob.arrayBuffer().then(buf => {
 1981 |         window.parent.postMessage({
 1982 |           type:     'INFOPACE_SCREENSHOT',
 1983 |           buffer:   buf,
 1984 |           filename: `dashboard-${Date.now()}.png`,
 1985 |         }, '*', [buf]); // transfer ownership for performance
 1986 |       });
 1987 | 
 1988 |     }, 'image/png', 1.0);
 1989 | 
 1990 |   } catch(e) {
 1991 |     console.warn('Screenshot failed:', e.message);
 1992 |   }
 1993 | }
 1994 | 
 1995 | /* Repair a truncated JSON string by closing any open structures */
 1996 | function repairTruncatedJSON(s){
 1997 |   // Walk the string tracking depth; truncate at last complete top-level section
 1998 |   // Strategy: find the last occurrence of "}]}" or "}]," and close from there
 1999 |   let best=s;
 2000 |   // Try progressively shorter slices to find parseable JSON
 2001 |   for(let i=s.length-1;i>s.length*0.4;i--){
 2002 |     const c=s[i];
 2003 |     if(c==='}'){
 2004 |       try{
 2005 |         const candidate=closeJSON(s.slice(0,i+1));
 2006 |         JSON.parse(candidate);
 2007 |         best=candidate;
 2008 |         break;
 2009 |       }catch(_){}
 2010 |     }
 2011 |   }
 2012 |   return best;
 2013 | }
 2014 | 
 2015 | function closeJSON(s){
 2016 |   // Count open brackets/braces
 2017 |   let depth=0; const stack=[];
 2018 |   for(const c of s){
 2019 |     if(c==='{'){stack.push('}');}
 2020 |     else if(c==='['){stack.push(']');}
 2021 |     else if(c==='}'||c===']'){stack.pop();}
 2022 |   }
 2023 |   // Close any trailing comma before we close
 2024 |   let result=s.replace(/,\s*$/,'');
 2025 |   return result+stack.reverse().join('');
 2026 | }
 2027 | 
 2028 | function renderSection(idx,sec){
 2029 |   const el=document.getElementById('q'+idx);
 2030 |   if(!el||!sec)return;
 2031 |   let html=`<div class="sec-hd"><div class="sec-icon">${sec.icon||'📋'}</div><div><div class="sec-ttl">${sec.title}</div><div class="sec-sub">${sec.subtitle||''}</div></div></div><div class="fg">`;
 2032 |   (sec.questions||[]).forEach(q=>{
 2033 |     const wide=q.type==='checks'||q.type==='textarea';
 2034 |     html+=`<div class="fd ${wide?'s2':''}">`;
 2035 |     html+=`<label>${q.label}</label>`;
 2036 |     if(q.hint)html+=`<div class="hint">💡 ${q.hint}</div>`;
 2037 |     if(q.type==='select'){
 2038 |       html+=`<select class="ai-sel" id="${q.id}" data-w="${q.w||2}" onchange="calcLive()"><option value="">Select…</option>`;
 2039 |       (q.options||[]).forEach(o=>{html+=`<option value="${o.v}">${o.t}</option>`;});
 2040 |       html+=`</select>`;
 2041 |     }else if(q.type==='pills'){
 2042 |       html+=`<div class="pills ai-pills" id="${q.id}_pills">`;
 2043 |       (q.options||[]).forEach((o,oi,arr)=>{
 2044 |   const autoV = o.v || Math.round(5 - (oi/(Math.max(arr.length-1,1)))*4);
 2045 |   html+=`<span class="pill" data-val="${autoV}" onclick="pickAIPill(this)">${o.t}</span>`;
 2046 | });
 2047 |       html+=`</div>`;
 2048 |     }else if(q.type==='checks'){
 2049 |       html+=`<div class="ckg">`;
 2050 |       (q.options||[]).forEach(o=>{html+=`<label class="cki"><input type="checkbox" class="ai-chk" onchange="calcLive()"> ${o.t}</label>`;});
 2051 |       html+=`</div>`;
 2052 |     }else if(q.type==='text'){
 2053 |       html+=`<input type="text" class="ai-txt" id="${q.id}" placeholder="${q.placeholder||'Enter value…'}" oninput="calcLive()"/>`;
 2054 |     }
 2055 |     html+=`</div>`;
 2056 |   });
 2057 |   html+=`</div>`;
 2058 |   el.innerHTML=html;
 2059 | }

 2839 | function collectData(){

 2841 |   const getv=id=>document.getElementById(id)?.value||'';

 2844 |   document.querySelectorAll('.ai-pills').forEach(grp=>{const on=grp.querySelector('.pill.on');if(on)answers[grp.id]=on.textContent;});
 2845 |   document.querySelectorAll('.ai-txt').forEach(el=>{if(el.value)answers[el.id]=el.value;});
 2846 |   const chkGroups={};
 2847 |   document.querySelectorAll('.ai-chk:checked').forEach(el=>{const g=el.closest('.ckg')?.parentElement?.querySelector('label')?.textContent||'checks';chkGroups[g]=(chkGroups[g]||[]);chkGroups[g].push(el.parentElement.textContent.trim());});
 2848 |   Object.assign(answers,chkGroups);
 2849 |   const fd={
 2850 |     bizName:getv('bizName')||'Unnamed Business',
 2851 |     sector:gopt('sector'),sectorCode:getv('sector'),
 2852 |     bizType:gopt('bizType'),bizTypeCode:getv('bizType'),
 2853 |     geo:gopt('geo'),geoCode:getv('geo'),
 2854 |     problem:getv('problem')||'Not described',
 2855 |     stage:document.querySelector('#stagePills .pill.on')?.textContent||'Not specified',
 2856 |     answers,
 2857 |   };
 2858 |   localStorage.setItem('infopace_form', JSON.stringify({
 2859 |     bizName: fd.bizName,
 2860 |     sector:  fd.sectorCode,
 2861 |     bizType: fd.bizTypeCode,
 2862 |     geo:     fd.geoCode,
 2863 |     problem: fd.problem,
 2864 |     stage:   document.querySelector('#stagePills .pill.on')?.dataset.val || ''
 2865 |   }));
 2866 |   return fd;

 2883 | // ✅ FIXED — tries API once, goes offline immediately on any failure:
 2884 | async function buildDashboard(){
 2885 |   const fd=collectData();
 2886 |   showLoader();
 2887 |   setLoader(1,'Reading your inputs…',8);
 2888 | 
 2889 |   const fetchWithTimeout=(url,opts,ms=8000)=>{
 2890 |     const abort=new AbortController();
 2891 |     const timer=setTimeout(()=>abort.abort(),ms);
 2892 |     return fetch(url,{...opts,signal:abort.signal}).finally(()=>clearTimeout(timer));
 2893 |   };
 2894 | 
 2895 |   let analysis;
 2896 |   try{
 2897 |     setLoader(2,`Analysing ${fd.sector} market…`,30);
 2898 |     const prompt=buildPrompt(fd);
 2899 |     const resp=await fetchWithTimeout('/api',{
 2900 |       method:'POST',
 2901 |       headers:{'Content-Type':'application/json'},
 2902 |       body:JSON.stringify({_type:'analysis',prompt})
 2903 |     },8000);
 2904 |     if(!resp.ok) throw new Error('HTTP '+resp.status);
 2905 |     const data=await resp.json();
 2906 |     const allText=(data?.candidates?.[0]?.content?.parts||[]).map(p=>p.text||'').join('');
 2907 |     if(!allText) throw new Error('Empty response');
 2908 |     let raw=allText.trim();
 2909 |     const fm=raw.match(/```(?:json)?\s*([\s\S]*?)```/);
 2910 |     if(fm) raw=fm[1].trim();
 2911 |     const s0=raw.indexOf('{'),e0=raw.lastIndexOf('}');
 2912 |     if(s0===-1||e0===-1) throw new Error('No JSON');
 2913 |     raw=raw.slice(s0,e0+1);
 2914 |     let parsed;
 2915 |     try{ parsed=JSON.parse(raw); }
 2916 |     catch(_){ try{ parsed=JSON.parse(repairTruncatedJSON(raw)); }catch(e2){ throw new Error('Parse failed'); } }
 2917 |     if(!parsed||typeof parsed!=='object') throw new Error('Invalid JSON');
 2918 |     analysis=parsed;
 2919 |     setLoader(5,'Assembling dashboard…',95);
 2920 |     await tick(300);
 2921 |   }catch(e){
 2922 |     console.warn('Gemini API failed, using offline analysis:',e.message);
 2923 |     setLoader(5,'Building live analysis…',95);
 2924 |     analysis=offlineAnalysis(fd);
 2925 |     await tick(200);
 2926 |   }
 2927 |   renderDash(fd,analysis);
 2928 | }

 3036 |   // Exponential backoff helper (shared pattern)
 3037 |   // ✅ REPLACE WITH — single attempt, 10s timeout, immediate throw on any failure:
 3038 | const fetchWithRetry=async(url,opts)=>{
 3039 |   const controller=new AbortController();
 3040 |   const timeout=setTimeout(()=>controller.abort(),10000); // 10s timeout
 3041 |   try{
 3042 |     const r=await fetch(url,{...opts,signal:controller.signal});
 3043 |     clearTimeout(timeout);
 3044 |     if(!r.ok) throw new Error('HTTP '+r.status);
 3045 |     return r;
 3046 |   }catch(e){
 3047 |     clearTimeout(timeout);
 3048 |     throw new Error('API unavailable: '+e.message);
 3049 |   }
 3050 | };

 3052 |   const _KEY2='USE_SERVER_KEY';
 3053 |   const resp=await fetchWithRetry('/api',{method:'POST',headers:{'Content-Type':'application/json'},body:JSON.stringify({

 3056 |   // ── Gemini response parsing ──
 3057 |   if(!resp.ok) throw new Error('HTTP '+resp.status);

 3060 |   if(!allText) throw new Error('Empty API response');
 3061 | 
 3062 |   // Strip markdown fences
 3063 |   let raw=allText.trim();
 3064 |   const fm=raw.match(/```(?:json)?\s*([\s\S]*?)```/);
 3065 |   if(fm) raw=fm[1].trim();
 3066 | 
 3067 |   // Find outermost JSON object
 3068 |   const s0=raw.indexOf('{'), e0=raw.lastIndexOf('}');
 3069 |   if(s0===-1||e0===-1) throw new Error('No JSON in response');
 3070 |   raw=raw.slice(s0,e0+1);
 3071 | 
 3072 |   // Parse with truncation repair fallback
 3073 |   let parsed;
 3074 |   try{ parsed=JSON.parse(raw); }
 3075 |   catch(_){

 3077 |     catch(e2){ throw new Error('JSON parse failed: '+e2.message); }
 3078 |   }

 3080 |   // This ensures we ALWAYS use real AI data where available, fill gaps from fallback
 3081 |   if(!parsed||typeof parsed!=='object'){
 3082 |     throw new Error('No valid JSON from Gemini');
 3083 |   }
 3084 |   console.log('Gemini returned fields:', Object.keys(parsed).join(', '));
 3085 |   // Return what we got — renderDash has guards for missing fields

 3193 | // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
 3194 | //  OFFLINE ANALYSIS  — fully input-driven replacement
 3195 | //  Drop this in place of the existing offlineAnalysis() in dashboard.html
 3196 | //  Every number, every label, every text is derived from the user's
 3197 | //  actual inputs: sector, geo, bizType, stage, problem length/keywords,
 3198 | //  and the per-dimension live scores from their assessment answers.

 3200 | function offlineAnalysis(fd) {
 3201 | 
 3202 |   // ── 1. RAW INPUTS ─────────────────────────────────────────────
 3203 |   const sc   = fd.sectorCode   || 'OT';
 3204 |   const gc   = fd.geoCode      || 'PI';
 3205 |   const bt   = fd.bizTypeCode  || 'B2B_SME';
 3206 |   const stage= (fd.stage       || '').toLowerCase();

 3208 |   const bizN = fd.bizName       || 'Your Product';
 3209 |   const answers = fd.answers   || {};
 3210 | 
 3211 |   // ── 2. READ PER-DIMENSION LIVE SCORES ─────────────────────────
 3212 |   // Re-derive from DOM the same way calcLive() does so we get
 3213 |   // genuine spread across the 6 dimensions, not just overall.
 3214 |   function readDimScores() {
 3215 |     const dimMap = {
 3216 |       s1:'d1',s2:'d2',s3:'d3',s4:'d4',s5:'d5',s6:'d4',s7:'d2',s8:'d6',
 3217 |       f1:'d1',f2:'d2',f3:'d3',f4:'d4',f5:'d5',f6:'d4',f7:'d2',f8:'d6'
 3218 |     };
 3219 |     const buckets = { d1:[], d2:[], d3:[], d4:[], d5:[], d6:[] };
 3220 | 
 3221 |     document.querySelectorAll('.ai-sel').forEach(el => {
 3222 |       if (!el.value) return;
 3223 |       const v = +(el.value) || 0;
 3224 |       const w = +(el.dataset.w) || 2;
 3225 |       const prefix = el.id.replace(/q\d+$/, '').slice(0, 2);
 3226 |       const dim = dimMap[prefix] || 'd1';
 3227 |       buckets[dim].push({ v, w });
 3228 |     });
 3229 |     document.querySelectorAll('.ai-pills').forEach(grp => {
 3230 |       const on = grp.querySelector('.pill.on');
 3231 |       if (!on) return;
 3232 |       const v = +(on.dataset.val) || 3;
 3233 |       const prefix = (grp.id || '').slice(0, 2);
 3234 |       const dim = dimMap[prefix] || 'd1';
 3235 |       buckets[dim].push({ v, w: 2 });
 3236 |     });
 3237 | 
 3238 |     const score = key => {
 3239 |       const items = buckets[key] || [];
 3240 |       if (!items.length) return null;
 3241 |       const totalW   = items.reduce((s, i) => s + i.w, 0);
 3242 |       const weighted = items.reduce((s, i) => s + i.v * i.w, 0);
 3243 |       return Math.round(((weighted / totalW) - 1) / 4 * 100);
 3244 |     };
 3245 | 
 3246 |     return {
 3247 |       d1: score('d1'), // Market Size
 3248 |       d2: score('d2'), // Audience Quality
 3249 |       d3: score('d3'), // Competition Edge
 3250 |       d4: score('d4'), // Revenue Potential
 3251 |       d5: score('d5'), // Risk Profile
 3252 |       d6: score('d6'), // Sector Fit
 3253 |     };
 3254 |   }
 3255 | 
 3256 |   const dims = readDimScores();
 3257 | 
 3258 |   // Overall score from DOM (already computed by calcLive)
 3259 |   // ✅ REPLACEMENT — compute score from fd.answers directly
 3260 | 
 3261 | // ── SCORE FROM ANSWERS ─────────────────────────────────────────
 3262 | // fd.answers stores option TEXT labels (e.g. "₹500Cr–₹5,000Cr").

 3264 | // using the same lookup table the questions were built with.

 3275 |   'Already paying – validated':5,'Strong intent, not yet paying':4,'Moderate interest':3,'Price-sensitive':2,'Expects free / subsidized':1,
 3276 |   'Same day':5,'<1 month':4,'1–3 months':3,'3–12 months':2,'>12 months':1,
 3277 |   // Section 3 — Competition
 3278 |   'None (Blue Ocean)':5,'1–3 direct competitors':4,'4–10 direct competitors':3,'11–30 direct competitors':2,'30+ direct competitors':1,
 3279 |   'No funded competitors':5,'Bootstrapped only':4,'Series A/B':3,'Series C+ / Growth stage':2,'Listed / MNC / Large Corp':1,
 3280 |   'Proprietary technology / AI / IP':5,'10× lower cost than alternatives':4,'Exclusive distribution / partnerships':4,
 3281 |   'Network effects / data flywheel':5,'Regulatory licence / compliance edge':4,'Similar to competition':2,'No clear moat yet':1,

 3309 |   'Hyper-scalable (software)':5,'High scalability':4,'Moderate scalability':3,'Limited scalability':2,'Linear cost scaling':1,
 3310 |   'High investor interest':5,'Moderate interest':3,'Low interest / niche':2,'Difficult to fund':1,
 3311 |   '>10× ARR (SaaS / AI)':5,'5–10× ARR':4,'3–5× ARR':3,'1–3× Revenue':2,'<1× Revenue':1,
 3312 | };
 3313 | 
 3314 | // Map question ID prefix → dimension bucket
 3315 | const DIM_MAP = {
 3316 |   f1:'d1', f2:'d2', f3:'d3', f4:'d4', f5:'d5', f6:'d4', f7:'d2', f8:'d6',
 3317 |   s1:'d1', s2:'d2', s3:'d3', s4:'d4', s5:'d5', s6:'d4', s7:'d2', s8:'d6',
 3318 | };
 3319 | 
 3320 | const buckets = { d1:[], d2:[], d3:[], d4:[], d5:[], d6:[] };
 3321 | 
 3322 | Object.entries(fd.answers || {}).forEach(([key, val]) => {
 3323 |   const prefix = key.slice(0, 2); // e.g. "f1", "f2", "s3"
 3324 |   const dim = DIM_MAP[prefix];
 3325 |   if (!dim) return;
 3326 | 
 3327 |   const vals = Array.isArray(val) ? val : [val];
 3328 |   vals.forEach(v => {
 3329 |     const score = ANSWER_SCORES[v];
 3330 |     if (score) buckets[dim].push(score);
 3331 |     // checkboxes: each checked item is a moderate signal (no numeric value)
 3332 |     else if (typeof v === 'string' && v.length > 2) buckets[dim].push(4);
 3333 |   });
 3334 | });
 3335 | 
 3336 | const dimAvg = key => {
 3337 |   const items = buckets[key];
 3338 |   if (!items.length) return null;
 3339 |   const avg = items.reduce((a,b)=>a+b,0)/items.length; // 1.0–5.0
 3340 |   const linear = (avg-1)/4*100; // 0–100
 3341 |   // Stretch: floor at 40, push high scores up
 3342 | // Full range: low answers score low, high answers score high
 3343 |   return Math.min(100, Math.max(0, Math.round(linear<25 ? linear*0.8 : linear>75 ? 75+(linear-75)*1.0 : linear)));
 3344 | };
 3345 | 
 3346 | const computedDims = {
 3347 |   d1: dimAvg('d1'), d2: dimAvg('d2'), d3: dimAvg('d3'),
 3348 |   d4: dimAvg('d4'), d5: dimAvg('d5'), d6: dimAvg('d6'),
 3349 | };
 3350 | 
 3351 | // Context bonus from fd fields (sector + bizType + geo + problem length + stage)
 3352 | const probLen2    = (fd.problem || '').length;
 3353 | const probScore2  = probLen2 > 120 ? 5 : probLen2 > 60 ? 3 : probLen2 > 20 ? 1 : 0;
 3354 | const stageIdx2   = ['idea','mvp','pilot','paying','scaling'].findIndex(k => (fd.stage||'').toLowerCase().includes(k));
 3355 | const contextBonus = (fd.sectorCode ? 3 : 0) + (fd.bizTypeCode ? 3 : 0) + (fd.geoCode ? 2 : 0) + probScore2 + Math.min(Math.max(stageIdx2,0), 5);
 3356 | 
 3357 | const answeredDims = [computedDims.d1, computedDims.d2, computedDims.d3, computedDims.d4, computedDims.d5, computedDims.d6].filter(v => v !== null);
 3358 | let t = 0;
 3359 | if (answeredDims.length > 0) {
 3360 |   const weights = [15, 20, 25, 25, 10, 5];
 3361 |   const allD    = [computedDims.d1, computedDims.d2, computedDims.d3, computedDims.d4, computedDims.d5, computedDims.d6];
 3362 |   let wSum = 0, wTotal = 0;
 3363 |   allD.forEach((v, i) => { if (v !== null) { wSum += v * weights[i]; wTotal += weights[i]; } });
 3364 | const bonus = answeredDims.length >= 1 ? Math.round(contextBonus * 0.25) : 0;
 3365 |   t = Math.min(100, Math.round((wSum/wTotal) + bonus));
 3366 | }
 3367 | 
 3368 | // Sync live score panel with the final computed score
 3369 | const lsEl2 = document.getElementById('liveScore');
 3370 | if (lsEl2) lsEl2.textContent = t;
 3371 | 
 3372 | // Also update the liveScore DOM element so it stays in sync
 3373 | // const lsEl2 = document.getElementById('liveScore');
 3374 | // if (lsEl2) lsEl2.textContent = t;
 3375 | 
 3376 |   // ── 3. PROBLEM-STATEMENT SIGNALS ─────────────────────────────
 3377 |   // Extract signals from the problem text to vary TAM / score / insights
 3378 |   const probLen = prob.length;
 3379 | 
 3380 |   // Is this B2B, enterprise-focused, or consumer?
 3381 |   const isEnterprise = /enterprise|corporat|large.?org|fortune|bank|hospital/i.test(prob);
 3382 |   const isB2B        = bt.startsWith('B2B') || isEnterprise;
 3383 |   const isConsumer   = /consumer|retail|individual|student|family|personal/i.test(prob);
 3384 |   const isTech       = /ai|ml|saas|platform|api|automat|software/i.test(prob);
 3385 |   const isDeep       = /research|deep.?tech|biotech|hardware|manufactur/i.test(prob);
 3386 |   const isMarket     = /market|distribution|supply.?chain|logistic/i.test(prob);
 3387 | 
 3388 |   // Problem clarity score (0–10) — longer, specific problems = better
 3389 |   const probClarity  = probLen > 200 ? 10 : probLen > 120 ? 7 : probLen > 60 ? 4 : probLen > 20 ? 2 : 0;
 3390 | 
 3391 |   // ── 4. STAGE MULTIPLIERS ──────────────────────────────────────
 3392 |   // Earlier stage = lower SOM realism, higher risk
 3393 |   const STAGE_IDX = { 'idea':0, 'mvp':1, 'pilot':2, 'paying':3, 'scaling':4 };
 3394 |   const stageIdx  = Object.entries(STAGE_IDX).find(([k]) => stage.includes(k))?.[1] ?? 2;
 3395 |   // SOM reachability rises with stage
 3396 |   const somMult   = [0.015, 0.025, 0.04, 0.06, 0.09][stageIdx];
 3397 |   // Risk is highest at idea stage
 3398 |   const riskBase  = [30, 40, 52, 65, 72][stageIdx];
 3399 | 
 3400 |   // ── 5. GEO MULTIPLIERS ────────────────────────────────────────
 3401 |   const GEO_MULT = { T1:0.22, T2:0.28, PI:0.18, SA:0.35, SE:0.42, MEA:0.55, EU:1.0, NA:1.2, GL:1.0 };
 3402 |   const geoMult  = GEO_MULT[gc] || 0.18;
 3403 |   const isIndia  = ['T1','T2','PI'].includes(gc);
 3404 | 
 3405 |   // ── 6. SECTOR BASE TAM & GROWTH ──────────────────────────────
 3406 |   // Base TAM in ₹Cr (India context) or $M (global)
 3407 |   const SECTOR_DATA = {
 3408 |     IT:  { tam:2800, gr:28, samPct:0.22, compConc:'fragmented' },
 3409 |     HC:  { tam:1400, gr:22, samPct:0.18, compConc:'moderate'   },
 3410 |     FS:  { tam:3500, gr:25, samPct:0.20, compConc:'consolidated'},
 3411 |     EC:  { tam:8000, gr:35, samPct:0.15, compConc:'consolidated'},
 3412 |     ED:  { tam: 650, gr:30, samPct:0.25, compConc:'fragmented' },

 3415 |     LG:  { tam:4500, gr:14, samPct:0.16, compConc:'moderate'   },
 3416 |     ME:  { tam:1200, gr:18, samPct:0.20, compConc:'consolidated'},
 3417 |     AG:  { tam: 900, gr:20, samPct:0.22, compConc:'fragmented' },
 3418 |     EN:  { tam:2200, gr:32, samPct:0.18, compConc:'fragmented' },
 3419 |     OT:  { tam: 500, gr:18, samPct:0.20, compConc:'fragmented' },
 3420 |   };
 3421 | 
 3422 |   const SD   = SECTOR_DATA[sc] || SECTOR_DATA.OT;
 3423 |   const tamC = Math.round(SD.tam * geoMult);
 3424 | 
 3425 |   // Adjust growth rate slightly based on answers (competition edge score)
 3426 |   const grAdjust = dims.d3 !== null ? Math.round((dims.d3 - 50) / 50 * 4) : 0;
 3427 |   const gr       = Math.max(8, SD.gr + grAdjust);
 3428 | 
 3429 |   // SAM: adjusted by problem clarity (specific problem = bigger reachable slice)
 3430 |   const samPctAdj = SD.samPct + probClarity * 0.005;
 3431 |   const samC      = Math.round(tamC * Math.min(samPctAdj, 0.45));
 3432 | 
 3433 |   // SOM: stage-driven + bonus for high revenue-potential score
 3434 |   const revBonus   = dims.d4 !== null ? (dims.d4 - 50) / 50 * 0.015 : 0;
 3435 |   const somC       = Math.round(tamC * Math.max(0.01, somMult + revBonus));
 3436 | 
 3437 |   // Target market share % — driven by stage + score, not just TAM math
 3438 |   const scoreBoost = t >= 70 ? 1.6 : t >= 55 ? 1.3 : t >= 40 ? 1.0 : 0.75;
 3439 |   const stageBoost = [0.7, 0.9, 1.1, 1.4, 1.8][stageIdx] || 1.0;
 3440 |   const tgtPct     = Math.min(25, Math.max(1, Math.round((somC / tamC * 100) * scoreBoost * stageBoost)));
 3441 | 
 3442 |   // ── 7. COMPETITORS (sector + bizType aware) ───────────────────
 3443 |   // Different competitor sets per bizType within sector where relevant
 3444 |   const COMPS = {

 3463 |   // ── 8. COMPETITOR MARKET SHARE SPLIT ─────────────────────────
 3464 |   // Split varies by market concentration + competition-edge score

 3472 |     ? [0.40 + incumbentStrength * 0.08, 0.27, 0.17]
 3473 |     : SD.compConc === 'moderate'

 3483 |   const c2pct     = Math.round(rem2 * spl[2]);

 3569 |   // ── 11. RADAR SCORES ─────────────────────────────────────────
 3570 |   // Our scores derived from actual per-dimension assessment answers.

 3572 |   const radarAxes = ['pricingPower','distribution','brandValue','innovation','marketReach','customerSat'];

 3574 |   // Map dimension scores to radar axes for our product
 3575 |   // d1=MarketSize→marketReach, d2=Audience→customerSat, d3=Competition→brandValue+distribution,
 3576 |   // d4=Revenue→pricingPower, d5=Risk→(inverse)innovation, d6=SectorFit→overall
 3577 |   const safeD = d => d !== null ? d : t; // fall back to overall if dim not answered
 3578 |   const ourR = [
 3579 |     Math.min(100, Math.max(5, safeD(dims.d4) + (isTech ? 8 : 0))),                              // pricingPower

 3585 |   ];
 3586 | 
 3587 |   // Competitor offsets — driven by user's competition-edge score (d3)
 3588 |   // Low competition score = incumbents are stronger vs us
 3589 |   // High competition score = we hold our own, gaps are smaller
 3590 |   const d3Safe      = dims.d3 !== null ? dims.d3 : 50;
 3591 |   const incumbentAdv = Math.round(10 + (100 - d3Safe) * 0.25); // 10–35 range
 3592 |   const midAdv       = Math.round(5  + (100 - d3Safe) * 0.12); // 5–17 range
 3593 |   const innovEdge    = Math.round(8  + (d3Safe / 100) * 14);   // our innovation edge 8–22
 3594 |   const brandGap     = Math.round(12 + (100 - d3Safe) * 0.18); // brand gap 12–30
 3595 |   const distGap      = Math.round(15 + (100 - d3Safe) * 0.20); // distribution gap 15–35
 3596 |   const COMP_OFFSETS = [
 3597 |     // Incumbent: strong distribution & brand, weak on innovation vs us
 3598 |     [+Math.round(incumbentAdv*0.4), +distGap, +brandGap, -innovEdge, +Math.round(incumbentAdv*0.8), +Math.round(incumbentAdv*0.5)],
 3599 |     // Mid-market: moderate across board
 3600 |     [+Math.round(midAdv*0.5), +Math.round(midAdv*0.8), +Math.round(midAdv*0.9), -Math.round(innovEdge*0.5), +Math.round(midAdv*0.6), +Math.round(midAdv*0.4)],
 3601 |     // Emerging: weaker brand & distribution, close on innovation
 3602 |     [-Math.round(midAdv*0.3), -Math.round(midAdv*0.4), -Math.round(midAdv*0.6), +Math.round(innovEdge*0.2), -Math.round(midAdv*0.4), -Math.round(midAdv*0.2)],
 3603 |   ];
