 3613 |   // ── 12. TREND DATA ────────────────────────────────────────────
 3614 |   // Our trend: starts from 0 at stage 1, has a lag proportional to stage
 3615 |   // Competitors: established curves with phase differences per sector
 3616 |   const months   = ['Apr','May','Jun','Jul','Aug','Sep','Oct','Nov','Dec','Jan','Feb','Mar'];
 3617 |   const launchMo = 0;// capped at 2 so line is never invisible
 3618 | 
 3619 |   // ── TREND LINES — fully answer-driven ───────────────────────────────
 3620 |   // Our curve slope: driven by overall score + revenue potential (d4) + stage
 3621 |   // High score = steep growth; low score = flat/slow ramp
 3622 |   const d4Safe      = dims.d4 !== null ? dims.d4 : 50;
 3623 |   const slopeBoost  = (t / 100) * 1.4 + (d4Safe / 100) * 0.6; // 0.0–2.0 range
 3624 |   const curvePower  = t >= 65 ? 1.0 : t >= 45 ? 1.2 : 1.5;    // softer curve — line always visibly rises
 3625 |   const growthRate12 = tgtPct * slopeBoost;
 3626 |  const ourBaseline = Math.max(tgtPct * 0.6, 1.0);
 3627 |   // Competitor trends — driven by competition-edge score (d3)
 3628 |   // High competition score = competitor curves flatter (we're closing gap)
 3629 |   // Low competition score = competitors stable/growing (entrenched)
 3630 |   const c1Base = Math.min(rem * spl[0], 40);
 3631 | const c2Base = Math.min(rem * spl[1], 35);
 3632 | const c3Base = Math.min(rem * spl[2], 30);
 3633 |   // Competition edge: high d3 = incumbent slightly declining, low d3 = incumbent stable/growing
 3634 |   const d3Norm    = (dims.d3 !== null ? dims.d3 : 50) / 100; // 0–1
 3635 |   const c1Growth  = 0.005 + (1 - d3Norm) * 0.008; // low edge = competitors growing faster
 3636 |   const c2Growth  = 0.004 + (1 - d3Norm) * 0.006;
 3637 |   const c3Growth  = 0.003 + (1 - d3Norm) * 0.005;
 3638 |   const c1Decay   = d3Norm > 0.65 ? -0.002 * (d3Norm - 0.65) : 0; // strong edge = top comp slightly losing share
 3639 |   const c2Decay   = d3Norm > 0.65 ? -0.001 * (d3Norm - 0.65) : 0;
 3640 | 
 3641 |   // Phase shift by sector — prevents same-shaped curves across sectors
 3642 |   const PHASE = { IT:0.7, HC:1.1, FS:0.9, EC:1.3, ED:0.8, MF:1.4, RE:0.6, LG:1.0, ME:1.2, AG:0.5, EN:1.5, OT:1.0 };
 3643 |   const ph    = PHASE[sc] || 1.0;
 3644 | 
 3645 |   // Audience quality (d2) drives competitor wobble — fragmented audience = more volatility
 3646 |   const wobble = 0.5 + (1 - (dims.d2 !== null ? dims.d2 : 50) / 100) * 1.5;
 3647 | 
 3648 |   const c1Trend = months.map((_, i) => Math.max(0, +(c1Base * (0.90 + i * c1Growth + i * c1Decay) + Math.sin(i * ph)       * wobble).toFixed(1)));
 3649 |   const c2Trend = months.map((_, i) => Math.max(0, +(c2Base * (0.86 + i * c2Growth + i * c2Decay) + Math.sin(i * ph + 1.5) * wobble * 0.8).toFixed(1)));
 3650 |   const c3Trend = months.map((_, i) => Math.max(0, +(c3Base * (0.82 + i * c3Growth)               + Math.sin(i * ph + 3.0) * wobble * 0.6).toFixed(1)));
 3651 | 
 3652 |   const ourWobble = wobble * 0.6;
 3653 |   const ourTrend = months.map((_, i) => {
 3654 |     const sine = Math.sin(i * ph + 2.1) * ourWobble;
 3655 |     if (i < launchMo) return +Math.max(0, ourBaseline * (0.85 + i * 0.04) + sine * 0.3).toFixed(1);
 3656 |     const progress = (i - launchMo + 1) / (12 - launchMo);
 3657 |     const endTarget = Math.max(tgtPct, ourBaseline * 2.5);
 3658 | const base = ourBaseline + (endTarget - ourBaseline) * Math.pow(progress, 0.65);
 3659 |     return +Math.max(0, base + sine).toFixed(1);
 3660 |   });

 4280 |   // ── HTML end-labels for trend chart — rendered OUTSIDE canvas, never clipped ──
 4281 |   (function renderTrendEndLabels(){
 4282 |     const chart   = dashCharts.trend;
 4283 |     const labels  = document.getElementById('trendEndLabels');
 4284 |     if(!chart||!labels) return;
 4285 | 
 4286 |     function place(){
 4287 |       labels.innerHTML='';
 4288 |       const meta     = chart.getDatasetMeta(0);
 4289 |       if(!meta||!meta.data||!meta.data.length) return;
 4290 | 
 4291 |       const chartArea = chart.chartArea;
 4292 |       const totalH    = chart.height;
 4293 |       const lastIdx   = chart.data.labels.length - 1;
 4294 | 
 4295 |       // Collect {y, color, label, value} for all visible series
 4296 |       const items = chart.data.datasets.map((ds,i)=>{
 4297 |         const m = chart.getDatasetMeta(i);
 4298 |         if(m.hidden) return null;
 4299 |         const pt = m.data[lastIdx];
 4300 |         if(!pt) return null;
 4301 |         const rawY = pt.y;                          // pixel Y relative to canvas
 4302 |         const val  = ds.data[lastIdx];
 4303 |         return { y: rawY, color: ds.borderColor, label: ds.label, val };
 4304 |       }).filter(Boolean);
 4305 | 
 4306 |       if(!items.length) return;
 4307 | 
 4308 |       // Sort by Y descending (top of chart = lowest y pixel)
 4309 |       items.sort((a,b)=>a.y - b.y);
 4310 | 
 4311 |       // Anti-overlap: push labels apart if they are closer than minGap px
 4312 |       const minGap = 20;
 4313 |       for(let pass=0; pass<8; pass++){
 4314 |         for(let i=1;i<items.length;i++){
 4315 |           const gap = items[i].y - items[i-1].y;
 4316 |           if(gap < minGap){
 4317 |             const push = (minGap - gap) / 2;
 4318 |             items[i-1].y -= push;
 4319 |             items[i].y   += push;
 4320 |           }
 4321 |         }
 4322 |       }
 4323 | 
 4324 |       // Clamp so labels don't go above chart area top or below chart area bottom
 4325 |       const top    = chartArea ? chartArea.top    : 10;
 4326 |       const bottom = chartArea ? chartArea.bottom : totalH - 30;
 4327 |       items.forEach(item=>{
 4328 |         item.y = Math.max(top + 8, Math.min(bottom - 8, item.y));
 4329 |       });
 4330 | 
 4331 |       // Render each label as an absolutely-positioned HTML element
 4332 |       items.forEach(item=>{
 4333 |         // Truncate name to 10 chars max
 4334 |         const name = item.label.length > 10 ? item.label.slice(0,10)+'…' : item.label;
 4335 |         const valStr = (+(item.val||0)).toFixed(1)+'%';
 4336 | 
 4337 |         const el = document.createElement('div');
 4338 |         el.className = 'tel';
 4339 |         el.style.top = item.y + 'px';
 4340 |         el.innerHTML =
 4341 |           '<span class="tel-dot" style="background:'+item.color+';box-shadow:0 0 0 2px '+item.color+'33"></span>'+
 4342 |           '<span class="tel-txt" style="color:'+item.color+';border-color:'+item.color+'44">'+
 4343 |             name+'&nbsp;<strong>'+valStr+'</strong>'+
 4344 |           '</span>';
 4345 |         labels.appendChild(el);
 4346 |       });
 4347 |     }
 4348 | 
 4349 |     // Place immediately after render, and on every resize
 4350 |     chart.options.animation.onComplete = place;
 4351 |     chart.options.onResize = ()=>setTimeout(place,50);
 4352 |     // Also place after a short delay in case animation hasn't fired yet
 4353 |     setTimeout(place, 800);
 4354 |   })();

 4503 |   function renderMap(world){
 4504 |     const wrap=document.getElementById('mapWrap');
 4505 |     const tip=document.getElementById('mapTT');
 4506 |     const W=wrap.offsetWidth,H=wrap.offsetHeight;
 4507 |     if(W<50||H<30){setTimeout(()=>renderMap(world),150);return;}
 4508 |     const svgEl=document.getElementById('worldMap');
 4509 |     svgEl.setAttribute('width',W);svgEl.setAttribute('height',H);
 4510 |     svgEl.setAttribute('viewBox',`0 0 ${W} ${H}`);
 4511 |     svgEl.style.width=W+'px';svgEl.style.height=H+'px';
 4512 |     const svg=d3.select(svgEl);svg.selectAll('*').remove();
 4513 |     const proj=d3.geoEquirectangular().fitSize([W,H],{type:'Sphere'});
 4514 |     const pathFn=d3.geoPath().projection(proj);
 4515 |     const countries=topojson.feature(world,world.objects.countries);
 4516 |     const borders=topojson.mesh(world,world.objects.countries,(a,b)=>a!==b);
 4517 |     // Dark ocean
 4518 |     svg.append('rect').attr('width',W).attr('height',H).attr('fill','#bfdbfe');
 4519 |     svg.append('path').datum(d3.geoGraticule().step([30,30])()).attr('d',pathFn).attr('fill','none').attr('stroke','rgba(26,86,219,0.3)').attr('stroke-width','0.4');
 4520 |     svg.selectAll('.ctry').data(countries.features).join('path').attr('class','ctry').attr('d',pathFn)
 4521 |       .attr('fill',d=>{

 4523 |         if(!r)return '#c7d9f5';

 4529 |       .attr('opacity',d=>{const r=getRegion(d.id);return r&&RDATA_D[r]?.zero?0.5:1;})
 4530 |       .on('mouseover',function(ev,d){

 4535 |         tip.style.opacity='1';
 4536 |         svg.selectAll('.ctry').style('opacity',e=>getRegion(e.id)===r?1:0.35);
 4537 |         d3.select(this).attr('stroke','rgba(99,231,183,0.4)').attr('stroke-width','1');
 4538 |       })
 4539 |       .on('mousemove',function(ev){
 4540 |         const rc=wrap.getBoundingClientRect();
 4541 |         let x=ev.clientX-rc.left+12,y=ev.clientY-rc.top-38;
 4542 |         if(x+240>W)x-=252;if(y<4)y=4;

 4544 |       })

 4546 |         tip.style.opacity='0';
 4547 |         svg.selectAll('.ctry').style('opacity',1);
 4548 |         d3.select(this).attr('stroke','rgba(6,18,40,0.4)').attr('stroke-width','0.3');
 4549 |       })
 4550 |       .on('click',function(ev,d){
 4551 |         // India drill-down on click (country id 356)

 4553 |         else{const r=getRegion(d.id);if(r)openPop('geomap');}
 4554 |       });
 4555 |     svg.append('path').datum(borders).attr('d',pathFn).attr('fill','none').attr('stroke','rgba(6,18,40,0.5)').attr('stroke-width','0.25');
 4556 |

 4699 | // Receive: render dashboard with analysis result from React
 4700 | window.addEventListener('message', function(event) {
 4701 |   if (!event.data) return;
 4702 | 
 4703 |   if (event.data.type === 'INFOPACE_RENDER') {
 4704 |     clearTimeout(window._renderFallbackTimer);
 4705 |     const { fd, analysis } = event.data;
 4706 |     if (!fd) return;
 4707 |     // null analysis = Gemini failed, use offline fallback
 4708 |     const finalAnalysis = (analysis && typeof analysis === 'object' && Object.keys(analysis).length > 0)
 4709 |       ? analysis : offlineAnalysis(fd);
 4710 |     const assess = document.getElementById('assessShell');
 4711 |     const loader  = document.getElementById('loaderShell');
 4712 |     if (assess) assess.style.display = 'none';
 4713 |     if (loader)  loader.style.display = 'none';
 4714 |     renderDash(fd, finalAnalysis);
 4715 |     if (window.parent && window.parent !== window) {
 4716 |       window.parent.postMessage({ type: 'INFOPACE_READY' }, '*');
 4717 |     }
 4718 |   }
 4719 | 
 4720 |   // Receive: pre-fill user details from React onboarding into the form
 4721 |   if (event.data.type === 'INFOPACE_PREFILL') {
 4722 |     const u = event.data.userData;
 4723 |     if (!u) return;
 4724 |     // Business name = organization
 4725 |     const bn = document.getElementById('bizName');
 4726 |     if (bn) bn.value = u.organization || '';
 4727 | 
 4728 |     // Sector — match by value
 4729 |     const sec = document.getElementById('sector');
 4730 |     if (sec && u.sectorCode) sec.value = u.sectorCode;
 4731 | 
 4732 |     // Business type — map role to closest bizType
 4733 |     const bt = document.getElementById('bizType');
 4734 |     if (bt && u.bizTypeCode) bt.value = u.bizTypeCode;
 4735 | 
 4736 |     // Geography
 4737 |     const geo = document.getElementById('geo');
 4738 |     if (geo && u.geoCode) geo.value = u.geoCode;
 4739 | 
 4740 |     // Problem
 4741 |     const prob = document.getElementById('problem');
 4742 |     if (prob) prob.value = u.problem || '';
 4743 | 
 4744 |     const probLen = (u.problem||'').trim().length;
 4745 | const counter = document.getElementById('probCounter');
 4746 | if (counter) { counter.textContent = probLen + ' / 20'; counter.style.color = probLen >= 20 ? '#059669' : '#94a3b8'; }
 4747 | 
 4748 |     // Stage pill
 4749 |     if (u.stage) {
 4750 |       const pill = document.querySelector(`#stagePills .pill[data-val="${u.stage}"]`);
 4751 |       if (pill) pickPill(pill, 'stagePills');
 4752 |     }
 4753 | 
 4754 |     // Trigger live score refresh
 4755 |     onCtxChange();
 4756 |     updateGeoPreview();
 4757 |     calcLive();
 4758 |   }

 4765 |     const fd = collectData();

 4771 |       const loader = document.getElementById('loaderShell');
 4772 |       if (loader && loader.style.display !== 'none') {
 4773 |         console.warn('INFOPACE_RENDER not received — falling back to offline analysis');
 4774 |         renderDash(fd, offlineAnalysis(fd));
 4775 |       }
 4776 |     }, 12000);
 4777 |   } else {
 4778 |     await _originalBuildDashboard();
 4779 |   }
 4780 | };

 4808 | /* ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════

 4811 | function switchView(v){
 4812 |   const isCharts=v==='charts';
 4813 |   const vc=document.getElementById('viewCharts');
 4814 |   const vr=document.getElementById('viewReport');
 4815 |   if(vc){ vc.style.display=isCharts?'flex':'none'; }
 4816 |   if(vr&&isCharts){ vr.style.display='none'; }
 4817 |   // Show paywall when switching to report view

 4895 |     function scoreGaugeSVG(score,W,H){
 4896 |       const cx=W/2,cy=88,R=68,sw=13;
 4897 |       const pct=Math.max(0,Math.min(100,score))/100;
 4898 |       const arcColor=score>=70?'#10B981':score>=50?'#f59e0b':'#ef4444';
 4899 |       const gradId='g'+Math.random().toString(36).slice(2,6);
 4900 |       const sx=cx-R,sy=cy,ex=cx+R,ey=cy;
 4901 |       const angle=Math.PI-pct*Math.PI;
 4902 |       const scX=cx+R*Math.cos(angle),scY=cy-R*Math.sin(angle);
 4903 |       const lg=pct>0.5?1:0;
 4904 |       return `<svg width="${W}" height="118" viewBox="0 0 ${W} 118" style="display:block;overflow:visible;">
 4905 |         <defs><linearGradient id="${gradId}" x1="0%" y1="0%" x2="100%" y2="0%">
 4906 |           <stop offset="0%" stop-color="${arcColor}" stop-opacity="0.4"/>
 4907 |           <stop offset="100%" stop-color="${arcColor}"/>
 4908 |         </linearGradient></defs>
 4909 |         <path d="M${sx},${sy} A${R},${R} 0 0,1 ${ex},${ey}" fill="none" stroke="rgba(255,255,255,0.1)" stroke-width="${sw}" stroke-linecap="round"/>
 4910 |         <path d="M${sx},${sy} A${R},${R} 0 ${lg},1 ${scX},${scY}" fill="none" stroke="url(#${gradId})" stroke-width="${sw}" stroke-linecap="round"/>
 4911 |         <text x="${sx-4}" y="${sy+16}" text-anchor="end" font-size="9" fill="rgba(255,255,255,0.3)" font-family="'IBM Plex Mono',monospace">0</text>
 4912 |         <text x="${ex+4}" y="${ey+16}" text-anchor="start" font-size="9" fill="rgba(255,255,255,0.3)" font-family="'IBM Plex Mono',monospace">100</text>
 4913 |         <line x1="${cx}" y1="${cy-R-sw/2-2}" x2="${cx}" y2="${cy-R+sw/2+2}" stroke="rgba(255,255,255,0.2)" stroke-width="1.5"/>
 4914 |         <text x="${cx}" y="${cy-R-sw/2-6}" text-anchor="middle" font-size="8" fill="rgba(255,255,255,0.2)" font-family="'IBM Plex Mono',monospace">50</text>
 4915 |         <line x1="${cx}" y1="${cy}" x2="${scX}" y2="${scY}" stroke="rgba(255,255,255,0.7)" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round"/>
 4916 |         <circle cx="${cx}" cy="${cy}" r="5" fill="rgba(255,255,255,0.15)" stroke="rgba(255,255,255,0.4)" stroke-width="1"/>
 4917 |         <circle cx="${cx}" cy="${cy}" r="2.5" fill="rgba(255,255,255,0.8)"/>
 4918 |         <text x="${cx}" y="${cy-22}" text-anchor="middle" font-family="'IBM Plex Mono',monospace" font-size="34" font-weight="700" fill="${arcColor}">${score}</text>
 4919 |         <text x="${cx}" y="${cy-38}" text-anchor="middle" font-family="'Inter',sans-serif" font-size="8.5" fill="rgba(255,255,255,0.35)" letter-spacing=".12em">OUT OF 100</text>
 4920 |       </svg>`;
 4921 |     }

 4923 |     function funnelSVG(){
 4924 |       const tam=+(a.tamCrore)||100,sam=+(a.samCrore)||30,som=+(a.somCrore)||5;
 4925 |       const fmtV=v=>v>=1000?'₹'+(v/1000).toFixed(1)+'K Cr':'₹'+Math.round(v)+'Cr';
 4926 |       const SVG_W=480,FW=200,LX=224,SEG=64,GAP=4,SVG_H=SEG*3+GAP*2+12;
 4927 |       const steps=[
 4928 |         {v:tam,l:'TAM',pct:100,c:'#1144a0',title:'Total Addressable Market',desc:'The entire market demand for your product category in the target geography.',tw:FW,bw:Math.round(FW*0.68)},
 4929 |         {v:sam,l:'SAM',pct:Math.round(sam/tam*100),c:'#3b82f6',title:'Serviceable Available Market',desc:'The segment you can realistically reach with your current model and channels.',tw:Math.round(FW*0.68),bw:Math.round(FW*0.38)},
 4930 |         {v:som,l:'SOM',pct:Math.round(som/tam*100),c:'#059669',title:'3-Year Revenue Target',desc:'Your realistic capture target — typically 2-8% of SAM at early stage.',tw:Math.round(FW*0.38),bw:Math.round(FW*0.16)}
 4931 |       ];
 4932 |       const parts=steps.map((s,i)=>{
 4933 |         const y=6+i*(SEG+GAP),cx=FW/2;
 4934 |         const tlx=cx-s.tw/2,trx=cx+s.tw/2,blx=cx-s.bw/2,brx=cx+s.bw/2;
 4935 |         const path=`M${tlx},${y} L${trx},${y} L${brx},${y+SEG} L${blx},${y+SEG} Z`;
 4936 |         const my=y+SEG/2,midRightX=(trx+brx)/2,dotX=midRightX+4,lmy=my;
 4937 |         const labelLines=s.desc.match(/.{1,44}(\s|$)/g)||[s.desc];
 4938 |         const innerLabel=s.tw>60?`${s.l} · ${s.pct}% of TAM`:s.l;
 4939 |         const innerFontSize=s.tw>80?9:8;
 4940 |         return `<path d="${path}" fill="${s.c}" opacity="0.85"/>
 4941 |           <path d="${path}" fill="none" stroke="rgba(255,255,255,0.3)" stroke-width="1.2"/>
 4942 |           <text x="${cx}" y="${my-7}" text-anchor="middle" font-family="'IBM Plex Mono',monospace" font-size="${i===2?12:15}" font-weight="700" fill="#fff">${fmtV(s.v)}</text>
 4943 |           <text x="${cx}" y="${my+8}" text-anchor="middle" font-family="'Inter',sans-serif" font-size="${innerFontSize}" fill="rgba(255,255,255,0.85)">${innerLabel}</text>
 4944 |           <circle cx="${dotX}" cy="${lmy}" r="4" fill="${s.c}"/>
 4945 |           <line x1="${dotX+4}" y1="${lmy}" x2="${LX-4}" y2="${lmy}" stroke="${s.c}" stroke-width="1.5" stroke-dasharray="3,2"/>
 4946 |           <text x="${LX}" y="${lmy-14}" font-family="'Inter',sans-serif" font-size="10" font-weight="700" fill="${s.c}">${s.title}</text>
 4947 |           ${labelLines.slice(0,2).map((ln,li)=>`<text x="${LX}" y="${lmy+li*12}" font-family="'Inter',sans-serif" font-size="8.5" fill="#6080a0">${ln.trim()}</text>`).join('')}`;
 4948 |       }).join('');
 4949 |       const dividers=[1,2].map(i=>{
 4950 |         const y=6+i*(SEG+GAP)-GAP;
 4951 |         return `<line x1="2" y1="${y}" x2="${FW-2}" y2="${y}" stroke="rgba(255,255,255,0.2)" stroke-width="1"/>`;
 4952 |       }).join('');
 4953 |       return `<svg width="${SVG_W}" height="${SVG_H}" viewBox="0 0 ${SVG_W} ${SVG_H}" style="display:block;width:100%;max-width:${SVG_W}px;overflow:visible;">${parts}${dividers}</svg>`;
 4954 |     }

 4956 |     function donutSVG(data,W,cx,cy,OR,IR){
 4957 |       const tot=data.reduce((s,d)=>s+(+d.v||0),0)||100;
 4958 |       let ang=-Math.PI/2;
 4959 |       return data.map((d,i)=>{
 4960 |         const sw=(+d.v||0)/tot*2*Math.PI;
 4961 |         if(sw<0.02){ang+=sw;return '';}
 4962 |         const x1=cx+OR*Math.cos(ang),y1=cy+OR*Math.sin(ang);
 4963 |         const x2=cx+OR*Math.cos(ang+sw),y2=cy+OR*Math.sin(ang+sw);
 4964 |         const x3=cx+IR*Math.cos(ang+sw),y3=cy+IR*Math.sin(ang+sw);
 4965 |         const x4=cx+IR*Math.cos(ang),y4=cy+IR*Math.sin(ang);
 4966 |         const lg=sw>Math.PI?1:0;
 4967 |         const mx=cx+(OR+IR)/2*Math.cos(ang+sw/2),my=cy+(OR+IR)/2*Math.sin(ang+sw/2);
 4968 |         const pct=Math.round((+d.v||0)/tot*100);
 4969 |         const lbl2=pct>=6?`<text x="${mx}" y="${my+3.5}" text-anchor="middle" font-size="9" font-weight="700" fill="rgba(255,255,255,.95)" font-family="'IBM Plex Mono',monospace">${pct}%</text>`:'';
 4970 |         ang+=sw;
 4971 |         return `<path d="M${x1},${y1} A${OR},${OR} 0 ${lg},1 ${x2},${y2} L${x3},${y3} A${IR},${IR} 0 ${lg},0 ${x4},${y4} Z" fill="${d.c}" stroke="#fff" stroke-width="1.5"/>${lbl2}`;
 4972 |       }).join('');
 4973 |     }

 5570 | function submitReportEmail() {
 5571 |   var email = (document.getElementById('rptEmailInput').value || '').trim();
 5572 |   var errEl = document.getElementById('rptEmailErr');
 5573 | 
 5574 |   if (!email || !/^[^\s@]+@[^\s@]+\.[^\s@]+$/.test(email)) {
 5575 |     errEl.textContent = 'Please enter a valid email address.';
 5576 |     errEl.style.display = 'block';
 5577 |     return;
 5578 |   }
 5579 |   errEl.style.display = 'none';
 5580 | 
 5581 |   if (!dd || !dd.a) {
 5582 |     errEl.textContent = 'Please complete the assessment first to generate your report.';
 5583 |     errEl.style.display = 'block';
 5584 |     // Auto-redirect to assessment after 1.5 seconds
 5585 |     setTimeout(function(){ 
 5586 |         if(typeof switchView === 'function') switchView('assess');
 5587 |     }, 1500);
 5588 |     return;
 5589 | }

 5593 |   document.getElementById('rptLoadingState').style.display = 'block';

 5609 |     growthRate:         a.growthRate,
 5610 |     dimensions:         a.dimensions,
 5611 |     dimensionExplanations: a.dimensionExplanations,

 5613 |     stageContext:       a.stageContext,
 5614 |     sectorBrutalTruth:  a.sectorBrutalTruth,
 5615 |     investorReadiness:  a.investorReadiness,

 5619 |     competitorProfiles: a.competitorProfiles,
 5620 |     riskMitigations:    a.riskMitigations,
 5621 |     recommendations:    a.recommendations,
 5622 |   };
 5623 | 
 5624 |   fetch('/api/send-report', {
 5625 |     method:  'POST',
 5626 |     headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
 5627 |     body:    JSON.stringify(payload)
 5628 |   })
 5629 |   .then(function(r) { return r.json(); })
 5630 |   .then(function(data) {
 5631 |     document.getElementById('rptLoadingState').style.display = 'none';
 5632 |     if (data.ok) {
 5633 |       document.getElementById('rptSentTo').textContent = 'Sent to ' + email;
 5634 |       document.getElementById('rptSuccessState').style.display = 'block';
 5635 |     } else {
 5636 |       document.getElementById('rptInputState').style.display = 'block';
 5637 |       errEl.textContent = data.error || 'Something went wrong. Please try again.';
 5638 |       errEl.style.display = 'block';
 5639 |     }
 5640 |   })
 5641 |   .catch(function() {
 5642 |     document.getElementById('rptLoadingState').style.display = 'none';
 5643 |     document.getElementById('rptInputState').style.display   = 'block';
 5644 |     errEl.textContent = 'Network error — is server.js running?';
 5645 |     errEl.style.display = 'block';
 5646 |   });
 5647 | }
 5648 | </script>
 5649 | </body>
 5650 | </html>

  219 |   function detectZoom() {
  220 |     const originalWidth = window.outerWidth;
  221 |     const currentWidth = window.innerWidth;
  222 |     const ratio = originalWidth / currentWidth;
  223 |     
  224 |     // Alternative method: check device pixel ratio and page zoom
  225 |     const dpr = window.devicePixelRatio || 1;
  226 |     
  227 |     // More reliable method: use getBoundingClientRect
  228 |     const div = document.createElement('div');
  229 |     div.style.width = '100px';
  230 |     document.body.appendChild(div);
  231 |     const boxWidth = div.getBoundingClientRect().width;
  232 |     document.body.removeChild(div);
  233 |     
  234 |     currentZoom = 100 / boxWidth;
  235 |     document.documentElement.style.setProperty('--current-zoom', currentZoom);
  236 |   }

  255 |   async function loadSubmissions() {

  257 |       .from("submissions")

  295 |       html += '    <div class="info">';
  296 |       html += '      <span class="name">' + (r.name || "—") + '</span>';
  297 |       html += '      <span class="org">' + (r.organization || "—") + '</span>';
  298 |       html += '      <span class="email">' + (r.email || "") + '</span>';
  299 |       html += '      <span class="date">' + date + scoreInfo + '</span>';
  300 |       html += '    </div>';
  301 |       html += '    ' + statusBadge;
  302 |       html += '  </div>';
  303 |

  343 |   function downloadImg(id, name) {
  344 |     const imgs = document.querySelectorAll(".card-body img");

  352 |       }

📄 FILE #12: README.md
----------------------------------------------------------------------
    1 | # Infopace — React + Supabase Edition
    2 | 
    3 | > AI-powered market intelligence assessment platform.
    4 | > Built with React + Vite + Tailwind CSS + Gemini AI + Supabase.
    5 | 
    6 | ---
    7 | 
    8 | ## What This App Does
    9 | 
   10 | 1. **Onboarding Form** — Collects user details (name, email, phone, organization, role, website, LinkedIn, team size, sector, geography, problem statement, stage)
   11 | 2. **AI Assessment** — Generates 8 tailored question groups using Gemini AI, with a live market score panel updating as you answer
   12 | 3. **Results Dashboard** — Full market intelligence dashboard with:
   13 |    - Score donut + dimension bars + capability radar
   14 |    - Revenue projection chart (conservative / base / optimistic)
   15 |    - TAM / SAM / SOM estimates
   16 |    - Competitor analysis
   17 |    - Key AI-generated insights
   18 |    - 90-day action plan
   19 |    - Full printable report view
   20 |    - Raw JSON data view
   21 | 4. **Supabase Storage** — Every submission (user details + all answers + full analysis) is saved to your Supabase database
   22 | 
   23 | ---
   24 | 
   25 | ## Prerequisites
   26 | 
   27 | - Node.js 18+
   28 | - A free [Gemini API key](https://aistudio.google.com) (already in `server.js`)
   29 | - A free [Supabase](https://supabase.com) project
   30 | 
   31 | ---
   32 | 
   33 | ## Quick Start
   34 | 
   35 | ### Step 1 — Set up Supabase
   36 | 
   37 | 1. Create a free project at [supabase.com](https://supabase.com)
   38 | 2. Go to **SQL Editor** and paste + run the contents of `supabase_setup.sql`
   39 | 3. Go to **Settings → API** and copy:
   40 |    - **Project URL** (looks like `https://xxxx.supabase.co`)
   41 |    - **anon / public key** (long JWT string)
   42 | 
   43 | ### Step 2 — Configure environment
   44 | 
   45 | ```bash
   46 | cp .env.example .env
   47 | ```
   48 | 
   49 | Edit `.env` and fill in your values:
   50 | 
   51 | ```env
   52 | VITE_SUPABASE_URL=https://YOUR_PROJECT_ID.supabase.co
   53 | VITE_SUPABASE_ANON_KEY=YOUR_ANON_PUBLIC_KEY
   54 | ```
   55 | 
   56 | ### Step 3 — Install dependencies
   57 | 
   58 | ```bash
   59 | npm install
   60 | ```
   61 | 
   62 | ### Step 4 — Run the app (two terminals)
   63 | 
   64 | **Terminal 1** — Start the Gemini proxy server (port 4000):
   65 | ```bash
   66 | node server.js
   67 | ```
   68 | 
   69 | **Terminal 2** — Start the React dev server (port 3000):
   70 | ```bash
   71 | npm run dev
   72 | ```
   73 | 
   74 | Open **http://localhost:3000**
   75 | 
   76 | The Vite dev server automatically proxies `/api` requests to `server.js` on port 4000.
   77 | 
   78 | ---
   79 | 
   80 | ## Project Structure
   81 | 
   82 | ```
   83 | infopace-react/
   84 | ├── server.js                    ← Gemini AI proxy (Node.js, port 4000)
   85 | ├── supabase_setup.sql           ← Run once in Supabase SQL Editor
   86 | ├── .env.example                 ← Copy to .env and fill in keys
   87 | │
   88 | ├── index.html                   ← Vite entry HTML
   89 | ├── vite.config.js               ← Dev server + /api proxy config
   90 | ├── tailwind.config.js
   91 | ├── postcss.config.js
   92 | ├── package.json
   93 | │
   94 | └── src/
   95 |     ├── main.jsx                 ← React entry point
   96 |     ├── App.jsx                  ← Screen router (onboarding → assessment → results)
   97 |     ├── index.css                ← Tailwind + IBM Plex fonts
   98 |     │
   99 |     ├── pages/
  100 |     │   ├── OnboardingForm.jsx   ← Step 1: User & venture details
  101 |     │   ├── AssessmentShell.jsx  ← Step 2: AI questions + live scoring
  102 |     │   └── ResultsDashboard.jsx ← Step 3: Full dashboard + report
  103 |     │
  104 |     └── lib/
  105 |         ├── supabase.js          ← Supabase client init
  106 |         ├── gemini.js            ← Gemini API helpers (questions + analysis)
  107 |         └── db.js                ← Save / load submissions
  108 | ```
  109 | 
  110 | ---
  111 | 
  112 | ## Data Saved to Supabase
  113 | 
  114 | Every completed assessment saves one row to the `submissions` table:
  115 | 
  116 | | Column | Type | Description |
  117 | |---|---|---|
  118 | | `id` | uuid | Auto-generated primary key |
  119 | | `name` | text | Full name |
  120 | | `email` | text | Email address |
  121 | | `phone` | text | Phone number |
  122 | | `organization` | text | Company name |
  123 | | `role` | text | Job role |
  124 | | `website` | text | Website URL |
  125 | | `linkedin` | text | LinkedIn URL |
  126 | | `team_size` | text | Team size bracket |
  127 | | `sector` | text | e.g. "HealthTech", "B2B SaaS" |
  128 | | `geography` | text | e.g. "PI" (Pan India), "GL" (Global) |
  129 | | `problem` | text | Problem statement |
  130 | | `stage` | text | Business stage (1–5) |
  131 | | `answers` | jsonb | All question answers keyed by question ID |
  132 | | `overall_score` | integer | Final market score (0–100) |
  133 | | `grade` | text | e.g. "A", "B+", "C" |
  134 | | `dimensions` | jsonb | Six dimension scores |
  135 | | `analysis_json` | jsonb | Complete AI analysis (TAM/SAM/SOM, competitors, insights, action plan, projections) |
  136 | | `created_at` | timestamptz | Submission timestamp |
  137 | 
  138 | ---
  139 | 
  140 | ## Production Deployment
  141 | 
  142 | ### Build the React app
  143 | 
  144 | ```bash
  145 | npm run build
  146 | ```
  147 | 
  148 | This creates a `dist/` folder.
  149 | 
  150 | ### Serve with server.js
  151 | 
  152 | Update `server.js` to serve the `dist/` folder as static files. Replace the static file section at the bottom of `server.js` with:
  153 | 
  154 | ```javascript
  155 | // Serve React build
  156 | let fp = req.url === '/' ? '/index.html' : req.url.split('?')[0];
  157 | 
  158 | // For React Router — serve index.html for unknown routes
  159 | const fullPath = path.join(process.cwd(), 'dist', fp);
  160 | fs.readFile(fullPath, (err, data) => {
  161 |   if (err) {
  162 |     // Fallback to index.html for client-side routing
  163 |     fs.readFile(path.join(process.cwd(), 'dist', 'index.html'), (e2, d2) => {
  164 |       if (e2) { res.writeHead(404); res.end('Not found'); return; }
  165 |       res.writeHead(200, { 'Content-Type': 'text/html' });
  166 |       res.end(d2);
  167 |     });
  168 |     return;
  169 |   }
  170 |   res.writeHead(200, { 'Content-Type': MIME[path.extname(fullPath)] || 'text/plain' });
  171 |   res.end(data);
  172 | });
  173 | ```
  174 | 
  175 | Then run just `node server.js` — it serves both the API and the React app on port 4000.
  176 | 
  177 | ### Deploy options
  178 | 
  179 | - **Railway / Render / Fly.io** — push repo, set env vars, run `node server.js`
  180 | - **Vercel** — deploy React app, add serverless function wrapping Gemini calls
  181 | - **VPS** — clone repo, `npm run build`, run with `pm2 start server.js`
  182 | 
  183 | ---
  184 | 
  185 | ## Customisation
  186 | 
  187 | ### Change sectors / geographies
  188 | Edit the `SECTORS` and `GEO` arrays at the top of `src/pages/OnboardingForm.jsx`.
  189 | 
  190 | ### Change AI models
  191 | Edit `MODEL_FAST` and `MODEL_SMART` constants in `server.js`.
  192 | 
  193 | ### Change question count
  194 | Edit the prompt in `src/lib/gemini.js` → `generateQuestions()`.
  195 | 
  196 | ### Add email notifications
  197 | After `saveSubmission()` in `AssessmentShell.jsx`, call a Supabase Edge Function or a service like Resend/SendGrid.
  198 | 
  199 | ---
  200 | 
  201 | ## Troubleshooting
  202 | 
  203 | | Problem | Fix |
  204 | |---|---|
  205 | | `/api` returns 500 | Check Gemini API key on line 8 of `server.js` |
  206 | | Supabase save fails | Verify `.env` values and that `supabase_setup.sql` was run |
  207 | | Questions don't load | Gemini API key may be rate-limited; fallback questions will show |
  208 | | Blank dashboard | Open browser console — look for JSON parse errors in analysis response |
  209 | 
  210 | ---

   43 | // ── Gmail SMTP transporter ───────────────────────────────────────
   44 | function createTransporter() {
   45 |   return nodemailer.createTransport({
   46 |     host:              'smtp.gmail.com',
   47 |     port:              587,
   48 |     secure:            false,
   49 |     requireTLS:        true,
   50 |     family:            4,
   51 |     connectionTimeout: 10000,
   52 |     greetingTimeout:   10000,
   53 |     socketTimeout:     15000,
   54 |     tls: { rejectUnauthorized: false },
   55 |     auth: {
   56 |       user: GMAIL_USER,
   57 |       pass: GMAIL_APP_PASSWORD,
   58 |     },
   59 |   });
   60 | }

   62 | // ── Gemini request helper ────────────────────────────────────────
   63 | function geminiRequest(apiKey, model, maxTokens, promptText, callback) {
   64 |   const payload = JSON.stringify({
   65 |     contents: [{ parts: [{ text: promptText }] }],
   66 |     generationConfig: {
   67 |       temperature:      0.7,
   68 |       maxOutputTokens:  maxTokens,
   69 |       responseMimeType: 'text/plain'
   70 |     }
   71 |   });
   72 |   const options = {
   73 |     hostname: 'generativelanguage.googleapis.com',
   74 |     path:     '/v1beta/models/' + model + ':generateContent?key=' + apiKey,
   75 |     method:   'POST',
   76 |     headers: {
   77 |       'Content-Type':   'application/json',
   78 |       'Content-Length': Buffer.byteLength(payload)
   79 |     }
   80 |   };
   81 |   const req = https.request(options, res => {
   82 |     let body = '';
   83 |     res.on('data', c => body += c);
   84 |     res.on('end', () => callback(null, res.statusCode, body));
   85 |   });
   86 |   req.on('error', e => callback(e, null, null));
   87 |   req.write(payload);
   88 |   req.end();
   89 | }
   90 |

  365 | // ── HTTP Server ──────────────────────────────────────────────────
  366 | http.createServer(function(req, res) {
  367 |   res.setHeader('Access-Control-Allow-Origin',  '*');
  368 |   res.setHeader('Access-Control-Allow-Methods', 'GET, POST, OPTIONS');
  369 |   res.setHeader('Access-Control-Allow-Headers', 'Content-Type');
  370 |   if (req.method === 'OPTIONS') { res.writeHead(204); res.end(); return; }
  371 | 
  372 |   // ── /api → Gemini proxy ────────────────────────────────────────
  373 |   if (req.url === '/api' && req.method === 'POST') {
  374 |     var body = '';
  375 |     req.on('data', function(c){ body += c; });
  376 |     req.on('end', function() {
  377 |       var payload;
  378 |       try { payload = JSON.parse(body); }
  379 |       catch(e) { res.writeHead(400); res.end('bad json'); return; }
  380 | 
  381 |       var type        = payload._type || 'analysis';
  382 |       var isQuestions = type === 'questions';
  383 |       var apiKey      = isQuestions ? API_KEY_QUESTIONS : API_KEY_ANALYSIS;
  384 |       var model       = isQuestions ? MODEL_QUESTIONS   : MODEL_ANALYSIS;
  385 |       var maxTokens   = isQuestions ? TOKENS_QUESTIONS  : TOKENS_ANALYSIS;
  386 |       var label       = isQuestions ? 'questions'       : 'analysis';
  387 | 
  388 |       // No key → return 503 so client falls back gracefully
  389 |       if (!apiKey) {
  390 |         console.log('  ⚠️  ' + label + ' key not set — client will use built-in fallback');
  391 |         res.writeHead(503, { 'Content-Type':'application/json', 'Access-Control-Allow-Origin':'*' });
  392 |         res.end(JSON.stringify({ error:'api_key_not_configured', type:label, fallback:true }));
  393 |         return;
  394 |       }
  395 | 
  396 |       var prompt = payload.prompt || '';
  397 |       console.log('  →  ' + label + ' | ' + model + ' | ' + maxTokens + ' tokens');
  398 | 
  399 |       geminiRequest(apiKey, model, maxTokens, prompt, function(err, status, respBody) {
  400 |         if (err) {
  401 |           console.log('  ❌ Network error (' + label + '):', err.message);
  402 |           res.writeHead(502, { 'Content-Type':'application/json', 'Access-Control-Allow-Origin':'*' });
  403 |           res.end(JSON.stringify({ error: err.message }));
  404 |           return;
  405 |         }
  406 |         console.log('  ' + (status < 300 ? '✅' : '❌') + '  ' + status + '  ' + label);
  407 | 
  408 |         var wrapped;
  409 |         try {
  410 |           var gd   = JSON.parse(respBody);
  411 |           var text = (gd && gd.candidates && gd.candidates[0] && gd.candidates[0].content && gd.candidates[0].content.parts || [])
  412 |             .map(function(p){ return p.text || ''; }).join('');
  413 |           wrapped = JSON.stringify({ candidates: gd.candidates, content: [{ type:'text', text:text }] });
  414 |         } catch(e) { wrapped = respBody; }
  415 | 
  416 |         res.writeHead(status, { 'Content-Type':'application/json', 'Access-Control-Allow-Origin':'*' });
  417 |         res.end(wrapped);
  418 |       });
  419 |     });
  420 |     return;
  421 |   }
  422 | 
  423 |   // ── /api/send-report → Gmail SMTP ─────────────────────────────
  424 |   if (req.url === '/api/send-report' && req.method === 'POST') {
  425 |     if (!GMAIL_APP_PASSWORD) {
  426 |       console.log('  ❌ GMAIL_APP_PASSWORD not set');
  427 |       res.writeHead(500, { 'Content-Type':'application/json', 'Access-Control-Allow-Origin':'*' });
  428 |       res.end(JSON.stringify({ error: 'Gmail App Password not set in server.js' }));
  429 |       return;
  430 |     }
  431 | 
  432 |     var body = '';
  433 |     req.on('data', function(c){ body += c; });
  434 |     req.on('end', function() {
  435 |       var payload;
  436 |       try { payload = JSON.parse(body); }
  437 |       catch(e) { res.writeHead(400); res.end('bad json'); return; }
  438 | 
  439 |       var recipientEmail = payload.recipientEmail;
  440 |       if (!recipientEmail) {
  441 |         res.writeHead(400, { 'Content-Type':'application/json', 'Access-Control-Allow-Origin':'*' });
  442 |         res.end(JSON.stringify({ error: 'Missing recipientEmail' }));
  443 |         return;
  444 |       }
  445 | 
  446 |       var reportData = Object.assign({}, payload);
  447 |       delete reportData.recipientEmail;
  448 | 
  449 |       var subject = 'Market Intelligence Report — ' + (reportData.bizName || 'Your Assessment');
  450 |       var html    = buildReportEmail(reportData);
  451 | 
  452 |       console.log('  →  send-report to: ' + recipientEmail);
  453 | 
  454 |       var transporter = createTransporter();
  455 |       transporter.sendMail({
  456 |         from:    '"Infopace Reports" <' + GMAIL_USER + '>',
  457 |         to:      recipientEmail,
  458 |         subject: subject,
  459 |         html:    html,
  460 |       }, function(err) {
  461 |         if (err) {
  462 |           console.log('  ❌ Email error:', err.message);
  463 |           res.writeHead(500, { 'Content-Type':'application/json', 'Access-Control-Allow-Origin':'*' });
  464 |           res.end(JSON.stringify({ error: err.message }));
  465 |           return;
  466 |         }
  467 |         console.log('  ✅ Report emailed to: ' + recipientEmail);
  468 |         res.writeHead(200, { 'Content-Type':'application/json', 'Access-Control-Allow-Origin':'*' });
  469 |         res.end(JSON.stringify({ ok: true }));
  470 |       });
  471 |     });
  472 |     return;
  473 |   }
  474 | 
  475 |   // ── Static files ───────────────────────────────────────────────
  476 |   var fp = req.url === '/' ? '/index.html' : req.url.split('?')[0];
  477 |   fp = path.join(process.cwd(), fp);
  478 |   fs.readFile(fp, function(err, data) {
  479 |     if (err) { res.writeHead(404); res.end('Not found'); return; }
  480 |     res.writeHead(200, { 'Content-Type': MIME[path.extname(fp)] || 'text/plain' });
  481 |     res.end(data);
  482 |   });
  483 | 
  484 | }).listen(PORT, function() {
  485 |   var gmailOk = !!(GMAIL_APP_PASSWORD && GMAIL_APP_PASSWORD !== '');
  486 |   var qOk     = !!(API_KEY_QUESTIONS  && API_KEY_QUESTIONS  !== '');
  487 |   var aOk     = !!(API_KEY_ANALYSIS   && API_KEY_ANALYSIS   !== '');
  488 |   console.log('');
  489 |   console.log('  Infopace — Gemini + Gmail SMTP Edition');
  490 |   console.log('  ────────────────────────────────────────────────────');
  491 |   console.log('  🌐  http://localhost:' + PORT);
  492 |   console.log('  ────────────────────────────────────────────────────');
  493 |   console.log('  📧  Gmail         : ' + GMAIL_USER);
  494 |   console.log('  🔑  App Password  : ' + (gmailOk ? '✅ Set' : '❌ NOT SET — edit line 17'));
  495 |   console.log('  ❓  Questions key : ' + (qOk ? '✅ Set' : '⬜ Empty → fallback questions'));
  496 |   console.log('  📊  Analysis key  : ' + (aOk ? '✅ Set' : '⬜ Empty → offline analysis'));
  497 |   console.log('  ────────────────────────────────────────────────────');
  498 |   if (!gmailOk) {
  499 |     console.log('');
  500 |     console.log('  To enable email reports:');
  501 |     console.log('  1. Gmail → myaccount.google.com → Security → 2-Step Verification → ON');
  502 |     console.log('  2. Security → App Passwords → create one → copy 16-char password');
  503 |     console.log('  3. Paste into GMAIL_APP_PASSWORD on line 17 of this file');
  504 |     console.log('  ⚠  If email hangs: your network blocks SMTP. Use mobile hotspot.');
  505 |   }
  506 |   console.log('');
  507 | });

   68 | 
   69 | 
   70 | import { useState, useRef } from "react";
   71 | import OnboardingForm from "./pages/OnboardingForm";
   72 | import AssessmentAndDashboard from "./pages/AssessmentAndDashboard";
   73 | import { saveOnboarding, saveResult, saveScreenshotDataUrl } from "./lib/db";
   74 | 
   75 | // ── Flow:
   76 | //   1. User fills OnboardingForm → onComplete(userData) fires
   77 | //      → saveOnboarding() inserts row into Supabase, returns submissionId
   78 | //   2. User completes dashboard questions → AI generates result
   79 | //      → AssessmentAndDashboard calls onResult(answers, result)
   80 | //      → saveResult() updates the same row with scores + analysis
   81 | // ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   82 | 
   83 | export default function App() {
   84 |   const [userData, setUserData]       = useState(null);
   85 |   const submissionIdRef               = useRef(null); // holds Supabase row UUID
   86 | 
   87 |   // ── Called when onboarding form is submitted ──────────────────
   88 |   async function handleOnboardingComplete(formData) {
   89 |     setUserData(formData);
   90 | 
   91 |     // Save to Supabase immediately — non-blocking
   92 |     const id = await saveOnboarding(formData);
   93 |     submissionIdRef.current = id; // store for phase 2
   94 |   }
   95 | 
   96 |   // ── Called when AI analysis completes inside the dashboard ────
   97 |   async function handleResult(answers, result) {
   98 |     // Fire-and-forget — don't block the UI
   99 |     saveResult(submissionIdRef.current, answers, result).catch(e =>
  100 |       console.warn("DB result save failed:", e.message)
  101 |     );
  102 |   }
  103 | 
  104 |   // ── Called when a screenshot data URL is captured from the dashboard ──
  105 |   async function handleScreenshot(dataUrl) {
  106 |     const id = submissionIdRef.current;
  107 |     if (!id || !dataUrl) {
  108 |       console.warn("⚠️ handleScreenshot: missing id or dataUrl, skipping.");
  109 |       return;
  110 |     }
  111 |     try {
  112 |       await saveScreenshotDataUrl(id, dataUrl);
  113 |     } catch (e) {
  114 |       console.warn("Screenshot save failed:", e.message);
  115 |     }
  116 |   }
  117 | 
  118 |   function handleRestart() {
  119 |     setUserData(null);
  120 |     submissionIdRef.current = null;
  121 |   }
  122 | 
  123 |   if (userData) {
  124 |     return (
  125 |       <AssessmentAndDashboard
  126 |         userData={userData}
  127 |         onResult={handleResult}
  128 |         onScreenshot={handleScreenshot}
  129 |         onRestart={handleRestart}
  130 |       />
  131 |     );
  132 |   }
  133 | 
  134 |   return <OnboardingForm onComplete={handleOnboardingComplete} user={null} />;
  135 | }

    1 | import { supabase } from "./supabase";

    3 | export async function signUp(email, password) {
    4 |   const { data, error } = await supabase.auth.signUp({ email, password });
    5 |   if (error) throw new Error(error.message);
    6 |   return data;
    7 | }
    8 | 
    9 | export async function signIn(email, password) {
   10 |   const { data, error } = await supabase.auth.signInWithPassword({ email, password });
   11 |   if (error) throw new Error(error.message);
   12 |   return data;
   13 | }
   14 | 
   15 | export async function signOut() {
   16 |   const { error } = await supabase.auth.signOut();
   17 |   if (error) throw new Error(error.message);
   18 | }
   19 | 
   20 | export async function getUser() {
   21 |   const { data: { user } } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
   22 |   return user;
   23 | }
   24 | 
   25 | export function onAuthChange(callback) {
   26 |   return supabase.auth.onAuthStateChange((_event, session) => {
   27 |     callback(session?.user ?? null);
   28 |   });
   29 | }

    1 | // src/lib/db.js
    2 | import { supabase } from "./supabase";
    3 | 
    4 | // ── Phase 1: Save onboarding form immediately after submit ────────
    5 | export async function saveOnboarding(userData) {
    6 |   try {
    7 |     const { data, error } = await supabase
    8 |       .from("submissions")
    9 |       .insert([{
   10 |         name:          userData.name,
   11 |         email:         userData.email,
   12 |         phone:         userData.phone         || null,
   13 |         phone_full:    userData.phoneFull     || null,
   14 |         country_code:  userData.countryCode   || null,
   15 |         organization:  userData.organization  || null,
   16 |         role:          userData.role          || null,
   17 |         website:       userData.website       || null,
   18 |         linkedin:      userData.linkedin      || null,
   19 |         team_size:     userData.teamSize      || null,
   20 |         product_name:  userData.productName   || null,
   21 |         business_type: userData.businessType  || null,
   22 |         sector:        userData.sector        || null,
   23 |         geography:     userData.geography     || null,
   24 |         problem:       userData.problem       || null,
   25 |         stage:         userData.stage         || null,
   26 |         status:        "onboarding_complete",
   27 |       }])
   28 |       .select("id")
   29 |       .single();
   30 | 
   31 |     if (error) {
   32 |       console.error("❌ saveOnboarding error:", error.message);
   33 |       return null;
   34 |     }
   35 |     console.log("✅ Onboarding saved — ID:", data.id);
   36 |     return data.id;
   37 |   } catch (err) {
   38 |     console.error("❌ saveOnboarding exception:", err.message);
   39 |     return null;
   40 |   }
   41 | }
   42 | 
   43 | // ── Phase 2: Save AI analysis result ─────────────────────────────
   44 | export async function saveResult(submissionId, answers, result) {
   45 |   if (!submissionId) {
   46 |     console.warn("⚠️ saveResult: no submissionId, skipping.");
   47 |     return;
   48 |   }
   49 |   try {
   50 |     const { error } = await supabase
   51 |       .from("submissions")
   52 |       .update({
   53 |         answers,
   54 |         overall_score: result?.overallScore ?? null,
   55 |         grade:         result?.grade        ?? null,
   56 |         verdict:       result?.verdict      ?? null,
   57 |         tam_crore:     result?.tamCrore     ?? null,
   58 |         sam_crore:     result?.samCrore     ?? null,
   59 |         som_crore:     result?.somCrore     ?? null,
   60 |         growth_rate:   result?.growthRate   ?? null,
   61 |         dimensions:    result?.dimensions   ?? null,
   62 |         key_insights:  result?.keyInsights  ?? null,
   63 |         top_risks:     result?.topRisks     ?? null,
   64 |         quick_wins:    result?.quickWins    ?? null,
   65 |         analysis_json: result              ?? null,
   66 |         status:        "assessment_complete",
   67 |       })
   68 |       .eq("id", submissionId);
   69 | 
   70 |     if (error) console.error("❌ saveResult error:", error.message);
   71 |     else        console.log("✅ Result saved — ID:", submissionId);
   72 |   } catch (err) {
   73 |     console.error("❌ saveResult exception:", err.message);
   74 |   }
   75 | }
   76 | 
   77 | // ── Phase 3: Save screenshot as base64 data URL directly in DB ───
   78 | // Stores the image inline in the screenshot_url column (text type).
   79 | // This avoids needing a Supabase Storage bucket.
   80 | export async function saveScreenshotDataUrl(submissionId, dataUrl) {
   81 |   if (!submissionId || !dataUrl) {
   82 |     console.warn("⚠️ saveScreenshotDataUrl: missing id or dataUrl");
   83 |     return;
   84 |   }
   85 |   try {
   86 |     const { error } = await supabase
   87 |       .from("submissions")
   88 |       .update({ screenshot_url: dataUrl })
   89 |       .eq("id", submissionId);
   90 | 
   91 |     if (error) {
   92 |       console.error("❌ saveScreenshotDataUrl error:", error.message);
   93 |     } else {
   94 |       console.log("✅ Screenshot saved for:", submissionId, "(length:", dataUrl.length, "chars)");
   95 |     }
   96 |   } catch (err) {
   97 |     console.error("❌ saveScreenshotDataUrl exception:", err.message);
   98 |   }
   99 | }
  100 | 
  101 | // ── Legacy export (keeps old references working) ──────────────────
  102 | export async function saveSubmission({ userData, answers, result }) {
  103 |   const id = await saveOnboarding(userData);
  104 |   if (id) await saveResult(id, answers, result);
  105 | }

📄 FILE #18: src\lib\exportPdf.js

    1 | /**
    2 |  * exportPdf — captures the Charts view from the dashboard iframe
    3 |  * and opens it as a print-ready page for the user to save as PDF.
    4 |  *
    5 |  * Usage (unchanged):
    6 |  *   exportPdf({ userData, answers, result, iframeEl })
    7 |  *
    8 |  * NOTE: Pass the iframe DOM element as `iframeEl` from ResultsDashboard.jsx
    9 |  */
   10 | 
   11 | // ── Load html2canvas from CDN once ────────────────────────────────────────────
   12 | function loadHtml2Canvas() {
   13 |   return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
   14 |     if (window.html2canvas) { resolve(window.html2canvas); return; }
   15 |     const script   = document.createElement("script");
   16 |     script.src     = "https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/html2canvas/1.4.1/html2canvas.min.js";
   17 |     script.onload  = () => resolve(window.html2canvas);
   18 |     script.onerror = () => reject(new Error("html2canvas failed to load"));
   19 |     document.head.appendChild(script);
   20 |   });
   21 | }
   22 | 
   23 | // ── Capture only the #viewCharts section (or full dashboard as fallback) ──────
   24 | async function captureChartsSection(iframeEl) {
   25 |   const html2canvas = await loadHtml2Canvas();
   26 |   const iframeDoc   = iframeEl?.contentDocument || iframeEl?.contentWindow?.document;
   27 |   const iframeWin   = iframeEl?.contentWindow;
   28 | 
   29 |   if (!iframeDoc) throw new Error("Cannot access iframe document");
   30 | 
   31 |   // ── Step 1: Switch to charts view ─────────────────────────────────────────
   32 |   if (typeof iframeWin?.switchView === "function") {
   33 |     iframeWin.switchView("charts");
   34 |   }
   35 |   await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, 300));
   36 | 
   37 |   // ── Step 2: Expand iframe to a large fixed viewport so Chart.js canvases
   38 |   //    render at full size (they are sized to the iframe viewport) ──────────
   39 |   const CAPTURE_W = 1600;
   40 |   const CAPTURE_H = 900;
   41 |   const prevW = iframeEl.style.width;
   42 |   const prevH = iframeEl.style.height;
   43 |   iframeEl.style.width  = CAPTURE_W + "px";
   44 |   iframeEl.style.height = CAPTURE_H + "px";
   45 |   await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, 200));
   46 | 
   47 |   // ── Step 3: Force all Chart.js instances to resize to the new viewport ────
   48 |   const charts = iframeWin?.dashCharts || {};
   49 |   Object.values(charts).forEach(ch => { try { ch?.resize?.(); } catch (_) {} });
   50 | 
   51 |   // Wait for canvases to finish redrawing
   52 |   await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, 1000));
   53 | 
   54 |   // ── Step 4: #viewCharts is position:fixed — html2canvas can't measure it.
   55 |   //    Temporarily make it position:relative so scroll dimensions are correct.
   56 |   const viewCharts = iframeDoc.getElementById("viewCharts");
   57 |   const sidebar    = iframeDoc.getElementById("outputSidebar");
   58 |   let origVC = null, origSB = null;
   59 | 
   60 |   if (viewCharts) {
   61 |     origVC = viewCharts.getAttribute("style") || "";
   62 |     viewCharts.style.cssText = [
   63 |       "position:relative",
   64 |       "left:0",
   65 |       "top:0",
   66 |       "width:" + CAPTURE_W + "px",
   67 |       "height:auto",
   68 |       "overflow:visible",
   69 |       "display:flex",
   70 |       "flex-direction:column",
   71 |     ].join(";");
   72 |   }
   73 |   if (sidebar) {
   74 |     origSB = sidebar.getAttribute("style") || "";
   75 |     sidebar.style.display = "none";
   76 |   }
   77 | 
   78 |   await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, 150));
   79 | 
   80 |   const target = viewCharts || iframeDoc.getElementById("dashShell") || iframeDoc.body;
   81 |   const capW   = target.scrollWidth  || CAPTURE_W;
   82 |   const capH   = target.scrollHeight || CAPTURE_H;
   83 | 
   84 |   // ── Step 5: Capture ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   85 |   const canvas = await html2canvas(target, {
   86 |     useCORS:         true,
   87 |     allowTaint:      true,
   88 |     scale:           2,
   89 |     backgroundColor: "#EEF2F7",
   90 |     logging:         false,
   91 |     width:           capW,
   92 |     height:          capH,
   93 |     windowWidth:     CAPTURE_W,   // must match the viewport we forced above
   94 |     windowHeight:    CAPTURE_H,
   95 |     x: 0,
   96 |     y: 0,
   97 |     ignoreElements: el =>
   98 |       el.id === "outputSidebar" ||
   99 |       el.classList?.contains("sb-btn") ||
  100 |       el.classList?.contains("no-print"),
  101 |   });
  102 | 
  103 |   // ── Step 6: Restore everything ────────────────────────────────────────────
  104 |   if (viewCharts && origVC !== null) viewCharts.setAttribute("style", origVC);
  105 |   if (sidebar   && origSB !== null) sidebar.setAttribute("style", origSB);
  106 |   iframeEl.style.width  = prevW;
  107 |   iframeEl.style.height = prevH;
  108 | 
  109 |   return canvas.toDataURL("image/png", 0.95);
  110 | }
  111 | 
  112 | // ── Main export function ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────

📄 FILE #19: src\lib\gemini.js

    1 | /**
    2 |  * generateAnalysis — calls the Node proxy (server.js → Gemini)
    3 |  * Returns a parsed analysis object.
    4 |  */
    5 | export async function generateAnalysis(userData, answers = {}) {
    6 |   const answerLines = Object.entries(answers)
    7 |     .filter(([, v]) => v && v !== "")
    8 |     .map(([, v]) => `  - ${Array.isArray(v) ? v.join(", ") : v}`)
    9 |     .join("\n");
   10 | 
   11 |   const prompt = `You are a senior market intelligence analyst with deep knowledge of Indian and global markets.
   12 | 
   13 | Analyse this product and produce a data-driven market assessment using your real knowledge of this sector, geography, and companies.
   14 | 
   15 | PRODUCT: ${userData.organization || "Unnamed"}
   16 | SECTOR: ${userData.sector || "Not specified"}
   17 | BUSINESS TYPE: ${userData.role || "Not specified"}
   18 | TARGET GEOGRAPHY: ${userData.geography || "Not specified"}
   19 | BUSINESS STAGE: ${userData.stage || "Not specified"}
   20 | PROBLEM BEING SOLVED: ${userData.problem || "Not described"}
   21 | 
   22 | WHAT THE FOUNDER TOLD US ABOUT THEIR MARKET:
   23 | ${answerLines || "(answers not provided)"}
   24 | 
   25 | CRITICAL INSTRUCTIONS:
   26 | 1. Use your REAL knowledge of the ${userData.sector} market in ${userData.geography} — cite real TAM figures, real CAGR rates
   27 | 2. Name REAL competitors that actually exist in ${userData.sector} in ${userData.geography} — not placeholders
   28 | 3. Score those competitors based on your actual knowledge of their market position
   29 | 4. Revenue by region must reflect real market concentration for ${userData.sector} in ${userData.geography}
   30 | 5. The overall score must genuinely reflect the founder's answers above
   31 | 6. TAM/SAM/SOM must be realistic for this specific sector and geography
   32 | 
   33 | Return ONLY raw JSON, no markdown fences, no explanation before or after:
   34 | {
   35 | "overallScore": <0-100>,
   36 | "grade": "Excellent" or "Strong" or "Moderate" or "Needs Work" or "Critical",
   37 | "verdict": "<One specific sentence naming the product, its key opportunity, and its biggest risk>",
   38 | "realTimeInsight": "<One real market fact with actual numbers>",
   39 | "dimensions": {"marketSize":<0-100>,"audienceQuality":<0-100>,"competitionEdge":<0-100>,"revenuePotential":<0-100>,"riskProfile":<0-100>,"sectorFit":<0-100>},
   40 | "tamCrore": <realistic TAM in ₹Crore>,
   41 | "samCrore": <serviceable portion>,
   42 | "somCrore": <3-year realistic target>,
   43 | "growthRate": <real CAGR %>,
   44 | "competitorProfiles": [
   45 |   {"name":"<REAL company 1>","stage":"<funding/size>","strength":"<real strength>","weakness":"<real gap>","marketSharePct":<realistic %>},
   46 |   {"name":"<REAL company 2>","stage":"<funding/size>","strength":"<real strength>","weakness":"<real gap>","marketSharePct":<realistic %>},
   47 |   {"name":"<REAL company 3>","stage":"<funding/size>","strength":"<real strength>","weakness":"<real gap>","marketSharePct":<realistic %>}
   48 | ],
   49 | "marketShare": [
   50 |   {"name":"<product>","pct":<1-10>,"val":"₹<somCrore>Cr"},
   51 |   {"name":"<real comp 1>","pct":<their share %>,"val":"₹<amount>Cr"},
   52 |   {"name":"<real comp 2>","pct":<their share %>,"val":"₹<amount>Cr"},
   53 |   {"name":"<real comp 3>","pct":<their share %>,"val":"₹<amount>Cr"},
   54 |   {"name":"Others","pct":<remainder>,"val":"—"}
   55 | ],
   56 | "revenueByRegion": {
   57 |   "labels": [<5-6 real cities relevant to the sector>],
   58 |   "currentMarket": [<real ₹Cr market size per city>],
   59 |   "projected2027": [<apply growthRate CAGR>],
   60 |   "ourTarget": [<realistic 2-8% of each city market>]
   61 | },
   62 | "competitorRadar": [
   63 |   {"name":"<product>","scores":{"pricingPower":<0-100>,"distribution":<0-100>,"brandValue":<0-100>,"innovation":<0-100>,"marketReach":<0-100>,"customerSat":<0-100>},"avg":"<average>"},
   64 |   {"name":"<comp 1>","scores":{"pricingPower":<n>,"distribution":<n>,"brandValue":<n>,"innovation":<n>,"marketReach":<n>,"customerSat":<n>},"avg":"<average>"},
   65 |   {"name":"<comp 2>","scores":{"pricingPower":<n>,"distribution":<n>,"brandValue":<n>,"innovation":<n>,"marketReach":<n>,"customerSat":<n>},"avg":"<average>"},
   66 |   {"name":"<comp 3>","scores":{"pricingPower":<n>,"distribution":<n>,"brandValue":<n>,"innovation":<n>,"marketReach":<n>,"customerSat":<n>},"avg":"<average>"}
   67 | ],
   68 | "trendData": {
   69 |   "months": ["Apr","May","Jun","Jul","Aug","Sep","Oct","Nov","Dec","Jan","Feb","Mar"],
   70 |   "series": [
   71 |     {"label":"<product>","dash":[],"data":[<12 monthly values 0-1% to 3-8%>]},
   72 |     {"label":"<comp 1>","dash":[],"data":[<12 monthly values ~20-35%>]},
   73 |     {"label":"<comp 2>","dash":[],"data":[<12 monthly values ~15-25%>]},
   74 |     {"label":"<comp 3>","dash":[],"data":[<12 monthly values ~10-20%>]}
   75 |   ]
   76 | },
   77 | "geoRegions": {
   78 |   "Asia Pacific": {"rev":"<global sector size>","pct":"<% of global TAM>","ids":[4,50,156,356,360,392,410,458,702,704,764]},
   79 |   "North America": {"rev":"<global sector size>","pct":"<% of global TAM>","ids":[124,484,840]},
   80 |   "South America": {"rev":"<global sector size>","pct":"<% of global TAM>","ids":[32,68,76,152,170]},
   81 |   "Europe": {"rev":"<global sector size>","pct":"<% of global TAM>","ids":[276,250,826,380,724,528,208,752,756,616]},
   82 |   "Africa": {"rev":"<global sector size>","pct":"<% of global TAM>","ids":[566,710,404,818,12]}
   83 | },
   84 | "keyInsights": ["<insight 1 with numbers>","<insight 2>","<insight 3>","<insight 4>","<90-day action>"],
   85 | "topRisks": ["<risk 1>","<risk 2>","<risk 3>"],
   86 | "quickWins": ["<win 1>","<win 2>","<win 3>"],
   87 | "popups": {
   88 |   "mktshare": "<2 sentences: TAM/SAM/SOM + competitor context>",
   89 |   "revregion": "<2 sentences: priority cities and why>",
   90 |   "radar": "<2 sentences: where product leads and trails>",
   91 |   "trend": "<2 sentences: trajectory and inflection point>",
   92 |   "geomap": "<2 sentences: geographic focus rationale>"
   93 | }
   94 | }`;
   95 | 
   96 |   const resp = await fetch("/api", {
   97 |     method: "POST",
   98 |     headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
   99 |     body: JSON.stringify({ _type: "analysis", prompt }),
  100 |   });
  101 | 
  102 |   if (!resp.ok) throw new Error("API error " + resp.status);
  103 | 
  104 |   const data = await resp.json();
  105 | 
  106 |   // Support both Gemini native format and Anthropic-style wrapper
  107 |   const allText = (data?.candidates?.[0]?.content?.parts || [])
  108 |     .map((p) => p.text || "")
  109 |     .join("") || (data?.content?.[0]?.text || "");
  110 | 
  111 |   if (!allText) throw new Error("Empty API response");
  112 | 
  113 |   let raw = allText.trim();
  114 |   const fm = raw.match(/```(?:json)?\s*([\s\S]*?)```/);
  115 |   if (fm) raw = fm[1].trim();
  116 | 
  117 |   const s0 = raw.indexOf("{"), e0 = raw.lastIndexOf("}");
  118 |   if (s0 === -1 || e0 === -1) throw new Error("No JSON in response");
  119 |   raw = raw.slice(s0, e0 + 1);
  120 | 
  121 |   return JSON.parse(raw);
  122 | }
  123 |

    1 | // src/pages/AssessmentAndDashboard.jsx
    2 | import { useEffect, useRef } from "react";
    3 | import { generateAnalysis } from "../lib/gemini";
    4 | import { exportPdf } from "../lib/exportPdf";

    6 | // ── Load html2canvas from CDN once ─────────────────────────────────
    7 | function loadHtml2Canvas() {
    8 |   return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
    9 |     if (window.html2canvas) { resolve(window.html2canvas); return; }
   10 |     const script   = document.createElement("script");
   11 |     script.src     = "https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/html2canvas/1.4.1/html2canvas.min.js";
   12 |     script.onload  = () => resolve(window.html2canvas);
   13 |     script.onerror = () => reject(new Error("html2canvas failed to load"));
   14 |     document.head.appendChild(script);
   15 |   });
   16 | }
   17 | 
   18 | // Maps React onboarding userData → dashboard.html iframe field codes
   19 | function buildPrefill(userData) {
   20 |   const SECTOR_MAP = {
   21 |     "Information Technology / SaaS": "IT",
   22 |     "Healthcare & Pharma":           "HC",
   23 |     "Financial Services / FinTech":  "FS",
   24 |     "E-Commerce & Retail":           "EC",
   25 |     "Education & EdTech":            "ED",
   26 |     "Manufacturing":                 "MF",
   27 |     "Real Estate & PropTech":        "RE",
   28 |     "Logistics & Supply Chain":      "LG",
   29 |     "Media & Entertainment":         "ME",
   30 |     "Agriculture & AgroTech":        "AG",
   31 |     "Energy & CleanTech":            "EN",
   32 |   };
   33 | 
   34 |   const BIZ_TYPE_MAP = {
   35 |   // Short form — matches OnboardingForm BUSINESS_TYPES values
   36 |   "B2B":             "B2B_SME",
   37 |   "B2C":             "B2C_MASS",
   38 |   "B2B2C":           "B2B_SME",
   39 |   "D2C":             "B2C_MASS",
   40 |   "Marketplace":     "B2B_SME",
   41 |   "SaaS / Platform": "B2B_SME",
   42 |   // Long form — kept for backwards compatibility
   43 |   "B2B (Business to Business)": "B2B_SME",
   44 |   "B2C (Business to Consumer)": "B2C_MASS",
   45 |   "D2C (Direct to Consumer)":   "B2C_MASS",
   46 |   "Other":                      "B2B_SME",
   47 | };
   48 | 
   49 |   return {
   50 |     organization: userData.organization,
   51 |     bizName:      userData.productName   || userData.organization,
   52 |     sectorCode:   SECTOR_MAP[userData.sector]       || "OT",
   53 |     bizTypeCode:  BIZ_TYPE_MAP[userData.businessType] || "B2B_SME",
   54 |     geoCode:      userData.geography     || "PI",
   55 |     problem:      userData.problem,
   56 |     stage:        userData.stage,
   57 |   };
   58 | }
   59 | 
   60 | const LOADER_STEPS = [
   61 |   { n: 1, msg: "Reading your inputs…",                                    pct: 8  },
   62 |   { n: 2, msg: "Searching live market data & sector sizing…",             pct: 25 },
   63 |   { n: 3, msg: "Fetching real-time competitor profiles & funding data…",  pct: 48 },
   64 |   { n: 4, msg: "Calculating TAM/SAM/SOM, scores & 12-month projections…", pct: 75 },
   65 |   { n: 5, msg: "Assembling your market intelligence dashboard…",          pct: 95 },
   66 | ];
   67 | 
   68 | // ── onResult(answers, result) is called by App.jsx to save to Supabase
   69 | // ── onScreenshot(blob) is called by App.jsx to upload the dashboard image
   70 | export default function AssessmentAndDashboard({ userData, onResult, onScreenshot, onRestart }) {
   71 |   const iframeRef       = useRef(null);
   72 |   const prefillSentRef  = useRef(false);
   73 |   const latestResultRef = useRef(null);
   74 |   const latestFdRef     = useRef(null);
   75 | 
   76 |   function postToIframe(msg) {
   77 |     iframeRef.current?.contentWindow?.postMessage(msg, "*");
   78 |   }
   79 | 
   80 |   async function handleSubmit(fd) {
   81 |     latestFdRef.current = fd;
   82 | 
   83 |     // Drive loader steps
   84 |     for (const s of LOADER_STEPS) {
   85 |       postToIframe({ type: "INFOPACE_LOADER_STEP", step: s.n, msg: s.msg, pct: s.pct });
   86 |       await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, s.n === 3 ? 150 : 300));
   87 |     }
   88 | 
   89 |     try {
   90 |       const result = await generateAnalysis(userData, fd.answers || {});
   91 |       latestResultRef.current = result;
   92 | 
   93 |       // ── Save result to Supabase via App.jsx callback ──────────
   94 |       if (onResult) {
   95 |         onResult(fd.answers || {}, result);
   96 |       }
   97 | 
   98 |       // Render dashboard in iframe with AI result
   99 |       postToIframe({ type: "INFOPACE_RENDER", fd, analysis: result });
  100 | 
  101 |       // ── Capture screenshot after dashboard renders (with delay for animations) ──
  102 |       captureAndUpload();
  103 | 
  104 |     } catch (err) {
  105 |       console.warn("Gemini analysis failed, falling back to offline:", err.message);
  106 | 
  107 |       // Pass null analysis — dashboard.html will run offlineAnalysis(fd) itself
  108 |       postToIframe({ type: "INFOPACE_LOADER_STEP", step: 5, msg: "Building live analysis…", pct: 95 });
  109 | 
  110 |       if (onResult) {
  111 |         onResult(fd.answers || {}, {});
  112 |       }
  113 | 
  114 |       setTimeout(() => {
  115 |         postToIframe({ type: "INFOPACE_RENDER", fd, analysis: null });
  116 |         // Capture screenshot even for offline analysis
  117 |         captureAndUpload();
  118 |       }, 600);
  119 |     }
  120 |   }
  121 | 
  122 |   // ── Capture the rendered dashboard and save as base64 data URL ──
  123 |   async function captureAndUpload() {
  124 |     if (!onScreenshot) return;
  125 |     try {
  126 |       // Wait for Chart.js animations and rendering to finish
  127 |       await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, 3000));
  128 | 
  129 |       const html2canvas = await loadHtml2Canvas();
  130 |       const iframeDoc = iframeRef.current?.contentDocument
  131 |                      || iframeRef.current?.contentWindow?.document;
  132 |       if (!iframeDoc) {
  133 |         console.warn("⚠️ captureAndUpload: cannot access iframe document");
  134 |         return;
  135 |       }
  136 | 
  137 |       // Target the charts view or fall back to the full dashboard
  138 |       const target = iframeDoc.getElementById("viewCharts")
  139 |                   || iframeDoc.getElementById("dashShell")
  140 |                   || iframeDoc.body;
  141 | 
  142 |       const canvas = await html2canvas(target, {
  143 |         useCORS:         true,
  144 |         allowTaint:      true,
  145 |         scale:           1.5,            // balance quality vs size
  146 |         backgroundColor: "#EEF2F7",
  147 |         logging:         false,
  148 |       });
  149 | 
  150 |       // Convert canvas to base64 data URL and send to App.jsx
  151 |       const dataUrl = canvas.toDataURL("image/png", 0.85);
  152 |       if (dataUrl && dataUrl.length > 100) {
  153 |         console.log("📸 Dashboard screenshot captured, length:", dataUrl.length, "chars");
  154 |         onScreenshot(dataUrl);
  155 |       } else {
  156 |         console.warn("⚠️ Screenshot capture produced empty result");
  157 |       }
  158 |     } catch (err) {
  159 |       console.warn("⚠️ Screenshot capture failed:", err.message);
  160 |     }
  161 |   }
  162 | 
  163 |   useEffect(() => {
  164 |     function handleMessage(event) {
  165 |       if (!event.data) return;
  166 | 
  167 |       if (event.data.type === "INFOPACE_LOADED") {
  168 |         if (!prefillSentRef.current) {
  169 |           prefillSentRef.current = true;
  170 |           postToIframe({ type: "INFOPACE_PREFILL", userData: buildPrefill(userData) });
  171 |         }
  172 |       }
  173 | 
  174 |       if (event.data.type === "INFOPACE_SUBMIT") {
  175 |         handleSubmit(event.data.fd);
  176 |       }
  177 | 
  178 |       if (event.data.type === "INFOPACE_EXPORT_PDF") {
  179 |         handleExportPdf();
  180 |       }
  181 | 
  182 |       if (event.data.type === "INFOPACE_RESET") {
  183 |         onRestart();
  184 |       }
  185 |     }
  186 | 
  187 |     window.addEventListener("message", handleMessage);
  188 |     return () => window.removeEventListener("message", handleMessage);
  189 |   }, [userData]);
  190 | 
  191 |   function handleExportPdf() {
  192 |     exportPdf({
  193 |       userData,
  194 |       answers: latestFdRef.current?.answers || {},
  195 |       result:  latestResultRef.current || {},
  196 |       iframeEl: iframeRef.current,   
  197 |     });
  198 |   }
  199 | 
  200 |   return (
  201 |     <iframe
  202 |       ref={iframeRef}
  203 |       src="/dashboard.html"
  204 |       style={{ position: "fixed", inset: 0, border: "none", width: "100%", height: "100%" }}
  205 |       title="Infopace Assessment"
  206 |       sandbox="allow-scripts allow-same-origin allow-popups allow-downloads"
  207 |     />
  208 |   );
  209 | }

    1 | import { useState } from "react";
    2 | import { signIn, signUp } from "../lib/auth";
    3 | 
    4 | export default function AuthPage({ onAuth }) {
    5 |   const [mode, setMode]       = useState("login"); // "login" | "signup"
    6 |   const [email, setEmail]     = useState("");
    7 |   const [password, setPassword] = useState("");
    8 |   const [confirm, setConfirm] = useState("");
    9 |   const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);
   10 |   const [error, setError]     = useState("");
   11 |   const [success, setSuccess] = useState("");
   12 | 
   13 |   const inp = "w-full border border-[#D6DFED] rounded px-3 py-2 text-sm font-[IBM_Plex_Sans] bg-[#EEF2F7] outline-none focus:border-[#0091DA] focus:ring-2 focus:ring-[#0091DA]/10 focus:bg-white transition-all";
   14 | 
   15 |   async function handleSubmit(e) {
   16 |     e.preventDefault();
   17 |     setError(""); setSuccess("");
   18 |     if (!email || !password) { setError("Email and password are required."); return; }
   19 |     if (mode === "signup" && password !== confirm) { setError("Passwords do not match."); return; }
   20 |     if (password.length < 6) { setError("Password must be at least 6 characters."); return; }
   21 | 
   22 |     setLoading(true);
   23 |     try {
   24 |       if (mode === "signup") {
   25 |         await signUp(email, password);
   26 |         setSuccess("Account created! Check your email to confirm, then log in.");
   27 |         setMode("login");
   28 |       } else {
   29 |         const data = await signIn(email, password);
   30 |         onAuth(data.user);
   31 |       }
   32 |     } catch (err) {
   33 |       setError(err.message);
   34 |     } finally {
   35 |       setLoading(false);
   36 |     }
   37 |   }
   38 | 
   39 |   return (
   40 |     <div className="min-h-screen bg-[#EEF2F7] flex flex-col">
   41 |       {/* Topbar */}
   42 |       <div className="bg-[#00338D] h-12 flex items-center px-6 shadow-md">
   43 |         <div className="w-8 h-8 bg-[#0091DA] rounded flex items-center justify-center font-mono font-bold text-xs text-white mr-3">IP</div>
   44 |         <div>
   45 |           <div className="text-xs font-bold tracking-widest text-white uppercase">Infopace Management Pvt Ltd</div>
   46 |           <div className="text-[7px] tracking-widest text-white/40 uppercase">Market Intelligence Platform</div>
   47 |         </div>
   48 |       </div>
   49 | 
   50 |       {/* Card */}
   51 |       <div className="flex-1 flex items-center justify-center p-6">
   52 |         <div className="w-full max-w-md">
   53 |           <div className="text-center mb-8">
   54 |             <h1 className="text-3xl font-bold text-[#08152A] tracking-tight">
   55 |               Market <span className="text-[#0091DA] underline underline-offset-4" style={{ textDecorationThickness: 2 }}>Intelligence</span>
   56 |             </h1>
   57 |             <p className="text-sm text-[#627289] mt-2 max-w-xs mx-auto">
   58 |               {mode === "login" ? "Sign in to access your market assessments." : "Create an account to get started."}
   59 |             </p>
   60 |           </div>
   61 | 
   62 |           <div className="bg-white border border-[#D6DFED] rounded shadow-sm overflow-hidden relative">
   63 |             <div className="absolute top-0 left-0 right-0 h-[3px] bg-[#00338D]" />
   64 | 
   65 |             {/* Tabs */}
   66 |             <div className="flex border-b border-[#D6DFED]">
   67 |               {["login", "signup"].map(m => (
   68 |                 <button key={m} onClick={() => { setMode(m); setError(""); setSuccess(""); }}
   69 |                   className={`flex-1 py-3 text-xs font-semibold tracking-wide transition-all
   70 |                     ${mode === m ? "bg-white text-[#00338D] border-b-2 border-[#00338D]" : "bg-[#EEF2F7] text-[#627289] hover:text-[#08152A]"}`}>
   71 |                   {m === "login" ? "Sign In" : "Create Account"}
   72 |                 </button>
   73 |               ))}
   74 |             </div>
   75 | 
   76 |             <form onSubmit={handleSubmit} className="p-7 flex flex-col gap-4">
   77 |               <div className="flex flex-col gap-1.5">
   78 |                 <label className="text-[10px] font-semibold uppercase tracking-wider text-[#627289]">Email Address</label>
   79 |                 <input className={inp} type="email" placeholder="you@company.com"
   80 |                   value={email} onChange={e => setEmail(e.target.value)} />
   81 |               </div>
   82 | 
   83 |               <div className="flex flex-col gap-1.5">
   84 |                 <label className="text-[10px] font-semibold uppercase tracking-wider text-[#627289]">Password</label>
   85 |                 <input className={inp} type="password" placeholder="Min. 6 characters"
   86 |                   value={password} onChange={e => setPassword(e.target.value)} />
   87 |               </div>
   88 | 
   89 |               {mode === "signup" && (
   90 |                 <div className="flex flex-col gap-1.5">
   91 |                   <label className="text-[10px] font-semibold uppercase tracking-wider text-[#627289]">Confirm Password</label>
   92 |                   <input className={inp} type="password" placeholder="Repeat password"
   93 |                     value={confirm} onChange={e => setConfirm(e.target.value)} />
   94 |                 </div>
   95 |               )}
   96 | 
   97 |               {error   && <div className="text-xs text-red-600 bg-red-50 border border-red-200 rounded px-3 py-2">{error}</div>}
   98 |               {success && <div className="text-xs text-green-700 bg-green-50 border border-green-200 rounded px-3 py-2">{success}</div>}
   99 | 
  100 |               <button type="submit" disabled={loading}
  101 |                 className="mt-1 px-6 py-2.5 bg-[#00338D] text-white text-sm font-semibold rounded hover:bg-[#005EB8] transition-all disabled:opacity-50 disabled:cursor-not-allowed">
  102 |                 {loading ? "Please wait…" : mode === "login" ? "Sign In →" : "Create Account →"}
  103 |               </button>

  106 |                 <p className="text-center text-[10px] text-[#9BAABB]">
  107 |                   Don't have an account?{" "}
  108 |                   <button type="button" onClick={() => { setMode("signup"); setError(""); }}
  109 |                     className="text-[#0091DA] hover:underline font-semibold">Sign up free</button>
  110 |                 </p>
  111 |               )}
  112 |             </form>
  113 |           </div>
  114 | 
  115 |           <p className="text-center text-[10px] text-[#9BAABB] mt-4">
  116 |             🔒 Your data is stored securely. We never share personal details with third parties.
  117 |           </p>
  118 |         </div>
  119 |       </div>
  120 |     </div>
  121 |   );
  122 | }
