   88 |   textPrimary:   "#0A1628",
   89 |   textSecondary: "#475569",
   90 |   textMuted:     "#94a3b8",
   91 |   textOnDark:    "#FFFFFF",
   92 | 
   93 |   // Borders
   94 |   border:       "rgba(17,68,160,0.15)",
   95 |   borderDark:   "rgba(17,68,160,0.3)",
   96 | 
   97 |   // Error
   98 |   errText:   "#be123c",
   99 |   errBg:     "#fff1f2",
  100 |   errBorder: "#fda4af",
  101 | 
  102 |   // Fonts
  103 |   mono:  "'IBM Plex Mono', monospace",
  104 |   serif: "'Playfair Display', Georgia, serif",
  105 |   sans:  "'Inter', 'DM Sans', system-ui, sans-serif",
  106 | };
  107 | 
  108 | // ─── ANIMATED BACKGROUND CANVAS ──────────────────────────────────────────────
  109 | function AnimatedBackground() {
  110 |   const canvasRef = useRef(null);
  111 |   const mouseRef  = useRef({ x: -9999, y: -9999, vx: 0, vy: 0, px: -9999, py: -9999 });
  112 |   const rafRef    = useRef(null);
  113 | 
  114 |   useEffect(() => {
  115 |     const canvas = canvasRef.current;
  116 |     if (!canvas) return;
  117 |     const ctx = canvas.getContext("2d");
  118 |     let W = 0, H = 0;
  119 | 
  120 |     function resize() {
  121 |       W = canvas.width  = canvas.offsetWidth;
  122 |       H = canvas.height = canvas.offsetHeight;
  123 |       buildGrid();
  124 |     }
  125 | 
  126 |     // ── Mouse tracking ──
  127 |     const onMove = e => {
  128 |       const r = canvas.getBoundingClientRect();
  129 |       const mx = e.clientX - r.left;
  130 |       const my = e.clientY - r.top;
  131 |       mouseRef.current.vx = mx - mouseRef.current.x;
  132 |       mouseRef.current.vy = my - mouseRef.current.y;
  133 |       mouseRef.current.x  = mx;
  134 |       mouseRef.current.y  = my;
  135 |     };
  136 |     window.addEventListener("mousemove", onMove);
  137 | 
  138 |     // ── Grid of nodes for "ripple field" effect ──
  139 |     const COLS = 18, ROWS = 12;
  140 |     let nodes = [];
  141 |     function buildGrid() {
  142 |       nodes = [];
  143 |       for (let r = 0; r <= ROWS; r++) {
  144 |         for (let c = 0; c <= COLS; c++) {
  145 |           nodes.push({
  146 |             ox: (c / COLS) * W,
  147 |             oy: (r / ROWS) * H,
  148 |             x:  (c / COLS) * W,
  149 |             y:  (r / ROWS) * H,
  150 |             vx: 0, vy: 0,
  151 |             phase: Math.random() * Math.PI * 2,
  152 |           });
  153 |         }
  154 |       }
  155 |     }
  156 |     buildGrid();
  157 |     resize();
  158 |     window.addEventListener("resize", resize);
  159 | 
  160 |     // ── 3D Wireframe Shapes ──
  161 |     // Project a 3D point to 2D canvas coords
  162 |     function project(x, y, z, cx, cy, fov = 320) {
  163 |       const scale = fov / (fov + z);
  164 |       return { x: cx + x * scale, y: cy + y * scale, scale };
  165 |     }
  166 | 
  167 |     // Rotate a point around X and Y axes
  168 |     function rotateXY(x, y, z, rx, ry) {
  169 |       // Rotate around Y
  170 |       const x1 = x * Math.cos(ry) - z * Math.sin(ry);
  171 |       const z1 = x * Math.sin(ry) + z * Math.cos(ry);
  172 |       // Rotate around X
  173 |       const y2 = y * Math.cos(rx) - z1 * Math.sin(rx);
  174 |       const z2 = y * Math.sin(rx) + z1 * Math.cos(rx);
  175 |       return { x: x1, y: y2, z: z2 };
  176 |     }
  177 | 
  178 |     // Define cube vertices & edges
  179 |     function makeCube(size) {
  180 |       const h = size / 2;
  181 |       const verts = [
  182 |         [-h,-h,-h],[h,-h,-h],[h,h,-h],[-h,h,-h],
  183 |         [-h,-h, h],[h,-h, h],[h,h, h],[-h,h, h],
  184 |       ];
  185 |       const edges = [
  186 |         [0,1],[1,2],[2,3],[3,0],
  187 |         [4,5],[5,6],[6,7],[7,4],
  188 |         [0,4],[1,5],[2,6],[3,7],
  189 |       ];
  190 |       return { verts, edges };
  191 |     }
  192 | 
  193 |     // Define octahedron vertices & edges
  194 |     function makeOctahedron(size) {
  195 |       const s = size;
  196 |       const verts = [
  197 |         [0,-s,0],[s,0,0],[0,0,s],[-s,0,0],[0,0,-s],[0,s,0],
  198 |       ];
  199 |       const edges = [
  200 |         [0,1],[0,2],[0,3],[0,4],
  201 |         [5,1],[5,2],[5,3],[5,4],
  202 |         [1,2],[2,3],[3,4],[4,1],
  203 |       ];
  204 |       return { verts, edges };
  205 |     }
  206 | 
  207 |     // Define icosahedron-like diamond / tetrahedron
  208 |     function makeTetrahedron(size) {
  209 |       const s = size;
  210 |       const verts = [
  211 |         [0, s, 0],
  212 |         [ s * 0.94, -s * 0.33, 0],
  213 |         [-s * 0.47, -s * 0.33,  s * 0.82],
  214 |         [-s * 0.47, -s * 0.33, -s * 0.82],
  215 |       ];
  216 |       const edges = [
  217 |         [0,1],[0,2],[0,3],[1,2],[2,3],[3,1],
  218 |       ];
  219 |       return { verts, edges };
  220 |     }
  221 | 
  222 |     // Icosahedron
  223 |     function makeIcosahedron(size) {
  224 |       const t = (1 + Math.sqrt(5)) / 2;
  225 |       const s = size / Math.sqrt(1 + t * t);
  226 |       const verts = [
  227 |         [-1,t,0],[1,t,0],[-1,-t,0],[1,-t,0],
  228 |         [0,-1,t],[0,1,t],[0,-1,-t],[0,1,-t],
  229 |         [t,0,-1],[t,0,1],[-t,0,-1],[-t,0,1],
  230 |       ].map(([x,y,z]) => [x*s,y*s,z*s]);
  231 |       const edges = [
  232 |         [0,1],[0,5],[0,7],[0,10],[0,11],
  233 |         [1,5],[1,7],[1,8],[1,9],
  234 |         [2,3],[2,4],[2,6],[2,10],[2,11],
  235 |         [3,4],[3,6],[3,8],[3,9],
  236 |         [4,5],[4,9],[4,11],
  237 |         [5,9],[5,11],
  238 |         [6,7],[6,8],[6,10],
  239 |         [7,8],[7,10],
  240 |         [8,9],[10,11],
  241 |       ];
  242 |       return { verts, edges };
  243 |     }
  244 | 
  245 |     // Torus ring
  246 |     function makeTorus(R, r, segs = 10, rings = 14) {
  247 |       const verts = [];
  248 |       const edges = [];
  249 |       for (let i = 0; i < rings; i++) {
  250 |         const theta = (i / rings) * Math.PI * 2;
  251 |         for (let j = 0; j < segs; j++) {
  252 |           const phi = (j / segs) * Math.PI * 2;
  253 |           verts.push([
  254 |             (R + r * Math.cos(phi)) * Math.cos(theta),
  255 |             r * Math.sin(phi),
  256 |             (R + r * Math.cos(phi)) * Math.sin(theta),
  257 |           ]);
  258 |           edges.push([i * segs + j, i * segs + (j + 1) % segs]);
  259 |           edges.push([i * segs + j, ((i + 1) % rings) * segs + j]);
  260 |         }
  261 |       }
  262 |       return { verts, edges };
  263 |     }
  264 | 
  265 |     // Pyramid
  266 |     function makePyramid(size) {
  267 |       const b = size * 0.65, h = size;
  268 |       const verts = [[-b,b*0.5,-b],[b,b*0.5,-b],[b,b*0.5,b],[-b,b*0.5,b],[0,-h,0]];
  269 |       const edges = [[0,1],[1,2],[2,3],[3,0],[0,4],[1,4],[2,4],[3,4]];
  270 |       return { verts, edges };
  271 |     }
  272 | 
  273 |     // Initialise shape instances — 8 shapes, same style as original
  274 |     const SHAPES = [
  275 |       { ...makeCube(70),          rx: 0.003, ry: 0.005, rz: 0.002, angX: 0.4,  angY: 0.2  },
  276 |       { ...makeOctahedron(55),    rx: 0.004, ry: 0.003, rz: 0.003, angX: 1.0,  angY: 0.8  },
  277 |       { ...makeTetrahedron(62),   rx: 0.003, ry: 0.006, rz: 0.001, angX: 2.1,  angY: 1.4  },
  278 |       { ...makeIcosahedron(58),   rx: 0.002, ry: 0.004, rz: 0.002, angX: 0.7,  angY: 1.9  },
  279 |       { ...makeTorus(40,13),      rx: 0.005, ry: 0.003, rz: 0.002, angX: 0.3,  angY: 0.5  },
  280 |       { ...makePyramid(55),       rx: 0.003, ry: 0.005, rz: 0.001, angX: 1.6,  angY: 0.9  },
  281 |       { ...makeCube(48),          rx: 0.004, ry: 0.003, rz: 0.003, angX: 3.0,  angY: 2.4  },
  282 |       { ...makeOctahedron(42),    rx: 0.006, ry: 0.002, rz: 0.004, angX: 0.1,  angY: 2.2  },
  283 |     ];
  284 | 
  285 |     // Positions spread across the full canvas
  286 |     const shapePositions = [
  287 |       { fx: 0.12, fy: 0.25 },
  288 |       { fx: 0.88, fy: 0.65 },
  289 |       { fx: 0.55, fy: 0.12 },
  290 |       { fx: 0.80, fy: 0.18 },
  291 |       { fx: 0.15, fy: 0.72 },
  292 |       { fx: 0.93, fy: 0.40 },
  293 |       { fx: 0.42, fy: 0.82 },
  294 |       { fx: 0.68, fy: 0.50 },
  295 |     ];
  296 | 
  297 |     // ── Ripple trails ──
  298 |     const ripples = [];
  299 | 
  300 |     // ── Beam streaks from cursor movement ──
  301 |     const streaks = [];
  302 | 
  303 |     let t = 0;
  304 |     let prevSpeed = 0;
  305 | 
  306 |     function drawShape(shape, pos, alpha) {
  307 |       const cx = pos.fx * W;
  308 |       const cy = pos.fy * H;
  309 |       const projected = shape.verts.map(([x, y, z]) => {
  310 |         const rot = rotateXY(x, y, z, shape.angX, shape.angY);
  311 |         return project(rot.x, rot.y, rot.z, cx, cy);
  312 |       });
  313 | 
  314 |       ctx.lineWidth = 0.7;
  315 |       shape.edges.forEach(([a, b]) => {
  316 |         const pa = projected[a], pb = projected[b];
  317 |         // depth-based fade
  318 |         const depthAlpha = alpha * (0.5 + 0.5 * ((pa.scale + pb.scale) / 2));
  319 |         ctx.beginPath();
  320 |         ctx.moveTo(pa.x, pa.y);
  321 |         ctx.lineTo(pb.x, pb.y);
  322 |         ctx.strokeStyle = `rgba(59,130,246,${depthAlpha.toFixed(3)})`;
  323 |         ctx.stroke();
  324 |       });
  325 | 
  326 |       // small vertex dots
  327 |       projected.forEach(p => {
  328 |         ctx.beginPath();
  329 |         ctx.arc(p.x, p.y, 1.2, 0, Math.PI * 2);
  330 |         ctx.fillStyle = `rgba(147,197,253,${(alpha * 0.7).toFixed(3)})`;
  331 |         ctx.fill();
  332 |       });
  333 |     }
  334 | 
  335 |     function draw() {
  336 |       const m = mouseRef.current;
  337 |       const speed = Math.sqrt(m.vx * m.vx + m.vy * m.vy);
  338 |       const smoothSpeed = prevSpeed * 0.85 + speed * 0.15;
  339 |       prevSpeed = smoothSpeed;
  340 | 
  341 |       ctx.clearRect(0, 0, W, H);
  342 | 
  343 |       // ── 1. Slow-rotating 3D wireframe shapes ──
  344 |       SHAPES.forEach((shape, i) => {
  345 |         shape.angX += shape.rx;
  346 |         shape.angY += shape.ry;
  347 |         drawShape(shape, shapePositions[i], 0.22);
  348 |       });
  349 | 
  350 |       // ── 2. Grid mesh — distorted by cursor ──
  351 |       const W_COLS = COLS + 1, W_ROWS = ROWS + 1;
  352 |       nodes.forEach(n => {
  353 |         if (m.x > 0) {
  354 |           const dx = m.x - n.ox, dy = m.y - n.oy;
  355 |           const dist = Math.sqrt(dx*dx + dy*dy);
  356 |           const influence = Math.exp(-dist * dist / (2 * 160 * 160));
  357 |           // push nodes away from cursor in a wave
  358 |           const wave = Math.sin(dist * 0.025 - t * 0.07) * influence;
  359 |           n.tx = n.ox - dx * 0.08 * influence + m.vx * 0.12 * influence;
  360 |           n.ty = n.oy - dy * 0.08 * influence + m.vy * 0.12 * influence;
  361 |           // gentle idle oscillation
  362 |           n.tx += Math.sin(t * 0.015 + n.phase) * 3;
  363 |           n.ty += Math.cos(t * 0.013 + n.phase * 1.3) * 3;
  364 |         } else {
  365 |           n.tx = n.ox + Math.sin(t * 0.015 + n.phase) * 3;
  366 |           n.ty = n.oy + Math.cos(t * 0.013 + n.phase * 1.3) * 3;
  367 |         }
  368 |         n.x += (n.tx - n.x) * 0.08;
  369 |         n.y += (n.ty - n.y) * 0.08;
  370 |       });
  371 | 
  372 |       // Draw grid lines
  373 |       ctx.lineWidth = 0.4;
  374 |       for (let r = 0; r < W_ROWS; r++) {
  375 |         for (let c = 0; c < W_COLS; c++) {
  376 |           const n = nodes[r * W_COLS + c];
  377 |           // horizontal
  378 |           if (c < COLS) {
  379 |             const nr = nodes[r * W_COLS + c + 1];
  380 |             const mdx = (n.x + nr.x) / 2 - (m.x || W/2);
  381 |             const mdy = (n.y + nr.y) / 2 - (m.y || H/2);
  382 |             const d = Math.sqrt(mdx*mdx + mdy*mdy);
  383 |             const proximity = Math.exp(-d * d / (2 * 200 * 200));
  384 |             const alpha = 0.06 + proximity * 0.18;
  385 |             ctx.beginPath();
  386 |             ctx.moveTo(n.x, n.y); ctx.lineTo(nr.x, nr.y);
  387 |             ctx.strokeStyle = `rgba(26,86,219,${alpha.toFixed(3)})`;
  388 |             ctx.stroke();
  389 |           }
  390 |           // vertical
  391 |           if (r < ROWS) {
  392 |             const nb = nodes[(r + 1) * W_COLS + c];
  393 |             const mdx = (n.x + nb.x) / 2 - (m.x || W/2);
  394 |             const mdy = (n.y + nb.y) / 2 - (m.y || H/2);
  395 |             const d = Math.sqrt(mdx*mdx + mdy*mdy);
  396 |             const proximity = Math.exp(-d * d / (2 * 200 * 200));
  397 |             const alpha = 0.06 + proximity * 0.18;
  398 |             ctx.beginPath();
  399 |             ctx.moveTo(n.x, n.y); ctx.lineTo(nb.x, nb.y);
  400 |             ctx.strokeStyle = `rgba(26,86,219,${alpha.toFixed(3)})`;
  401 |             ctx.stroke();
  402 |           }
  403 |         }
  404 |       }
  405 | 
  406 |       // ── 3. Cursor halo ──
  407 |       if (m.x > 0) {
  408 |         const haloR = 100 + smoothSpeed * 3;
  409 |         const haloGrd = ctx.createRadialGradient(m.x, m.y, 0, m.x, m.y, haloR);
  410 |         haloGrd.addColorStop(0, "rgba(59,130,246,0.18)");
  411 |         haloGrd.addColorStop(0.4, "rgba(26,86,219,0.08)");
  412 |         haloGrd.addColorStop(1, "rgba(17,68,160,0)");
  413 |         ctx.beginPath();
  414 |         ctx.arc(m.x, m.y, haloR, 0, Math.PI * 2);
  415 |         ctx.fillStyle = haloGrd;
  416 |         ctx.fill();
  417 | 
  418 |         // inner sharp dot
  419 |         ctx.beginPath();
  420 |         ctx.arc(m.x, m.y, 3, 0, Math.PI * 2);
  421 |         ctx.fillStyle = "rgba(59,130,246,0.6)";
  422 |         ctx.fill();
  423 | 
  424 |         // ── 4. Ripple rings from fast movement ──
  425 |         if (smoothSpeed > 6) {
  426 |           ripples.push({ x: m.x, y: m.y, r: 0, maxR: 60 + smoothSpeed * 2, life: 1 });
  427 |         }
  428 |       }
  429 | 
  430 |       // Draw & age ripples
  431 |       for (let i = ripples.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
  432 |         const rp = ripples[i];
  433 |         rp.r += (rp.maxR - rp.r) * 0.06;
  434 |         rp.life -= 0.035;
  435 |         if (rp.life <= 0) { ripples.splice(i, 1); continue; }
  436 |         ctx.beginPath();
  437 |         ctx.arc(rp.x, rp.y, rp.r, 0, Math.PI * 2);
  438 |         ctx.strokeStyle = `rgba(59,130,246,${(rp.life * 0.35).toFixed(3)})`;
  439 |         ctx.lineWidth = 1.2;
  440 |         ctx.stroke();
  441 |       }
  442 | 
  443 |       // ── 5. Velocity streaks ──
  444 |       const spd = Math.sqrt(m.vx * m.vx + m.vy * m.vy);
  445 |       if (spd > 3 && m.x > 0) {
  446 |         streaks.push({
  447 |           x: m.x, y: m.y,
  448 |           dx: -m.vx, dy: -m.vy,
  449 |           len: spd * 3.5,
  450 |           life: 1,
  451 |           width: Math.min(spd * 0.15, 2),
  452 |         });
  453 |       }
  454 |       for (let i = streaks.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
  455 |         const s = streaks[i];
  456 |         s.life -= 0.07;
  457 |         if (s.life <= 0) { streaks.splice(i, 1); continue; }
  458 |         ctx.beginPath();
  459 |         ctx.moveTo(s.x, s.y);
  460 |         ctx.lineTo(s.x + s.dx * (s.len / spd + 1) * s.life, s.y + s.dy * (s.len / spd + 1) * s.life);
  461 |         ctx.strokeStyle = `rgba(147,197,253,${(s.life * 0.5).toFixed(3)})`;
  462 |         ctx.lineWidth = s.width * s.life;
  463 |         ctx.lineCap = "round";
  464 |         ctx.stroke();
  465 |       }
  466 | 
  467 |       t++;
  468 |       rafRef.current = requestAnimationFrame(draw);
  469 |     }
  470 | 
  471 |     draw();
  472 |     return () => {
  473 |       cancelAnimationFrame(rafRef.current);
  474 |       window.removeEventListener("resize", resize);
  475 |       window.removeEventListener("mousemove", onMove);
  476 |     };
  477 |   }, []);
  478 | 
  479 |   return (
  480 |     <canvas
  481 |       ref={canvasRef}
  482 |       style={{ position:"fixed", inset:0, width:"100%", height:"100%", pointerEvents:"none", zIndex:0 }}
  483 |     />
  484 |   );
  485 | }
  486 | 
  487 | // ─── STYLE HELPERS ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  488 | const fld = err => ({
  489 |   width:"100%", padding:"12px 14px", fontSize:13, fontFamily:C.sans,
  490 |   background: err ? C.errBg : "rgba(255,255,255,0.88)",
  491 |   border:`1.5px solid ${err ? C.errBorder : C.border}`,
  492 |   borderRadius:7, outline:"none", color:C.textPrimary,
  493 |   transition:"border-color 0.15s, box-shadow 0.15s, background 0.15s",
  494 |   boxSizing:"border-box", letterSpacing:"0.01em", lineHeight:1.6,
  495 |   backdropFilter:"blur(8px)",
  496 | });
  497 | const onFocus = e => {
  498 |   e.target.style.borderColor = C.blue500;
  499 |   e.target.style.boxShadow   = `0 0 0 4px rgba(26,86,219,0.12)`;
  500 |   e.target.style.background  = "#fff";
  501 | };
  502 | const onBlur = err => e => {
  503 |   e.target.style.borderColor = err ? C.errBorder : C.border;
  504 |   e.target.style.boxShadow   = "none";
  505 | };
  506 | 
  507 | // ─── ATOMS ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  508 | const Flag = ({ code }) => (
  509 |   <img src={`https://flagcdn.com/20x15/${code}.png`} srcSet={`https://flagcdn.com/40x30/${code}.png 2x`}
  510 |     width="20" height="15" alt={code}
  511 |     style={{ borderRadius:2, flexShrink:0 }}
  512 |     onError={e => { e.target.style.display="none"; }} />
  513 | );
  514 | 
  515 | const FieldErr = ({ msg }) => msg
  516 |   ? <p style={{ fontSize:11, color:C.errText, marginTop:5, letterSpacing:"0.01em" }}>{msg}</p>
  517 |   : null;
  518 | 
  519 | const FL = ({ children, optional }) => (
  520 |   <label style={{ display:"block", fontSize:10, fontWeight:600, letterSpacing:"0.14em",
  521 |     textTransform:"uppercase", color:C.blue600, marginBottom:7 }}>
  522 |     {children}
  523 |     {optional && <span style={{ fontWeight:400, textTransform:"none", color:C.textMuted, marginLeft:4 }}>(optional)</span>}
  524 |   </label>
  525 | );
  526 | 
  527 | const Chip = ({ label, active, onClick }) => (
  528 |   <button type="button" onClick={onClick} style={{
  529 |     padding:"8px 16px", borderRadius:6, fontSize:12,
  530 |     fontWeight: active ? 600 : 500, cursor:"pointer", fontFamily:C.sans,
  531 |     letterSpacing:"0.01em", transition:"all 0.18s",
  532 |     border:`1.5px solid ${active ? C.blue500 : C.border}`,
  533 |     background: active ? C.blue500 : "rgba(255,255,255,0.8)",
  534 |     color: active ? C.white : C.textSecondary,
  535 |     boxShadow: active ? "0 3px 10px rgba(26,86,219,0.3)" : "0 1px 3px rgba(0,0,0,0.05)",
  536 |   }}>
  537 |     {label}
  538 |   </button>
  539 | );
  540 | 
  541 | // glass card
  542 | const glassCard = {
  543 |   background:"rgba(255,255,255,0.88)",
  544 |   backdropFilter:"blur(28px) saturate(1.8)",
  545 |   WebkitBackdropFilter:"blur(28px) saturate(1.8)",
  546 |   border:`1.5px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.95)`,
  547 |   borderRadius:13,
  548 |   boxShadow:"0 8px 32px rgba(17,68,160,0.1), 0 1px 6px rgba(17,68,160,0.08)",
  549 | };
  550 | 
  551 | // ─── SIDEBAR ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  552 | function Sidebar() {
  553 |   return (
  554 |     <aside className="hidden lg:flex" style={{
  555 |       width:300, flexShrink:0,
  556 |       borderRight:`1.5px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.4)`,
  557 |       padding:"52px 36px",
  558 |       display:"flex", flexDirection:"column", gap:44,
  559 |       background:"rgba(10,22,40,0.88)",
  560 |       backdropFilter:"blur(28px)",
  561 |       position:"relative", zIndex:1,
  562 |     }}>
  563 |       {/* Top accent line */}
  564 |       <div style={{ position:"absolute", top:0, left:36, right:36, height:3, background:C.blue500, borderRadius:"0 0 3px 3px" }} />

  617 |                 <polyline points="2,6 5,9 10,3" stroke={C.blue300} strokeWidth="2" strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round"/>
  618 |               </svg>
  619 |             </div>
  620 |             <span style={{ fontSize:12, color:"rgba(255,255,255,0.65)" }}>{f}</span>
  621 |           </div>
  622 |         ))}
  623 |       </div>
  624 | 
  625 |       <p style={{ marginTop:"auto", fontSize:11, color:"rgba(255,255,255,0.3)", lineHeight:1.7 }}>
  626 |         End-to-end encrypted.<br/>Never shared with third parties.
  627 |       </p>
  628 |     </aside>
  629 |   );
  630 | }
  631 | 
  632 | // ─── MAIN ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  633 | export default function OnboardingForm({ onComplete, user }) {
  634 |   const [step, setStep]         = useState(1);
  635 |   const [ctry, setCtry]         = useState(COUNTRIES[0]);
  636 |   const [showDrop, setShowDrop] = useState(false);
  637 |   const [ctryQ, setCtryQ]       = useState("");
  638 |   const [vis, setVis]           = useState(true);
  639 | 
  640 |   const [form, setForm] = useState({
  641 |     name: user?.user_metadata?.full_name || "",
  642 |     email:"", phone:"", organization:"", role:"", teamSize:"",
  643 |     productName:"", businessType:"", sector:"", geography:"",
  644 |     problem:"", stage:"", consent:false,
  645 |   });
  646 |   const [errors, setErrors] = useState({});
  647 | 
  648 |   useEffect(() => {
  649 |     setVis(false);
  650 |     const timer = setTimeout(() => setVis(true), 70);
  651 |     return () => clearTimeout(timer);
  652 |   }, [step]);
  653 | 
  654 |   const set     = (k, v) => setForm(f => ({ ...f, [k]:v }));
  655 |   const clr     = k      => setErrors(e => { const n={...e}; delete n[k]; return n; });
  656 |   const phoneOk = ()     => isPhoneValidFor(form.phone, ctry);
  657 | 
  658 |   const handlePhone = e => {
  659 |     set("phone", e.target.value.replace(/\D/g,"").slice(0, ctry.length));
  660 |     clr("phone");
  661 |   };
  662 |   const pickCtry = c => { setCtry(c); set("phone",""); clr("phone"); setShowDrop(false); setCtryQ(""); };
  663 | 
  664 |   function validate(fields) {
  665 |     const errs = {};
  666 |     fields.forEach(f => {
  667 |       if (f==="consent") { if (!form[f]) errs[f]="Please accept to continue."; return; }
  668 |       if (!form[f] || form[f].trim?.()==="") errs[f]=`${FIELD_LABELS[f]||f} is required.`;
  669 |     });
  670 |     if (form.email && !isEmailValid(form.email))    errs.email = "Enter a valid email address.";
  671 |     if (form.phone && !phoneOk()) errs.phone = `Invalid for ${ctry.name}. ${ctry.hint}.`;
  672 |     if (fields.includes("problem") && form.problem.trim().length < 20) {
  673 |   errs.problem = `At least 20 characters required (${form.problem.trim().length}/20).`;
  674 | }
  675 |     return errs;
  676 |   }
  677 | 
  678 |   const step1ok = () =>
  679 |     STEP1.every(f => form[f] && form[f].trim?.()!=="") && isEmailValid(form.email) && phoneOk();
  680 |   const step2ok = () =>
  681 |   STEP2.every(f => form[f] && form[f].trim?.()!=="")
  682 |   && form.problem.trim().length >= 20
  683 |   && form.consent===true;
  684 | 
  685 |   function advance() {
  686 |     if (step===1) {
  687 |       const e = validate(STEP1);
  688 |       if (Object.keys(e).length) { setErrors(e); return; }
  689 |       setErrors({}); setStep(2);
  690 |     } else {
  691 |       const e = validate([...STEP2,"consent"]);
  692 |       if (Object.keys(e).length) { setErrors(e); return; }
  693 |       setErrors({});
  694 |       onComplete?.({ ...form, phoneFull:`${ctry.code}${form.phone}`, countryCode:ctry.code });
  695 |     }
  696 |   }
  697 | 
  698 |   const canGo    = step===1 ? step1ok() : step2ok();
  699 |   const filtered = COUNTRIES.filter(c =>
  700 |     c.name.toLowerCase().includes(ctryQ.toLowerCase()) || c.code.includes(ctryQ)
  701 |   );
  702 | 
  703 |   const inp = (key, extra={}) => ({
  704 |     style:{ ...fld(errors[key]), ...extra },
  705 |     value: form[key],
  706 |     onChange: e => { set(key, e.target.value); clr(key); },
  707 |     onFocus,
  708 |     onBlur: onBlur(errors[key]),
  709 |   });
  710 | 
  711 |   return (
  712 |     <div
  713 |       style={{ minHeight:"100vh", background:C.surface, fontFamily:C.sans,
  714 |         display:"flex", flexDirection:"column", position:"relative" }}
  715 |       onClick={() => showDrop && setShowDrop(false)}
  716 |     >
  717 |       <AnimatedBackground />
  718 | 
  719 |       {/* ── Header ── */}
  720 |       <header style={{ height:56, borderBottom:`1.5px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.3)`,
  721 |         padding:"0 28px", display:"flex", alignItems:"center", justifyContent:"space-between",
  722 |         position:"sticky", top:0, zIndex:50,
  723 |         background:"rgba(10,22,40,0.92)",
  724 |         backdropFilter:"blur(24px)" }}>
  725 |         <div style={{ display:"flex", alignItems:"center", gap:14 }}>
  726 |           <img src="/infopace-logo.jpg" alt="Infopace" style={{ width:32, height:32, borderRadius:7,
  727 |             objectFit:"contain", background:"#fff", padding:2,
  728 |             boxShadow:"0 2px 8px rgba(26,86,219,0.4)" }} />
  729 |           <div>
  730 |             <div style={{ fontSize:12, fontWeight:700, color:C.white,
  731 |               letterSpacing:"0.12em", textTransform:"uppercase" }}>Infopace Management Pvt Ltd</div>
  732 |             <div style={{ fontSize:10, color:C.blue300, letterSpacing:"0.11em",
  733 |               textTransform:"uppercase", marginTop:1 }}>Market Potential Assessment</div>
  734 |           </div>
  735 |         </div>
  736 |         <div style={{ display:"flex", alignItems:"center", gap:8 }}>
  737 |           <div style={{ width:7, height:7, borderRadius:"50%", background:"#34d399",
  738 |             boxShadow:"0 0 0 3px rgba(52,211,153,0.2)" }} />
  739 |           <span style={{ fontSize:10, color:C.blue200, letterSpacing:"0.12em", textTransform:"uppercase" }}>
  740 |             Live analysis
  741 |           </span>
  742 |         </div>
  743 |       </header>
  744 | 
  745 |       <main style={{ flex:1, display:"flex", position:"relative", zIndex:1 }}>
  746 |         <Sidebar />
  747 | 
  748 |         {/* ── Form panel ── */}
  749 |         <div style={{ flex:1, overflowY:"auto", padding:"52px 32px" }}>
  750 |           <div style={{ maxWidth:580, margin:"0 auto" }}>
  751 | 
  752 |             {/* Step indicator */}
  753 |             <div style={{ display:"flex", alignItems:"center", marginBottom:32 }}>
  754 |               {["Personal details","Venture context"].map((label, i) => {
  755 |                 const active = step===i+1, done = step>i+1;
  756 |                 return (
  757 |                   <div key={i} style={{ display:"flex", alignItems:"center" }}>
  758 |                     <button onClick={() => done && setStep(i+1)}
  759 |                       style={{ display:"flex", alignItems:"center", gap:9,
  760 |                         background:"none", border:"none",
  761 |                         cursor:done?"pointer":"default", padding:"6px 0" }}>
  762 |                       <div style={{ width:24, height:24, borderRadius:"50%",
  763 |                         border:`2px solid ${active ? C.blue500 : done ? "#34d399" : C.border}`,
  764 |                         background: active ? C.blue500 : done ? "#34d399" : "rgba(255,255,255,0.6)",
  765 |                         display:"flex", alignItems:"center", justifyContent:"center",
  766 |                         transition:"all 0.22s", flexShrink:0,
  767 |                         boxShadow: active ? "0 0 0 4px rgba(26,86,219,0.15)" : "none" }}>
  768 |                         {done
  769 |                           ? <svg width="10" height="10" viewBox="0 0 12 12" fill="none">
  770 |                               <polyline points="2,6 5,9 10,3" stroke="white" strokeWidth="2.2" strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round"/>
  771 |                             </svg>
  772 |                           : <span style={{ fontSize:10, fontWeight:700,
  773 |                               color:active?"white":C.textMuted, fontFamily:C.mono }}>{i+1}</span>
  774 |                         }
  775 |                       </div>
  776 |                       <span style={{ fontSize:12, fontWeight: active ? 600 : 400,
  777 |                         color:active?C.blue600:done?"#059669":C.textMuted }}>{label}</span>
  778 |                     </button>
  779 |                     {i===0 && (
  780 |                       <div style={{ width:28, height:2, background:step>1?"#34d399":C.border,
  781 |                         margin:"0 10px", borderRadius:2, transition:"background 0.35s" }} />
  782 |                     )}
  783 |                   </div>
  784 |                 );
  785 |               })}
  786 |               <span style={{ marginLeft:"auto", fontSize:10, color:C.textMuted,
  787 |                 fontFamily:C.mono, letterSpacing:"0.06em" }}>{step} / 2</span>
  788 |             </div>
  789 | 
  790 |             {/* Progress bar */}
  791 |             <div style={{ height:2, background:"rgba(17,68,160,0.1)", marginBottom:40,
  792 |               overflow:"hidden", borderRadius:2 }}>
  793 |               <div style={{ height:"100%", width:step===1?"50%":"100%",
  794 |                 background:C.blue500, borderRadius:2,
  795 |                 transition:"width 0.5s cubic-bezier(0.4,0,0.2,1)",
  796 |                 boxShadow:"0 0 12px rgba(26,86,219,0.4)" }} />
  797 |             </div>
  798 | 
  799 |             {/* Form card */}
  800 |             <div style={{ ...glassCard, padding:"42px 42px 34px",
  801 |               opacity:vis?1:0, transform:vis?"none":"translateY(10px)",
  802 |               transition:"opacity 0.28s ease, transform 0.28s ease" }}>
  803 | 
  804 |               {/* ── STEP 1 ── */}
  805 |               {step===1 && (
  806 |                 <>
  807 |                   <div style={{ marginBottom:30 }}>
  808 |                     <h1 style={{ fontFamily:C.serif, fontSize:27, fontWeight:700,
  809 |                       color:C.blue900, margin:0, letterSpacing:"-0.02em", lineHeight:1.2 }}>
  810 |                       Personal details
  811 |                     </h1>
  812 |                     <p style={{ fontSize:12, color:C.textMuted, marginTop:9, letterSpacing:"0.01em" }}>
  813 |                       Stored securely. Never shared.
  814 |                     </p>
  815 |                   </div>
  816 | 
  817 |                   <div style={{ display:"grid", gridTemplateColumns:"1fr 1fr", gap:"22px 20px" }}>
  818 | 
  819 |                     <div>
  820 |                       <FL>Full name *</FL>
  821 |                       <input placeholder="Jane Doe" {...inp("name")} />
  822 |                       <FieldErr msg={errors.name} />
  823 |                     </div>
  824 | 
  825 |                     <div>
  826 |                       <FL>Email *</FL>
  827 |                       <input type="email" placeholder="jane@company.com"
  828 |                         style={fld(errors.email)} value={form.email}
  829 |                         onChange={e => { set("email",e.target.value); clr("email"); }}
  830 |                         onFocus={onFocus}
  831 |                         onBlur={e => {
  832 |                           onBlur(errors.email)(e);
  833 |                           if (form.email && !isEmailValid(form.email))
  834 |                             setErrors(p => ({ ...p, email:"Enter a valid email address." }));
  835 |                         }} />
  836 |                       <FieldErr msg={errors.email} />
  837 |                     </div>
  838 | 
  839 |                     <div>
  840 |                       <FL>Organization *</FL>
  841 |                       <input placeholder="Acme Technologies" {...inp("organization")} />
  842 |                       <FieldErr msg={errors.organization} />
  843 |                     </div>
  844 | 
  845 |                     <div>
  846 |                       <FL>Role *</FL>
  847 |                       <select style={{ ...fld(errors.role), appearance:"none", cursor:"pointer" }}
  848 |                         value={form.role} onChange={e => { set("role",e.target.value); clr("role"); }}
  849 |                         onFocus={onFocus} onBlur={onBlur(errors.role)}>
  850 |                         <option value="">Select…</option>
  851 |                         {ROLES.map(r => <option key={r}>{r}</option>)}
  852 |                       </select>
  853 |                       <FieldErr msg={errors.role} />
  854 |                     </div>
  855 | 
  856 |                     {/* Phone */}
  857 |                     <div style={{ gridColumn:"span 2" }} onClick={e => e.stopPropagation()}>
  858 |                       <FL>Phone *</FL>
  859 |                       <div style={{ display:"flex",
  860 |                         border:`1.5px solid ${errors.phone ? C.errBorder : C.border}`,
  861 |                         borderRadius:6, background:errors.phone?"rgba(255,241,242,0.85)":"rgba(255,255,255,0.85)",
  862 |                         transition:"border-color 0.15s", backdropFilter:"blur(8px)" }}>
  863 |                         <div style={{ position:"relative", flexShrink:0 }}>
  864 |                           <button type="button" onClick={() => { setShowDrop(v => !v); setCtryQ(""); }}
  865 |                             style={{ display:"flex", alignItems:"center", gap:6, padding:"10px 13px",
  866 |                               background:"transparent", border:"none",
  867 |                               borderRight:`1.5px solid ${C.border}`, cursor:"pointer", height:"100%" }}>
  868 |                             <Flag code={ctry.flag} />
  869 |                             <span style={{ fontSize:11, fontWeight:600, color:C.blue700,
  870 |                               fontFamily:C.mono }}>{ctry.code}</span>
  871 |                             <span style={{ fontSize:8, color:C.textMuted }}>▾</span>
  872 |                           </button>
  873 |                           {showDrop && (
  874 |                             <div style={{ position:"absolute", top:"calc(100% + 4px)", left:0, zIndex:100,
  875 |                               background:"rgba(255,255,255,0.97)", backdropFilter:"blur(20px)",
  876 |                               border:`1.5px solid ${C.border}`, borderRadius:9,
  877 |                               boxShadow:"0 12px 40px rgba(10,22,40,0.12)", width:264, overflow:"hidden" }}>
  878 |                               <div style={{ padding:9, borderBottom:`1px solid ${C.border}` }}>
  879 |                                 <input autoFocus placeholder="Search country…" value={ctryQ}
  880 |                                   onChange={e => setCtryQ(e.target.value)}
  881 |                                   onClick={e => e.stopPropagation()}
  882 |                                   style={{ width:"100%", padding:"7px 10px", fontSize:12,
  883 |                                     border:`1.5px solid ${C.border}`, borderRadius:5, outline:"none",
  884 |                                     background:"rgba(240,244,255,0.7)", boxSizing:"border-box",
  885 |                                     fontFamily:C.sans, color:C.textPrimary }} />
  886 |                               </div>
  887 |                               <div style={{ maxHeight:220, overflowY:"auto" }}>
  888 |                                 {filtered.length===0
  889 |                                   ? <div style={{ fontSize:12, color:C.textMuted, padding:14, textAlign:"center" }}>No results</div>
  890 |                                   : filtered.map((c, i) => (
  891 |                                     <button key={i} type="button" onClick={() => pickCtry(c)}
  892 |                                       style={{ width:"100%", display:"flex", alignItems:"center", gap:9,
  893 |                                         padding:"9px 13px", border:"none", cursor:"pointer", textAlign:"left",
  894 |                                         fontSize:12, background:ctry.name===c.name?C.blue50:"transparent",
  895 |                                         color:C.textPrimary, fontFamily:C.sans }}>
  896 |                                       <Flag code={c.flag} />
  897 |                                       <span style={{ flex:1 }}>{c.name}</span>
  898 |                                       <span style={{ color:C.textMuted, fontFamily:C.mono, fontSize:10 }}>{c.code}</span>
  899 |                                     </button>
  900 |                                   ))
  901 |                                 }
  902 |                               </div>
  903 |                             </div>
  904 |                           )}
  905 |                         </div>
  906 |                         <input type="tel" inputMode="numeric" placeholder={ctry.placeholder} value={form.phone}
  907 |                           onChange={handlePhone}
  908 |                           onBlur={() => { if (form.phone && !phoneOk())
  909 |                             setErrors(p => ({ ...p, phone:`Invalid for ${ctry.name}. ${ctry.hint}.` })); }}
  910 |                           style={{ flex:1, border:"none", background:"transparent", outline:"none",
  911 |                             padding:"10px 13px", fontSize:13, color:C.textPrimary, fontFamily:C.sans }} />
  912 |                         <span style={{ padding:"10px 13px", fontSize:10, color:C.textMuted,
  913 |                           fontFamily:C.mono, alignSelf:"center", whiteSpace:"nowrap" }}>
  914 |                           {form.phone.length}/{ctry.length}
  915 |                         </span>
  916 |                       </div>
  917 |                       {errors.phone
  918 |                         ? <p style={{ fontSize:11, color:C.errText, marginTop:5 }}>{errors.phone}</p>
  919 |                         : <p style={{ fontSize:11, color:C.textMuted, marginTop:5 }}>{ctry.name}: {ctry.hint}</p>
  920 |                       }
  921 |                     </div>
  922 | 
  923 |                     <div style={{ gridColumn:"span 2" }}>
  924 |                       <FL optional>Team size</FL>
  925 |                       <div style={{ display:"flex", gap:8, flexWrap:"wrap" }}>
  926 |                         {TEAM_SIZES.map(s => (
  927 |                           <Chip key={s} label={s} active={form.teamSize===s}
  928 |                             onClick={() => set("teamSize",s)} />
  929 |                         ))}
  930 |                       </div>
  931 |                     </div>
  932 |                   </div>
  933 |                 </>
  934 |               )}
  935 | 
  936 |               {/* ── STEP 2 ── */}

  938 |                 <>

  941 |                       color:C.blue900, margin:0, letterSpacing:"-0.02em", lineHeight:1.2 }}>
  942 |                       Your venture
  943 |                     </h1>

📄 FILE #25: supabase_setup.sql
----------------------------------------------------------------------
    1 | -- ================================================================
    2 | --  Infopace — Supabase Database Setup (No Auth version)
    3 | --  Run this entire file in: Supabase → SQL Editor → Run
    4 | -- ================================================================
    5 | 
    6 | -- 1. Drop old table if re-running (comment out if you want to keep data)
    7 | -- drop table if exists public.submissions;
    8 | 
    9 | -- 2. Create submissions table
   10 | --    Stores BOTH the onboarding form data AND the final assessment result
   11 | create table if not exists public.submissions (
   12 |   id              uuid        default gen_random_uuid() primary key,
   13 | 
   14 |   -- ── Onboarding: Step 1 (Personal Info) ──────────────────────
   15 |   name            text        not null,
   16 |   email           text        not null,
   17 |   phone           text,
   18 |   phone_full      text,           -- e.g. +919876543210
   19 |   country_code    text,           -- e.g. +91
   20 |   organization    text,
   21 |   role            text,
   22 |   website         text,
   23 |   linkedin        text,
   24 |   team_size       text,
   25 | 
   26 |   -- ── Onboarding: Step 2 (Venture Context) ────────────────────
   27 |   product_name    text,
   28 |   business_type   text,
   29 |   sector          text,
   30 |   geography       text,
   31 |   problem         text,
   32 |   stage           text,
   33 | 
   34 |   -- ── Assessment answers (JSON from dashboard) ────────────────
   35 |   answers         jsonb,
   36 | 
   37 |   -- ── Final result from AI analysis ───────────────────────────
   38 |   overall_score   integer,
   39 |   grade           text,
   40 |   verdict         text,
   41 |   tam_crore       numeric,
   42 |   sam_crore       numeric,
   43 |   som_crore       numeric,
   44 |   growth_rate     numeric,
   45 |   dimensions      jsonb,      -- {d1,d2,d3,d4,d5,d6} scores
   46 |   key_insights    jsonb,      -- array of insight strings
   47 |   top_risks       jsonb,      -- array of risk strings
   48 |   quick_wins      jsonb,      -- array of quick win strings
   49 |   analysis_json   jsonb,      -- full raw analysis object
   50 | 
   51 |   -- ── Screenshot URL (stored in Supabase Storage) ─────────────
   52 |   screenshot_url  text,       -- public URL of captured dashboard image
   53 | 
   54 |   -- ── Status tracking ─────────────────────────────────────────
   55 |   status          text        default 'onboarding_complete',
   56 |   -- 'onboarding_complete' = form filled, assessment not yet done
   57 |   -- 'assessment_complete' = dashboard generated with result
   58 | 
   59 |   created_at      timestamptz default now(),
   60 |   updated_at      timestamptz default now()
   61 | );
   62 | 
   63 | -- 3. Enable Row Level Security
   64 | alter table public.submissions enable row level security;
   65 | 
   66 | -- 4. Allow public inserts (no auth required)
   67 | create policy "Allow public inserts"
   68 |   on public.submissions
   69 |   for insert
   70 |   with check (true);
   71 | 
   72 | -- 5. Allow public reads
   73 | create policy "Allow public reads"
   74 |   on public.submissions
   75 |   for select
   76 |   using (true);
   77 | 
   78 | -- 6. Allow public updates (needed to update result after assessment)
   79 | create policy "Allow public updates"
   80 |   on public.submissions
   81 |   for update
   82 |   using (true)
   83 |   with check (true);
   84 | 
   85 | -- 7. Useful indexes
   86 | create index if not exists submissions_email_idx
   87 |   on public.submissions (email);
   88 | 
   89 | create index if not exists submissions_created_at_idx
   90 |   on public.submissions (created_at desc);
   91 | 
   92 | create index if not exists submissions_status_idx
   93 |   on public.submissions (status);
   94 | 
   95 | -- 8. Auto-update updated_at on row change
   96 | create or replace function public.handle_updated_at()
   97 | returns trigger as $$
   98 | begin
   99 |   new.updated_at = now();
  100 |   return new;
  101 | end;
  102 | $$ language plpgsql;
  103 | 
  104 | drop trigger if exists set_updated_at on public.submissions;
  105 | create trigger set_updated_at
  106 |   before update on public.submissions
  107 |   for each row execute function public.handle_updated_at();
  108 | 
  109 | -- ================================================================
  110 | --  DONE. You should see the `submissions` table in Table Editor.
  111 | -- ================================================================
